### [1] [Heterotic Ouroboros](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22915)
*Chiara Altavista,Salvatore Raucci,Angel M. Uranga,Chuying Wang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper revisits the construction of ten-dimensional non-supersymmetric heterotic string theories from M-theory on a specific one-dimensional space, using the gauge enhancement mechanism of type I' string theory. The authors provide a consistent set of rules to derive the light spectra and gauge groups, including their global structure, and suggest evidence for junctions among these theories.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore and provide a consistent framework for constructing ten-dimensional non-supersymmetric heterotic string theories from M-theory compactified on a particular one-dimensional space. This is achieved by employing the gauge enhancement mechanism of type I' string theory, which allows for the reproduction of known heterotic theories and provides new insights into their interconnections.

Method: The method involves the use of M-theory compactified on a one-dimensional space, specifically ${\mathbf{S}}^1\vee{\mathbf{S}}^1$, and applying the gauge enhancement mechanism of type I' string theory. The type I' interval is curled onto itself, with its two boundaries separated by a branch cut, allowing for the derivation of the light spectra and gauge groups of the heterotic theories, as well as providing evidence for junctions among them.

Result: The result is a consistent set of rules that reproduces the light spectra and gauge groups of the ten-dimensional heterotic string theories, including indications of their global structure. Additionally, the authors present some evidence for the existence of junctions among these heterotic theories, suggesting a deeper interconnectedness within this class of string theories.

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the proposed construction successfully reproduces the known features of ten-dimensional non-supersymmetric heterotic string theories, and it provides a new perspective on their interrelations through the concept of junctions. This work offers a more unified and coherent approach to understanding these theories within the context of M-theory.

Abstract: M-theory on ${\mathbf{S}}^1\vee{\mathbf{S}}^1$ has recently been proposed to yield, via quotients, ten-dimensional non-supersymmetric string theories. We revisit the construction that leads to the heterotic theories, finding a consistent set of rules that reproduces the light spectra and gauge groups, including indications of their global structure. Our approach uses the gauge enhancement mechanism of type I' string theory, applied to a setting in which the type I' interval is curled onto itself, with its two boundaries separated by a branch cut. Using these tools, we reproduce the ten-dimensional heterotic theories and provide some evidence for junctions among them.

</details>


### [2] [String theory in the infrared](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22916)
*Ivano Basile*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper discusses a research program that explores the landscape of low-energy phases of string theory, revealing universal scaling relations and UV/IR relations that lead to holographic bounds, supporting swampland-motivated phenomenological scenarios and the potential for extracting empirical signatures of string theory from cosmological observations.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the non-generic nature of effective theories of gravity produced by low-energy string theory and to explore the connections between infrared data through universal scaling relations. The aim is to provide theoretical support for swampland-motivated phenomenological scenarios and to find empirically accessible signatures of string theory in cosmological observations.

动机是理解低能弦理论产生的引力有效理论的非通用性质，并通过普遍的缩放关系探索红外数据之间的联系。目的是为沼泽地启发的现象学场景提供理论支持，并在宇宙观测中寻找经验上可访问的弦理论特征。

Method: The method involves a global perspective on the landscape of low-energy phases of string theory, incorporating lessons from the swampland program. A worldsheet analysis is used to reveal UV/IR relations and parametric inequalities, which are expressed as holographic bounds. These relations and bounds are not visible from the viewpoint of effective field theory alone.

方法涉及从全局视角审视低能相位的弦理论景观，结合了来自沼泽地项目的教训。使用世界面分析揭示UV/IR关系和参数不等式，这些被表达为全息边界。这些关系和边界仅从有效场论的角度来看是不可见的。

Result: The results show that the effective theories of gravity produced by low-energy string theory have non-trivial universal scaling relations and UV/IR relations, leading to holographic bounds. These findings provide a more solid theoretical foundation for swampland-motivated phenomenological scenarios and suggest the possibility of extracting less direct but empirically accessible signatures of string theory from cosmological observations.

结果表明，低能弦理论产生的引力有效理论具有非平凡的普遍缩放关系和UV/IR关系，导致全息边界。这些发现为沼泽地启发的现象学场景提供了更坚实的理论基础，并暗示了从宇宙观测中提取较少直接但经验上可访问的弦理论特征的可能性。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the effective theories of gravity from low-energy string theory are far from generic and exhibit universal scaling relations and UV/IR relations, which manifest as holographic bounds. This supports the broader hopes of finding indirect but observable signatures of string theory in cosmological data, reinforcing the importance of the swampland program in guiding our understanding of quantum gravity.

结论是，来自低能弦理论的引力有效理论远非通用，并表现出普遍的缩放关系和UV/IR关系，这些表现为全息边界。这支持了在宇宙数据中找到间接但可观测的弦理论特征的更广泛希望，加强了沼泽地项目在指导我们对量子引力的理解中的重要性。

Abstract: I briefly summarize a recent research program aiming to probe the landscape of low-energy phases of string theory from a global perspective. Borrowing conceptual lessons from the swampland program, I will discuss how the effective theories of gravity produced by low-energy string theory are far from generic; rather, their infrared data is connected by universal scaling relations which become non-trivial in species limits. In particular, a worldsheet analysis reveals that higher-derivative Wilson coefficients and the vacuum energy exhibit UV/IR relations which are invisible from the viewpoint of effective field theory, leading to parametric inequalities which take the form of holographic bounds. This lends a more solid theoretical support to swampland-motivated phenomenological scenarios, and to the broader hopes of extracting less direct, but empirically accessible, signatures of string theory from cosmological observations.

</details>


### [3] [Kinematic Flow for Banana Loops and Unparticles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22918)
*Tom Westerdijk,Chen Yang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper extends the concept of kinematic flow to momentum-integrated loop-level cosmological correlators, focusing on specific types of scalar fields in power-law and de Sitter cosmologies. It introduces a new basis for master integrals and a set of combinatorial rules that describe the mixing of these integrals, providing a systematic framework for unparticle exchange in complex configurations.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to develop a systematic approach to handle momentum-integrated loop-level cosmological correlators, particularly for banana loops and unparticle exchanges, which are important in understanding the dynamics of conformally coupled scalars in different cosmological backgrounds. The aim is to find a finite set of master integrals and a corresponding basis that can be used to describe these correlators, thereby simplifying their computation and analysis.

动机是开发一种系统的方法来处理动量积分的环级宇宙关联函数，特别是香蕉环和无粒子交换，这对于理解不同宇宙背景下的共形耦合标量的动力学非常重要。目标是找到一组有限的主积分及其相应的基底，从而简化这些关联函数的计算和分析。

Method: The method involves extending the concept of kinematic flow to momentum-integrated loop-level cosmological correlators. The authors focus on banana loops of conformally coupled scalars in power-law cosmologies and arbitrary mixtures of massless and conformally coupled scalars in de Sitter space. They use the dual description of these correlators as tree-level exchanges of unparticles and construct a basis from tubings of marked graphs. This basis is characterized by nested tubes and an arborescence ordering of the vertices. The authors derive connection matrices using four combinatorial rules: activation, merger, swap, and copy, which are unique to unparticle exchanges.

该方法涉及将运动学流的概念扩展到动量积分的环级宇宙关联函数。作者专注于幂律宇宙中的共形耦合标量的香蕉环以及de Sitter空间中任意混合的无质量标量和共形耦合标量。他们使用这些关联函数作为无粒子树级交换的对偶描述，并从标记图的管状结构构造基底。这个基底的特点是嵌套的管状结构和顶点的树形排序。作者通过四种组合规则（激活、合并、交换和复制）推导出连接矩阵，这些规则是无粒子交换所特有的。

Result: The results show that the correlators associated with banana loops and unparticle exchanges can be described by a finite set of master integrals that obey a first-order system of differential equations. The basis constructed from tubings of marked graphs is distinguished by the appearance of nested tubes and an arborescence ordering of the vertices. The connection matrices derived from the combinatorial rules (activation, merger, swap, and copy) induce richer mixing among the basis functions and introduce new kinematic letters. The framework is shown to extend systematically to more complicated configurations, including necklace diagrams.

结果表明，与香蕉环和无粒子交换相关的关联函数可以由一组有限的主积分描述，这些主积分满足一阶微分方程组。从标记图的管状结构构造的基底以嵌套的管状结构和顶点的树形排序为特征。通过组合规则（激活、合并、交换和复制）推导出的连接矩阵在基底函数之间引入了更丰富的混合，并引入了新的运动学字母。该框架被证明可以系统地扩展到更复杂的构型，包括项链图。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the extension of kinematic flow to momentum-integrated loop-level cosmological correlators provides a powerful and systematic framework for handling unparticle exchanges in various cosmological settings. The use of a finite set of master integrals and the associated basis, along with the combinatorial rules, simplifies the computation and analysis of these correlators, making it possible to study more complex configurations, such as necklace diagrams, in a consistent manner.

结论是，将运动学流扩展到动量积分的环级宇宙关联函数提供了一个强大且系统的框架，用于处理各种宇宙背景下的无粒子交换。使用一组有限的主积分及其相关基底，以及组合规则，简化了这些关联函数的计算和分析，使得能够以一致的方式研究更复杂的构型，如项链图。

Abstract: We extend kinematic flow to momentum-integrated loop-level cosmological correlators, focusing on banana loops of conformally coupled scalars in power-law cosmologies and, in de Sitter, on arbitrary mixtures of massless and conformally coupled scalars. Exploiting their dual description as tree-level exchanges of unparticles, we show that the associated correlators are described by a finite set of master integrals obeying a first-order system of differential equations. The corresponding basis is constructed from tubings of marked graphs and is distinguished by the appearance of nested tubes and an arborescence ordering of the vertices. We derive the connection matrices from four combinatorial rules -- activation, merger, swap, and copy. The last two are unique to unparticle exchanges: they induce richer mixing among basis functions and introduce new kinematic letters. Our framework extends systematically to arbitrarily complicated configurations, including necklace diagrams, and establishes unparticle exchange as a distinct class of kinematic flow.

</details>


### [4] [Particle and Superparticle Confinement in Higher Codimension Braneworlds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22929)
*F. E. A. de Souza,M. O. Tahim,R. I. de Oliveira Júnior,I. M. Macêdo*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper analyzes the classical confinement of relativistic and supersymmetric spinning particles in higher-codimension braneworlds, showing that spin-curvature coupling can lead to stable equilibrium points and confinement, unlike the repulsive behavior observed for spinless particles.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore how spin-curvature coupling affects the confinement of spinning particles in braneworlds, which could provide insights into localization mechanisms in higher-dimensional theories. [English Text]

该动机是探索自旋-曲率耦合如何影响膜世界中自旋粒子的约束，这可以为高维理论中的局域化机制提供见解。

Method: The authors use a Polyakov-type action to derive the effective radial dynamics of particles in warped backgrounds generated by string-like $ n=2$ and global scalar defects $ n \geq 3$. They analyze the resulting effective potential for both spinless and spinning particles. [English Text]

作者使用Polyakov型作用量推导了由弦状$n=2$和全局标量缺陷$n \geq 3$生成的翘曲背景中粒子的有效径向动力学。他们分析了无自旋和有自旋粒子的有效势。

Result: For spinless particles, the effective potential is monotonically decreasing, leading to repulsive behavior and no confinement. For $N=1,2$ spinning particles, the spin-curvature coupling modifies the potential, allowing for stable equilibrium points and possible confinement. [English Text]

对于无自旋粒子，有效势单调递减，导致排斥行为且没有约束。对于$N=1,2$自旋粒子，自旋-曲率耦合改变了势能，允许存在稳定的平衡点和可能的约束。

Conclusion: The results highlight the crucial role of spin in the localization of particles in braneworlds, with spin-curvature coupling enabling confinement in scenarios where spinless particles are repelled. [English Text]

结果突出了自旋在膜世界中粒子局域化中的关键作用，自旋-曲率耦合在无自旋粒子被排斥的情况下实现了约束。

Abstract: In this work we analyze the classical confinement of relativistic and supersymmetric spinning particles in higher-codimension braneworlds. Considering warped backgrounds generated by string-like $ n=2$ and global scalar defects $ n \geq 3$, we derive the effective radial dynamics from a Polyakov-type action. For spinless particles, the effective potential is monotonically decreasing, leading to repulsive behavior and the absence of confinement. In contrast, for $N=1,2 $ spinning particles, spin-curvature coupling modifies the potential, allowing the emergence of stable equilibrium points. Depending on the coupling parameter, particles may be confined on the membrane or in nearby regions, exhibiting bounded or satellite-like motion. These results emphasize the role of spin in localization mechanisms.

</details>


### [5] [Fractions and Fakeons in Quantum Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23215)
*Damiano Anselmi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper explores quantum field theories with fractional or continuous powers of the d'Alembert operator, ensuring perturbative unitarity and a well-defined classical limit. It uses the fakeon prescription for continuation from Euclidean to Minkowski spacetime and discusses alternative formulations through decomposition. The paper also addresses potential calculation pitfalls and extends the treatment to fractional gauge and gravity theories, maintaining Ward and Cutkosky identities.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to formulate quantum field theories (QFTs) that incorporate fractional or continuous powers of the d'Alembert operator, while preserving key physical properties such as perturbative unitarity and a well-defined classical limit. The aim is to explore how these non-integer powers can be consistently included in QFTs, leading to new theoretical frameworks and potentially new physical insights.

动机是构建包含d'Alembert算子的分数或连续幂次的量子场论，同时保持微扰幺正性和明确的经典极限等关键物理性质。目标是探索如何在量子场论中一致地包含这些非整数幂次，从而形成新的理论框架并可能带来新的物理见解。

Method: The method involves formulating QFTs with fractional or continuous powers of the d'Alembert operator. The primary approach is to continue correlation functions from Euclidean space to Minkowski spacetime using the fakeon prescription. Alternative formulations are explored by decomposing the fractional part into a continuum of ordinary fakeons. The paper examines these formulations at tree level and for bubble diagrams, and also discusses potential pitfalls in the calculations. Finally, it extends the treatment to fractional gauge and gravity theories, ensuring that Ward and Cutkosky identities are maintained.

方法涉及构建具有d'Alembert算子的分数或连续幂次的量子场论。主要方法是使用fakeon处方将关联函数从欧几里得空间延拓到闵可夫斯基时空。通过将分数部分分解为普通fakeon的连续统来探讨替代形式。论文在树级和泡图层面上检查了这些形式，并讨论了计算中的潜在陷阱。最后，它将处理扩展到分数规范和引力理论，确保Ward和Cutkosky恒等式得以维持。

Result: The results show that there are multiple inequivalent Minkowskian theories with the same Euclidean counterpart when using the fakeon prescription and decomposition methods. The paper demonstrates these features at tree level and for bubble diagrams, and identifies potential pitfalls in the calculations. It also shows how to treat continuous powers of covariant d'Alembertians in fractional gauge and gravity theories, maintaining Ward and Cutkosky identities.

结果表明，使用fakeon处方和分解方法时，存在多个不等价的闵可夫斯基理论，它们具有相同的欧几里得对应物。论文在树级和泡图层面上展示了这些特征，并确定了计算中的潜在陷阱。它还展示了如何在分数规范和引力理论中处理协变d'Alembert算子的连续幂次，同时保持Ward和Cutkosky恒等式。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that it is possible to formulate QFTs with fractional or continuous powers of the d'Alembert operator while maintaining perturbative unitarity and a well-defined classical limit. The use of the fakeon prescription and decomposition into a continuum of fakeons provides a consistent framework. The study also highlights the importance of careful calculations and the maintenance of Ward and Cutkosky identities in these new formulations.

论文得出结论，可以在保持微扰幺正性和明确的经典极限的同时，构建具有d'Alembert算子的分数或连续幂次的量子场论。使用fakeon处方和分解为fakeon的连续统提供了一致的框架。研究还强调了在这些新形式中仔细计算和保持Ward和Cutkosky恒等式的重要性。

Abstract: We investigate formulations of quantum field theories whose kinetic terms involve fractional or continuous powers of the d'Alembert operator. The primary requirements are perturbative unitarity and a well-defined classical limit with a finite number of initial conditions. A direct approach consists of continuing the correlation functions from Euclidean space to Minkowski spacetime using the fakeon prescription for the fractional part of the power. Alternative formulations arise through decomposition, in which the fractional part is represented as a continuum of ordinary fakeons. These options are infinite in number and yield inequivalent Minkowskian theories with the same Euclidean counterpart. We demonstrate these features at tree level and for bubble diagrams. We also point out potential pitfalls in the calculations. Finally, we show how to treat continuous powers of covariant d'Alembertians in fractional gauge and gravity theories. The Ward and Cutkosky identities hold in all formulations.

</details>


### [6] [Chaos of Berry curvature for BPS microstates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23287)
*Yiming Chen,Sean Colin-Ellerin,Ohad Mamroud,Kyriakos Papadodimas*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper proposes using the non-Abelian Berry curvature of BPS states under certain deformations as an intrinsic probe of chaos to distinguish black hole microstates from smooth horizonless geometries. The authors find that for supersymmetric black holes, the Berry curvature resembles a random matrix, while for states dual to horizonless geometries, it is non-random and often exactly zero. This suggests that the Berry curvature can serve as a robust diagnostic of chaos in supersymmetric sectors.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to find a way to distinguish the chaotic properties of black hole microstates from those associated with other geometries, particularly in the context of supersymmetric black holes where traditional level statistics cannot be used due to exact degeneracy. The authors propose the use of non-Abelian Berry curvature as an intrinsic probe of chaos.

动机是找到一种方法来区分黑洞微观状态与其他几何结构相关的混沌特性，特别是在超对称黑洞的情况下，由于能级完全简并，传统的能级统计无法使用。作者提出使用非阿贝尔贝里曲率作为混沌的内在探针。

Method: The method involves calculating the non-Abelian Berry curvature for BPS states under marginal deformations. For states dual to horizonless geometries, such as 1/2-BPS states in the D1/D5 CFT and 1/4-BPS states in $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM, the authors show that the Berry curvature is non-random and often exactly zero. For states dual to supersymmetric black holes, the authors perform computations in $\mathcal{N}=2$ super-JT gravity and explicit numerics in the $\mathcal{N}=2$ SYK model, finding that the Berry curvature resembles a random matrix. Additionally, the topological features of the $\mathcal{N}=2$ SYK moduli space are probed through Chern numbers.

该方法涉及计算BPS态在边缘变形下的非阿贝尔贝里曲率。对于与无视界几何对应的态，如D1/D5 CFT中的1/2-BPS态和$\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM中的1/4-BPS态，作者表明贝里曲率是非随机的，并且通常是精确为零的。对于与超对称黑洞对应的态，作者在$\mathcal{N}=2$ 超JT引力中进行计算，并在$\mathcal{N}=2$ SYK模型中进行显式数值计算，发现贝里曲率类似于随机矩阵。此外，通过陈数探测了$\mathcal{N}=2$ SYK模空间的拓扑特征。

Result: For states dual to horizonless geometries, the Berry curvature is found to be non-random and often exactly zero at generic couplings. In contrast, for states dual to supersymmetric black holes, the Berry curvature is shown to resemble a random matrix. Furthermore, interesting topological features of the $\mathcal{N}=2$ SYK moduli space are uncovered through the analysis of Chern numbers.

对于与无视界几何对应的态，在一般耦合下发现贝里曲率是非随机的，并且通常是精确为零的。相比之下，对于与超对称黑洞对应的态，贝里曲率被证明类似于随机矩阵。此外，通过分析陈数揭示了$\mathcal{N}=2$ SYK模空间的一些有趣的拓扑特征。

Conclusion: The results suggest that the non-Abelian Berry curvature sharply distinguishes black hole microstates from smooth horizonless states and provides a robust diagnostic of chaos in supersymmetric sectors. This intrinsic probe of chaos could potentially be used to further understand the nature of black hole microstates and their chaotic properties.

结果表明，非阿贝尔贝里曲率可以清晰地区分黑洞微观状态和平滑无视界状态，并为超对称扇区中的混沌提供了一个稳健的诊断工具。这种混沌的内在探针有可能进一步用于理解黑洞微观状态及其混沌性质。

Abstract: We expect black hole microstates to differ in their chaotic properties from states associated with other geometries. For supersymmetric black holes, ordinary level statistics cannot diagnose this distinction, since their energy levels are exactly degenerate. We propose that there is an intrinsic probe of chaos, encoded in the mixing of the microstates under changes in the couplings of the theory, as determined by the non-Abelian Berry curvature of the BPS states under certain deformations. For states dual to horizonless geometries in holographic systems, such as 1/2-BPS states in the D1/D5 CFT and 1/4-BPS states in $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM, we find that the Berry curvature for marginal deformations is non-random and often exactly zero at generic couplings. By contrast, for states dual to supersymmetric black holes, we show through computations in $\mathcal{N}=2$ super-JT gravity and explicit numerics in the $\mathcal{N}=2$ SYK model that the Berry curvature resembles a random matrix. We also uncover interesting topological features of the $\mathcal{N}=2$ SYK moduli space, as probed by Chern numbers. These results suggest that the Berry curvature sharply distinguishes black hole microstates from smooth horizonless states and provides a robust diagnostic of chaos in supersymmetric sectors.

</details>


### [7] [Smooth Threshold Effects from Dimensional Regularization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23526)
*Yannick Kluth*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper introduces a non-minimal renormalization scheme that incorporates threshold effects of heavy particles, providing a mass-dependent approach that retains the benefits of minimal subtraction while addressing its limitations. The scheme is demonstrated in QCD and shown to be consistent with the Appelquist-Carazzone theorem.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation for this work is to develop a renormalization scheme that naturally includes the threshold effects of heavy particles, which are often neglected in mass-independent schemes like minimal subtraction. The authors aim to create a scheme that can smoothly transition at particle thresholds while retaining the advantages of minimal subtraction, such as gauge independence.

本文的动机是开发一种自然包含重粒子阈值效应的重整化方案，这些效应在像最小减除这样的质量无关方案中经常被忽略。作者旨在创建一个能够在粒子阈值处平滑过渡的方案，同时保留最小减除的优点，如规范独立性。

Method: The authors propose a non-minimal renormalization scheme based on dimensional regularization. This scheme renormalizes couplings and masses to subtract all poles in $d \geq 4$, making it mass-dependent. The method is designed to avoid the shortcomings of mass-independent schemes while retaining the advantages of minimal subtraction. Explicit one-loop computations in QCD are performed to demonstrate the scheme's effectiveness.

作者提出了一种基于维数正规化的非最小重整化方案。该方案通过重整耦合和质量来消除$d \geq 4$中的所有极点，使其依赖于质量。该方法旨在避免质量无关方案的缺点，同时保留最小减除的优点。通过在QCD中进行显式的一圈计算来展示该方案的有效性。

Result: The proposed scheme reduces to minimal subtraction at high energies, ensuring consistency with well-established results. At particle thresholds, the scheme provides smooth transitions, and it is consistent with the Appelquist-Carazzone theorem, which states that the effects of heavy particles decouple at low energies.

所提出的方案在高能情况下退化为最小减除，确保与已建立的结果一致。在粒子阈值处，该方案提供了平滑的过渡，并且与Appelquist-Carazzone定理一致，该定理指出重粒子在低能下的效应会解耦。

Conclusion: The new renormalization scheme successfully incorporates threshold effects of heavy particles, providing a mass-dependent approach that retains the benefits of minimal subtraction. It is demonstrated to be effective in QCD and could have potential applications in other areas of particle physics.

新的重整化方案成功地包含了重粒子的阈值效应，提供了一种依赖于质量的方法，同时保留了最小减除的优点。它在QCD中被证明是有效的，并可能在粒子物理的其他领域有潜在的应用。

Abstract: We suggest a non-minimal renormalization scheme based on dimensional regularization that naturally incorporates threshold effects of heavy particles. By renormalizing couplings and masses to subtract all poles in $d \geq 4$, the resulting scheme is mass-dependent and circumvents shortcomings of mass-independent schemes like minimal subtraction. At the same time, many advantages of minimal subtraction such as gauge independence are retained. Through explicit one-loop computations in QCD, we demonstrate that this scheme reduces to minimal subtraction at high energies while providing smooth transitions at particle thresholds and implementing the Appelquist-Carazzone theorem. Potential future applications and extensions are discussed.

</details>


### [8] [Universal Interpretation of Hidden Zero and $2$-Split of Tree-Level Amplitudes Using Feynman Diagrams, Part $\mathbf{I}$: ${\rm Tr}(φ^3)$, NLSM and YM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23680)
*Kang Zhou*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper introduces a universal diagrammatic interpretation for hidden zeros and 2-splits in tree-level amplitudes, extending the concept from Tr(φ^3) to NLSM and YM theories. This is achieved through a shuffle factorization along specific lines (SFASL), which unifies the understanding of these phenomena across different theories.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to provide a unified and generalized framework for interpreting hidden zeros and 2-splits in tree-level amplitudes, which were initially understood only for Tr(φ^3) amplitudes. By extending this to NLSM and YM theories, the authors aim to deepen the understanding of these amplitude properties across different theoretical contexts.

动机是为树级振幅中的隐藏零点和2-分裂提供一个统一且通用的解释框架，这些现象最初仅在Tr(φ^3)振幅中被理解。通过将这一理解扩展到NLSM和YM理论，作者旨在深化对不同理论背景下这些振幅性质的理解。

Method: The method involves extending the previously developed shuffle factorization along specific lines (SFASL) to NLSM and YM theories. This extension allows for the separation of Feynman diagrams along specific lines under certain kinematic constraints, leading to a unified interpretation of hidden zeros and 2-splits. The SFASL mechanism is based on summing over shuffle permutations and then separating the diagrams, akin to unzipping zippers.

该方法涉及将先前开发的特定线上的洗牌因子化（SFASL）扩展到NLSM和YM理论。这种扩展允许在某些运动学约束下沿着特定线分离费曼图，从而导致对隐藏零点和2-分裂的统一解释。SFASL机制基于对洗牌排列求和然后分离图，类似于拉开拉链。

Result: The results show that the hidden zeros in the tree-level amplitudes are due to the on-shell condition $k_j^2=0$ of a massless particle, while the 2-splits arise from separating each Feynman diagram along two lines. This provides a consistent and unified explanation for these phenomena across Tr(φ^3), NLSM, and YM theories.

结果表明，树级振幅中的隐藏零点是由于无质量粒子的在壳条件$k_j^2=0$，而2-分裂则源于沿两条线分离每个费曼图。这为Tr(φ^3)、NLSM和YM理论中的这些现象提供了一致且统一的解释。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the proposed SFASL mechanism successfully unifies the interpretation of hidden zeros and 2-splits in tree-level amplitudes for Tr(φ^3), NLSM, and YM theories. This provides a deeper and more general understanding of these amplitude properties, potentially opening up new avenues for further research in quantum field theory.

结论是，所提出的SFASL机制成功地统一了Tr(φ^3)、NLSM和YM理论中树级振幅的隐藏零点和2-分裂的解释。这为这些振幅性质提供了更深入和更通用的理解，可能为量子场论的进一步研究开辟新的途径。

Abstract: In this paper, we propose a universal diagrammatic interpretation of hidden zeros and $2$-splits of tree-level amplitudes. Originally developed for ${\rm Tr}(φ^3)$ amplitudes in our previous work, this interpretation is now extended to tree-level amplitudes in Nonlinear sigma model (NLSM) and Yang-Mills (YM) theories. The interpretation is based on a certain factorization behavior of Feynman diagrams under specific kinematic constraints, which we term shuffle factorization along a specific line (SFASL). This mechanism allows us to separate Feynman diagrams along specific lines after summing over shuffle permutations. When applied to NLSM and YM amplitudes, we perform proper extensions of the SFASL used in the ${\rm Tr}(φ^3)$ case. Through the SFASL, the interpretation for the hidden zeros and $2$-splits of tree amplitudes of ${\rm Tr}(φ^3)$, NLSM, and YM can be unified as: the hidden zeros are ascribed to the on-shell condition $k_j^2=0$ of a massless particle, while the $2$-splits are caused by separating each Feynman diagram along two lines, akin to unzipping two zippers.

### [9] [Rotating End of the World](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23845)
*Kyung Kiu Kim,Hawjin Eom,Jung Hun Lee,Yunseok Seo*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper investigates the thermodynamics and interior structures of EoW branes in a rotating BTZ black hole, using the JT system and SYK model. It derives the first law of thermodynamics for BCFT, verifies the equivalence of shadow and boundary entropies, and explores possible EoW brane configurations inside the horizon, showing a potential transition within the horizon.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the thermodynamic properties and internal structure of EoW branes in the context of a rotating BTZ black hole. The authors aim to incorporate boundary degrees of freedom into the thermodynamics of the BCFT, and explore the relationship between different EoW brane configurations and their energies inside the horizon.

动机是理解在旋转BTZ黑洞背景下的世界末日（EoW）膜的热力学性质和内部结构。作者旨在将边界自由度纳入边界共形场论（BCFT）的热力学中，并探讨不同EoW膜配置及其能量在视界内的关系。

Method: The authors map the induced metric of the EoW branes to an effective Jackiw-Teitelboim (JT) system, derive the first law of thermodynamics for the BCFT, and use the duality between the JT black hole and the Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (SYK) model. They also verify the equivalence of shadow entropy and boundary entropy using Hubeny-Ryu-Takayanagi (HRT) surfaces, and explore the interior configurations of the EoW brane, considering both single and double-joint EoW branes.

作者将EoW膜的诱导度量映射到有效的Jackiw-Teitelboim (JT) 系统，推导出BCFT的第一热力学定律，并使用JT黑洞与Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (SYK) 模型之间的对偶性。他们还利用Hubeny-Ryu-Takayanagi (HRT) 曲面验证了阴影熵和边界熵的等价性，并探讨了EoW膜的内部配置，考虑了单连接和双连接EoW膜。

Result: The key results include the derivation of the first law of thermodynamics for the BCFT, the verification of the equivalence between shadow entropy and boundary entropy, and the exploration of the interior configurations of the EoW branes. The authors show that a transition could occur within the horizon, as evidenced by the energy comparison of the single and double-joint EoW branes.

主要结果包括推导出BCFT的第一热力学定律、验证阴影熵和边界熵的等价性，以及探索EoW膜的内部配置。作者通过比较单连接和双连接EoW膜的能量表明，在视界内可能发生转变。

Conclusion: The study provides a deeper understanding of the thermodynamics and interior structures of EoW branes in a rotating BTZ black hole. The derived first law of thermodynamics for the BCFT, the equivalence of shadow and boundary entropies, and the potential transition of EoW brane configurations within the horizon offer new insights into the dynamics and energetics of these systems.

该研究提供了对旋转BTZ黑洞背景下EoW膜的热力学和内部结构的更深入理解。为BCFT推导出的第一热力学定律、阴影熵和边界熵的等价性，以及在视界内EoW膜配置可能发生的转变，为这些系统的动力学和能量学提供了新的见解。

Abstract: We study the thermodynamics and interior structures of dynamical end of the world (EoW) branes in the rotating BTZ black hole. By mapping the induced metric of the branes to an effective Jackiw-Teitelboim (JT) system, we derive the first law of thermodynamics for the boundary conformal field theory (BCFT), incorporating boundary degrees of freedom. To construct this thermodynamics, we adopt two frameworks of black hole chemistry and the duality between the JT black hole and the Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (SYK) model. In addition, we verify that the shadow entropy is equivalent to the boundary entropy via Hubeny-Ryu-Takayanagi (HRT) surfaces. Furthermore, we explore the possible interior configurations of the EoW brane inside the horizon. Two representative configurations, namely single and double-joint EoW branes, are considered. These disparate configurations share the same exterior brane configuration outside the horizon. By comparing their energies, we show that a transition could occur within the horizon.

### [10] [Weyl anomaly induced transport in hydrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23849)
*Shi-Zheng Yang,Jian-Hua Gao,Zuo-Tang Liang,Georgy Yu. Prokhorov,Shi Pu,Oleg V. Teryaev,Valentin I. Zakharov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper demonstrates that the Weyl (trace) anomaly in accelerated relativistic fluids generates a new non-dissipative vector current. This anomaly determines a unique second-order transport coefficient, which couples the electromagnetic field to the fluid's acceleration. The findings are derived through hydrodynamic anomaly matching and confirmed using boundary quantum field theory, with implications for screening and vacuum magnetization near the Rindler horizon.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to explore the implications of the Weyl (trace) anomaly in the context of accelerated relativistic fluids. The authors aim to uncover how this anomaly influences the transport properties of such fluids, particularly focusing on the coupling between the electromagnetic field and the fluid's acceleration. By doing so, they seek to identify new classes of anomaly-induced transport phenomena.

本文的动机是探讨Weyl（迹）反常在加速相对论流体中的影响。作者旨在揭示这种反常如何影响此类流体的输运性质，特别是关注电磁场与流体加速度之间的耦合。通过这样做，他们试图识别新的反常诱导输运现象类别。

Method: The authors employ two main methods to derive their results. First, they extend the concept of hydrodynamic anomaly matching to include the trace anomaly, allowing them to determine the second-order transport coefficient. Second, they use boundary quantum field theory, treating the Rindler horizon of an accelerated observer as an effective boundary. This dual approach provides a comprehensive understanding of the anomaly-induced transport in both the bulk and boundary perspectives.

作者采用了两种主要方法来得出他们的结果。首先，他们扩展了流体动力学反常匹配的概念，包括迹反常，从而确定二阶输运系数。其次，他们使用边界量子场论，将加速观察者的Rindler视界视为有效边界。这种双重方法提供了对块体和边界视角下反常诱导输运的全面理解。

Result: The key result of the paper is the identification of a new non-dissipative vector current in accelerated relativistic fluids, induced by the Weyl (trace) anomaly. This anomaly uniquely fixes the second-order transport coefficient, which governs the coupling between the electromagnetic field and the fluid's acceleration. In the local rest frame, the electric-field contribution induces an additional charge density, while the magnetic-field contribution generates a transverse current with a Nernst-like, thermomagnetic Hall-like tensor structure.

论文的关键结果是在加速相对论流体中识别出一个新的非耗散矢量流，由Weyl（迹）反常引起。该反常唯一地确定了二阶输运系数，该系数控制着电磁场与流体加速度之间的耦合。在局部静止框架中，电场贡献产生额外的电荷密度，而磁场贡献生成具有Nernst类、热磁霍尔类张量结构的横向电流。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that the Weyl (trace) anomaly leads to a new class of anomaly-induced transport phenomena in accelerated relativistic fluids. Specifically, it gives rise to a non-dissipative vector current, with the second-order transport coefficient uniquely determined by the anomaly. These findings have implications for the understanding of screening and vacuum magnetization effects near the Rindler horizon, and open up new avenues for exploring the interplay between anomalies and transport in relativistic systems.

论文总结说，Weyl（迹）反常导致了加速相对论流体中一类新的反常诱导输运现象。具体来说，它产生了一个非耗散矢量流，其二阶输运系数由反常唯一确定。这些发现对于理解Rindler视界附近的屏蔽和真空磁化效应具有重要意义，并为探索相对论系统中反常与输运之间的相互作用开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We show that the Weyl (trace) anomaly gives rise to a new non-dissipative vector current in accelerated relativistic fluids. The anomaly uniquely fixes the second-order transport coefficient governing the coupling between the electromagnetic field and the fluid acceleration. We derive this result by extending hydrodynamic anomaly matching to include the trace anomaly, and independently reproduce it in boundary quantum field theory by treating the Rindler horizon of an accelerated observer as an effective boundary. From the boundary perspective, the electric- and magnetic-field sectors correspond to screening and vacuum magnetization effects near the boundary. In the local rest frame, the electric-field contribution induces an additional charge density, while the magnetic-field contribution generates a transverse current with a Nernst-like, more generally thermomagnetic Hall-like, tensor structure. Our results reveal a new class of anomaly-induced transport governed by the trace anomaly.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Additionally, they seek to derive the matrix coordinates for fuzzy supersphere geometries and to investigate the geometric transformation between fuzzy objects induced by the theta correspondence of Howe duality.

Method: Howe duality is employed to relate different Landau levels and to reveal the emergence of a dual fuzzy geometry. Abstract: Landau models serve as quantum mechanical systems for generating quantum matrix geometries. In this paper, we demonstrate that Howe duality provides the underlying structure of the super Landau model, reflecting a general feature of coset-type Landau models. The (super) Howe duality relates different Landau levels and accounts for the emergence of a dual fuzzy geometry. By employing super-spinor derivative operators, the supermonopole harmonics in both integer and half-integer Landau levels are explicitly constructed and the algebraic structure of the super-Hilbert space is revealed. We propose a consistent probabilistic interpretation for these wavefunctions defined on a supermanifold. Through a level projection method, we derive the matrix coordinates of fuzzy supersphere geometries for arbitrary Landau levels, along with a precise determination of the non-commutative scale factor. It is shown that the theta correspondence of Howe duality induces a geometric transformation between fuzzy objects. Finally, we point out that Howe duality realizes an internal-external space duality and underlies quantum matrix geometries, suggesting that it may play a fundamental role in understanding Matrix model geometries.

TL;DR: The paper examines nonlinear EFTs with factorially growing perturbative expansions, using the resummed relative entropy to derive bounds on EFT coefficients and identify nonperturbative instabilities such as the Schwinger effect in fermionic QED.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore the behavior of EFTs with a factorial growth in their perturbative expansions, specifically focusing on how the relative entropy can be used to derive constraints on the coefficients of higher-dimensional operators. The goal is to understand the stability and nonperturbative effects in these theories. 

动机是研究具有阶乘增长的微扰展开的有效场论（EFTs），特别是关注相对熵如何用于推导高维算子系数的约束。目标是理解这些理论中的稳定性和非微扰效应。

Method: The method involves using the resummed relative entropy to analyze the EFTs. The non-negativity of the resummed relative entropy is used to fix the sign of the asymptotic growth of the EFT coefficients, while its violation signals instabilities. The authors also apply this method to fermionic QED, where the Schwinger effect, a nonperturbative instability, is captured by the resummed relative entropy. 

方法涉及使用重新求和的相对熵来分析EFTs。重新求和的相对熵的非负性用于确定EFT系数渐近增长的符号，而其违反则表明不稳定。作者还将此方法应用于费米子QED，其中非微扰不稳定性Schwinger效应通过重新求和的相对熵被捕获。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the resummed relative entropy is a valuable tool for analyzing the stability and nonperturbative effects in EFTs with factorially growing perturbative expansions. It provides a way to constrain the coefficients of higher-dimensional operators and to detect nonperturbative instabilities, such as the Schwinger effect in fermionic QED. 

结论是，重新求和的相对熵是分析具有阶乘增长的微扰展开的EFTs的稳定性和非微扰效应的有价值的工具。它提供了一种约束高维算子系数的方法，并能够检测非微扰不稳定性，例如费米子QED中的Schwinger效应。

Abstract: We study nonlinear effective field theories (EFTs) with factorially growing perturbative expansions, focusing on a class in which the relative entropy encodes an infinite tower of higher-dimensional operators. Using the resummed relative entropy, we derive bounds on EFT coefficients: the non-negativity of the resummed relative entropy fixes the sign of their asymptotic growth, while its violation signals instabilities. In fermionic QED, analytic continuation from Euclidean to Minkowski spacetime yields a concrete example: the Schwinger effect, a nonperturbative instability captured by the resummed relative entropy.

### [14] [Asymptotic regularization method. A constructive approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24292)
*Christian Durán Romero,Luis J. Garay,Mercedes Martín-Benito,Rita B. Neves*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: A new regularization scheme for divergent integrals in QFT is introduced, based on the asymptotic expansion of the integrand. This method isolates UV singularities and allows for consistent divergence subtraction while preserving covariance and gauge symmetry. It also provides a non-local logarithmic dependence in renormalized quantities, applicable to theories with modified dispersion relations and non-standard UV scaling, and can be extended to handle infrared singularities.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to develop a regularization scheme that can consistently subtract divergences in quantum field theory (QFT) while preserving important symmetries such as covariance and gauge invariance. The method aims to address the limitations of traditional renormalization techniques, especially in theories with non-standard UV behavior or modified dispersion relations, by focusing on the asymptotic structure of the integrand.

Method: The method involves a structural decomposition of the integrand's asymptotic expansion, distinguishing between contributions that lead to ultraviolet (UV) singularities and those that remain finite. This allows for the isolation of the genuinely singular sector, enabling a consistent subtraction of divergences. The approach does not rely on standard relativistic power counting, making it suitable for theories with modified dispersion relations and non-standard UV scaling. The method also reveals a non-local logarithmic dependence in renormalized quantities, which is determined by the UV asymptotics independently of the standard renormalization-group flows.

Result: The result is a regularization scheme that maintains covariance and gauge symmetry while allowing for the consistent subtraction of UV divergences. In single-scale theories, the renormalized quantities exhibit a non-local logarithmic dependence uniquely determined by the UV asymptotics. This method is applicable to theories with modified dispersion relations and non-standard UV scaling, and it can be extended to handle infrared (IR) singularities as well.

Conclusion: The new regularization scheme provides a robust framework for handling divergences in QFT, particularly in theories with non-standard UV behavior. By focusing on the asymptotic structure of the integrand, it offers a consistent way to isolate and subtract singularities while preserving key symmetries. The method also reveals a non-local logarithmic dependence in renormalized quantities, which is an important feature for understanding the behavior of QFTs beyond the standard renormalization group framework.

Abstract: We introduce a new regularization scheme for divergent integrals in quantum field theory. The framework is based on the structural decomposition of the integrand asymptotic expansion, which distinguishes between contributions that drive UV singularities and those that remain finite. This asymptotic regularization method isolates the genuinely singular sector and enables a consistent subtraction of divergences while maintaining covariance and gauge symmetry. In single-scale theories, we show that the renormalized quantities exhibit a non-local logarithmic dependence uniquely determined by the UV asymptotics, offering a derivation of logarithmic terms that is independent of standard renormalization-group flows. Because it relies only on asymptotic structure rather than on standard relativistic power counting, the method is naturally applicable to theories with modified dispersion relations and non-standard UV scaling. Although formulated here for ultraviolet divergences, the underlying strategy extends straightforwardly to infrared singularities.

### [15] [Chiral Magnetic effect as the anomaly in the transverse axial vector Ward Identity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24410)
*Fei Gao,Yi Lu,Minghui Ding,Xinyang Wang,Yuxin Liu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper analyzes the quark propagator under a magnetic field and establishes the axial anomaly's origin from an additional Dirac structure. It connects the axial anomaly to the system's topological properties and confirms that the chiral magnetic effect (CME) arises from the same term responsible for the axial anomaly, with a constant CME conductivity $C_{\rm CME}=\frac{1}{2\pi^2}$, robust against various parameters. Numerical verification is provided using the full quark propagator under a magnetic field from functional QCD methods.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of the paper is to explore the origin of the axial anomaly in the context of quark propagators under a magnetic field and to connect it to the topological properties of the system. The authors aim to understand the relationship between the axial anomaly and the chiral magnetic effect (CME), and to verify the robustness of the CME conductivity against temperature, chemical potential, magnetic field, and interactions.

本文的动机是探索在磁场下的夸克传播子中轴向反常的起源，并将其与系统的拓扑性质联系起来。作者旨在理解轴向反常与手征磁效应（CME）之间的关系，并验证CME电导率对温度、化学势、磁场和相互作用的鲁棒性。

Method: The method involves analyzing the quark propagator under a magnetic field, identifying the additional Dirac structure induced by the magnetic field, and connecting this structure to the axial anomaly through the axial vector Ward identity. The authors use the tree-level propagator to reproduce the anomalous axial current results from the Dirac Hamiltonian approach and kinetic theory. They also confirm the CME's origin from the same term responsible for the axial anomaly and numerically verify the CME conductivity using the full quark propagator under a magnetic field calculated from functional QCD methods.

该方法涉及分析磁场下的夸克传播子，识别由磁场引起的额外狄拉克结构，并通过轴向矢量沃德恒等式将此结构与轴向反常联系起来。作者使用树级传播子重现了从狄拉克哈密顿量方法和动力学理论得到的异常轴向电流结果。他们还确认了CME起源于负责轴向反常的同一项，并使用从泛函QCD方法计算出的磁场下的全夸克传播子数值验证了CME电导率。

Result: The key result is the confirmation that the chiral magnetic effect (CME) originates from the same term that is responsible for the axial anomaly, specifically, as the anomaly of the transversal axial vector Ward Identity. The CME conductivity $C_{\rm CME}$ is found to be a constant, given by $C_{\rm CME}=\frac{1}{2\pi^2}$, and is robust against variations in temperature, chemical potential, magnetic field, and interaction. This result is numerically verified using the full quark propagator under a magnetic field from functional QCD methods.

主要结果是确认手征磁效应（CME）起源于负责轴向反常的同一项，具体来说，作为横向轴向矢量沃德恒等式的反常。CME电导率 $C_{\rm CME}$ 被发现是一个常数，为 $C_{\rm CME}=\frac{1}{2\pi^2}$，并且对温度、化学势、磁场和相互作用的变化具有鲁棒性。这一结果通过使用从泛函QCD方法计算出的磁场下的全夸克传播子进行了数值验证。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that the axial anomaly and the chiral magnetic effect (CME) are intrinsically linked through the additional Dirac structure in the quark propagator under a magnetic field. The CME conductivity is a universal constant, robust against various physical conditions, and is confirmed both analytically and numerically. This work provides a deeper understanding of the interplay between the axial anomaly and the CME, and their topological origins.

本文得出结论，轴向反常和手征磁效应（CME）通过磁场下夸克传播子中的额外狄拉克结构内在地联系在一起。CME电导率是一个普遍的常数，对各种物理条件具有鲁棒性，并且得到了解析和数值上的确认。这项工作提供了对轴向反常和CME之间相互作用及其拓扑起源的更深入理解。

Abstract: Through analyzing the quark propagator under the magnetic field, we establish that the axial anomaly originates from an additional Dirac structure in quark propagator induced by the magnetic field. This Dirac structure also allows one to connect the axial anomaly with the topological properties of the system by checking the axial vector Ward identity. For the tree level propagator, we reproduce the result of the anomalous axial current as in the Dirac Hamiltonian approach and kinetic theory. Particularly, we confirm that the chiral magnetic effect (CME) comes from the same term that is in charge of the axial anomaly, specifically, as the anomaly of the transversal axial vector Ward Identity. The identity guarantees that the CME conductivity $C_{\rm CME}$ is a constant as $C_{\rm CME}=\frac{1}{2π^2}$, and is robust against the temperature, chemical potential, magnetic field and also interaction. Finally, we verify this numerically by applying the full quark propagator under magnetic field calculated from the functional QCD methods.

</details>


### [16] [Non-Relativistic Chern-Simons Supergravity with Torsion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24615)
*Francisco Barriga,Patrick Concha,Nelson Merino,Evelyn Rodríguez*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper constructs a 3D non-relativistic Chern--Simons supergravity theory with curvature and torsion using the Mielke--Baekler framework. It employs a $\mathcal{N}=2$ supersymmetric extension and a semigroup expansion method to overcome typical issues in non-relativistic supergravity, resulting in a model with two parameters $(p,q)$ that unifies various non-relativistic supergravity theories.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to develop a consistent non-relativistic supergravity formulation that overcomes the usual difficulties, such as the closure of the superalgebra and the existence of a non-degenerate invariant bilinear form. This is achieved by starting from a $\mathcal{N}=2$ supersymmetric extension of the Mielke--Baekler algebra and using the semigroup expansion method, rather than a naive contraction.

动机是开发一个一致的非相对论超引力公式，克服通常的困难，如超代数的闭合性和非退化不变双线性形式的存在。这是通过从Mielke--Baekler代数的$\mathcal{N}=2$超对称扩展开始，并使用半群展开方法而不是简单的收缩来实现的。

Method: The method involves constructing a three-dimensional non-relativistic Chern--Simons supergravity theory within the Mielke--Baekler framework. The authors use a $\mathcal{N}=2$ supersymmetric extension of the Mielke--Baekler algebra and apply the semigroup expansion method to implement a non-relativistic expansion. This approach ensures the closure of the superalgebra and the existence of a non-degenerate invariant bilinear form.

该方法涉及在Mielke--Baekler框架内构建三维非相对论Chern--Simons超引力理论。作者使用Mielke--Baekler代数的$\mathcal{N}=2$超对称扩展，并应用半群展开方法来实现非相对论展开。这种方法确保了超代数的闭合性和非退化不变双线性形式的存在。

Result: The result is a non-relativistic supergravity model characterized by two parameters $(p,q)$. These parameters interpolate between different non-relativistic supergravity theories, including the extended Bargmann, Newton--Hooke, and torsional models. The model provides a unified framework for non-relativistic supergravity with torsion and opens new avenues for exploring supersymmetric extensions of Galilean and Carrollian gravity theories.

结果是一个由两个参数$(p,q)$表征的非相对论超引力模型。这些参数在不同的非相对论超引力理论之间进行插值，包括扩展的Bargmann、Newton--Hooke和扭量模型。该模型为具有扭量的非相对论超引力提供了一个统一的框架，并为探索伽利略和Carroll引力理论的超对称扩展开辟了新的途径。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the constructed model successfully overcomes the usual difficulties in non-relativistic supergravity, providing a unified framework for various non-relativistic supergravity theories. This work opens new avenues for exploring supersymmetric extensions of Galilean and Carrollian gravity theories.

结论是，所构建的模型成功地克服了非相对论超引力中的常见困难，为各种非相对论超引力理论提供了一个统一的框架。这项工作为探索伽利略和Carroll引力理论的超对称扩展开辟了新的途径。

Abstract: In this work, we construct a three-dimensional non-relativistic Chern--Simons supergravity theory with both curvature and torsion within the Mielke--Baekler framework. We show that a consistent non-relativistic supergravity formulation requires starting from a $\mathcal{N}=2$ supersymmetric extension of the Mielke--Baekler algebra and implementing a non-relativistic expansion via the semigroup expansion method, rather than a naive contraction. This procedure allows one to overcome the usual difficulties of non-relativistic supergravity constructions, ensuring closure of the superalgebra and the existence of a non-degenerate invariant bilinear form. The resulting model is characterized by two parameters $(p,q)$, which interpolate between different non-relativistic supergravity theories, including the extended Bargmann, Newton--Hooke, and torsional models. Our results provide a unified framework for non-relativistic supergravity with torsion and open new avenues for exploring supersymmetric extensions of Galilean and Carrollian gravity theories.

### [17] [Solving Einstein's Equation Numerically on Manifolds with Non-Orientable Spatial Slices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22954)
*Fan Zhang,Lee Lindblom*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper explores solutions to Einstein's equations on manifolds with compact non-orientable spatial slices, covering a range of spatial curvatures. The solutions are used to test and evaluate the numerical methods and code employed in their construction.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to investigate the behavior of cosmological models on non-orientable manifolds and to rigorously test the numerical methods and codes used for constructing these solutions. This is important for understanding the limitations and robustness of the computational techniques in the context of general relativity and cosmology.

动机是研究非定向流形上的宇宙学模型的行为，并严格测试用于构建这些解的数值方法和代码。这对于理解广义相对论和宇宙学背景下的计算技术的局限性和稳健性非常重要。

Method: The authors construct solutions to Einstein's equations on manifolds with compact non-orientable spatial slices. They use numerical methods to solve the equations on a variety of manifolds with different spatial scalar curvatures (positive, negative, and vanishing). The solutions include both homogeneous and inhomogeneous cases, and the numerical methods are tested for accuracy and robustness.

作者在具有紧致非定向空间切片的流形上构造爱因斯坦方程的解。他们使用数值方法在不同空间标量曲率（正、负和消失）的各种流形上求解方程。这些解包括均匀和不均匀的情况，并且对数值方法的准确性和鲁棒性进行了测试。

Result: The results show that the constructed solutions can accurately represent both homogeneous and inhomogeneous cosmological models on non-orientable manifolds. One solution is locally indistinguishable from a homogeneous Friedman model, while others exhibit significant inhomogeneities. The numerical methods and code are found to be effective and reliable for the range of cases considered.

结果表明，所构造的解可以准确地表示非定向流形上的均匀和不均匀宇宙学模型。其中一个解在局部上与均匀弗里德曼模型无法区分，而其他解则表现出显著的不均匀性。数值方法和代码对于所考虑的各种情况被发现是有效和可靠的。

Conclusion: The study concludes that the numerical methods and code used are capable of handling a wide range of cosmological models on non-orientable manifolds. The ability to construct and analyze such solutions provides valuable insights into the behavior of spacetime in these unique geometries, and highlights the importance of rigorous testing in numerical relativity.

研究表明，所使用的数值方法和代码能够处理非定向流形上的各种宇宙学模型。能够构造和分析这样的解为这些独特几何中的时空行为提供了有价值的见解，并强调了数值相对论中严格测试的重要性。

Abstract: This paper presents solutions to Einstein's equation -- and the numerical methods used to construct them -- that describe simple cosmological models on manifolds with compact non-orientable spatial slices. These solutions have been constructed on a selection of manifolds having positive, negative, and vanishing spatial scalar curvatures. One example is shown to be indistinguishable locally from a homogeneous Friedman cosmological model, others are constructed with significant inhomogeneities. Together these examples are used to explore the strengths and the limitations of the numerical methods used in this study, and to test the code used to implement them.

</details>


### [18] [Assessing EMRI Detectability of the Rotating Quantum Oppenheimer-Snyder Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23163)
*Dan Zhang,Shulan Li,Guoyang Fu,Jian-Pin Wu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper evaluates the impact of quantum gravity on extreme-mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) for a rotating quantum Oppenheimer-Snyder black hole, finding that quantum effects produce detectable signatures in LISA, but these are suppressed by rotation.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore how quantum gravity corrections affect the gravitational wave (GW) dephasing in EMRIs and to understand the detectability of these effects with LISA, particularly in the presence of black hole rotation. [English Text]

动机是探讨量子引力修正如何影响EMRI中的引力波（GW）相位偏移，并理解这些效应在黑洞旋转存在的情况下通过LISA探测的可能性。

Method: The method involves using adiabatic evolution to compute the GW dephasing due to the quantum correction $\alpha$. The augmented analytic kludge (AAK) waveform is generated, and the faithfulness between waveforms with and without the quantum parameter $\alpha$ is investigated for different values of the rotation parameter $a$. [English Text]

方法包括使用绝热演化计算由于量子修正 $\alpha$ 引起的GW相位偏移。生成增强解析近似（AAK）波形，并针对不同的旋转参数 $a$ 值，研究有无量子参数 $\alpha$ 的波形之间的保真度。

Result: The results show that quantum gravity effects induce detectable imprints in LISA, but these signatures are suppressed by the presence of rotation. [English Text]

结果显示，量子引力效应在LISA中产生可检测的印记，但这些印记被旋转的存在所抑制。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that rotational degrees of freedom must be carefully considered when probing quantum gravity with EMRI observations, as they can significantly suppress the detectable signatures of quantum effects. [English Text]

结论是，在使用EMRI观测探测量子引力时，必须仔细考虑旋转自由度，因为它们可以显著抑制量子效应的可检测印记。

Abstract: This letter presents an assessment of quantum gravity effects on extreme-mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) for the rotating quantum Oppenheimer-Snyder (qOS) black hole. Employing the adiabatic evolution, we compute the gravitational wave (GW) dephasing, which quantifies the cumulative phase shift induced by the quantum correction α . We further generate the augmented analytic kludge (AAK) waveform and investigate the faithfulness between the waveforms with and without the quantum parameter α for different values of a. Our results reveal that the quantum gravity effect induces detectable imprints in LISA, while the presence of rotation suppresses these signatures. This suggests that rotational degrees of freedom must be carefully accounted for when probing quantum gravity with EMRI observations.

### [19] [Ground measurements of the gravitational redshift questioned:re-establishing the physical bases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23250)
*Anna M. Nobili,Alberto Anselmi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper addresses and refutes the claims made by Asenbaum, Overstreet, and Kasevic (2024) regarding the Pound and Rebka experiment. The authors clarify that the original experiment did indeed measure the gravitational redshift as predicted by Einstein, and not a Doppler shift due to non-gravitational forces, correcting a misunderstanding of reference systems and the interpretation of forces involved.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation for this paper is to address and correct the alleged inconsistencies in the scientific and educational literature concerning the first experimental measurement of the gravitational redshift by Pound and Rebka in 1960. Specifically, it aims to refute the claim by Asenbaum, Overstreet, and Kasevic (2024) that the experiment measured a Doppler shift rather than the gravitational redshift. 

本文的动机是解决科学和教育文献中关于Pound和Rebka在1960年首次测量引力红移实验的所谓不一致之处。具体来说，它旨在反驳Asenbaum、Overstreet和Kasevic（2024）提出的该实验测量的是多普勒频移而非引力红移的说法。

Method: The method involves a detailed re-examination of the Pound and Rebka experiment, focusing on the proper understanding of the reference systems used and the physical interpretation of the forces involved. The authors provide a clear distinction between gravitational and non-gravitational effects, clarifying the nature of the redshift observed in the original experiment. 

方法涉及对Pound和Rebka实验进行详细重新审查，重点在于正确理解所使用的参考系以及涉及力的物理解释。作者明确区分了引力效应和非引力效应，澄清了原始实验中观察到的红移的本质。

Result: The result of this work is a reaffirmation that the Pound and Rebka experiment successfully measured the gravitational redshift as predicted by Einstein's theory of general relativity. It also provides a deeper understanding of the experimental setup and the physical principles underlying the observed redshift. 

这项工作的结果是重申Pound和Rebka实验成功地测量了爱因斯坦广义相对论预测的引力红移。它还提供了对实验装置和观测到的红移背后的物理原理的更深入理解。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the original interpretation of the Pound and Rebka experiment as a measurement of gravitational redshift is correct. The paper corrects the misunderstandings presented by Asenbaum, Overstreet, and Kasevic (2024) and restores the significance of the Pound and Rebka experiment in the context of gravitational physics. 

结论是，将Pound和Rebka实验解释为引力红移的测量是正确的。该论文纠正了Asenbaum、Overstreet和Kasevic（2024）提出的误解，并恢复了Pound和Rebka实验在引力物理学中的重要性。

Abstract: Motivated by alleged inconsistencies in the scientific and educational literature, Asenbaum, Overstreet and Kasevic \href{https://doi.org/10.1088/1402-4896/ad340c}{(2024)} aim to clarify some fundamental concepts in the physics of gravitation. To this end they reexamine the first experimental measurement of the gravitational redshift by Pound and Rebka in 1960, claiming that it did not in fact measure the gravitational redshift predicted by Einstein almost half a century earlier, but rather a Doppler shift originating from non-gravitational reaction forces. We show that their conclusion arises from a misunderstanding of the reference systems involved, along with an unphysical interpretation of non gravitational forces. Thus, our work restores the Pound and Rebka experiment to its rightful place in Physics.

</details>


### [20] [Spectral Butterfly Effect and Resilient Ringdown in Thick Braneworlds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23364)
*Hai-Long Jia,Wen-Di Guo,Yu-Peng Zhang,Yu-Xiao Liu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper explores the quasinormal mode spectrum in thick braneworlds, revealing a spectral butterfly effect where small perturbations to the effective potential can cause significant changes in the quasinormal modes. Despite this, the early-stage gravitational wave signal remains dominated by the original fundamental mode, indicating that the standard fingerprint is still reliable for current detectors.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to investigate the stability and robustness of the quasinormal mode spectrum in thick braneworlds, which is a critical aspect linking gravitational-wave observations to extra-dimensional geometry. The authors aim to understand how infinitesimal deformations in the effective potential impact the quasinormal modes and whether these changes affect the observable gravitational wave signals.

Method: The authors use a combination of frequency-domain and time-domain analyses to study the effects of perturbations on the quasinormal modes. They analyze the sensitivity of the quasinormal modes to the location and strength of the perturbations. Additionally, they examine the localization of the graviton zero mode to ensure that four-dimensional gravity is preserved.

Result: The results show that thick braneworlds exhibit a spectral butterfly effect, where small perturbations to the effective potential can dramatically alter the quasinormal modes. Frequency-domain instabilities are highly sensitive to the perturbation's location and strength. In the time domain, near-brane perturbations mainly affect the early ringdown, while far-brane perturbations produce clean late-time echoes. Importantly, the graviton zero mode remains localized, preserving four-dimensional gravity.

Conclusion: The conclusion is that despite the pronounced spectral fragility, the observable early-stage gravitational wave signal under current detector sensitivities is still dominated by the original fundamental mode. This supports the continued use of the standard quasinormal mode fingerprint in present-day gravitational-wave astronomy, while also revealing its hidden sensitivity to extra-dimensional perturbations.

Abstract: The quasinormal mode spectrum is a unique fingerprint linking gravitational-wave observations to extra-dimensional geometry. In this Letter, we show that thick braneworlds exhibit a spectral butterfly effect: infinitesimal deformations of the effective potential trigger dramatic migrations of quasinormal modes, challenging the presumed stability of this fingerprint. Frequency-domain instabilities depend sensitively on the perturbation's location and strength. In the time domain, near-brane perturbations primarily modify the early ringdown, while far-brane perturbations generate clean late-time echoes. Crucially, the graviton zero mode remains localized, preserving four-dimensional gravity. Despite this pronounced spectral fragility, the observable early-stage signal under current detector sensitivities is still dominated by the original fundamental mode. Hence, thick braneworlds display a nontrivial coexistence of a fragile spectrum and a resilient ringdown, supporting the continued use of the standard fingerprint in present-day gravitational-wave astronomy while revealing its hidden sensitivity.

</details>


### [21] [Forecasting graviton-mass constraints from the full covariance of PTA-astrometry ORF estimators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23384)
*Jing-Hong Han,Zhi-Chao Zhao*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper develops a full-covariance formalism for joint pulsar timing array (PTA) and astrometric analyses to forecast graviton-mass constraints, showing that combining PTA and astrometry can significantly improve the constraints on the graviton mass.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to develop a more comprehensive approach for analyzing gravitational-wave backgrounds by combining data from pulsar timing arrays (PTAs) and astrometric surveys. This combined analysis aims to place tighter constraints on the mass of the graviton, which is a fundamental parameter in theories of gravity.

Method: The authors derive analytic covariance expressions for auto- and cross-channel overlap reduction function estimators, including signal-signal, noise-noise, and signal-noise contributions. These expressions are validated using numerical simulations. The method is then applied to both current and future sensitivity forecasts, comparing the results with existing PTA and astrometric survey sensitivities.

Result: For a current-like forecast with sensitivities similar to NANOGrav 15 yr and Gaia, the constraint remains dominated by PTA data. However, for a future-like forecast with sensitivities comparable to the SKA and Theia/Gaia-NIR, the joint PTA-astrometry analysis improves the graviton-mass bound by about one order of magnitude.

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that combining PTA and astrometric data through a full-covariance formalism provides a viable and powerful method for placing stronger constraints on the graviton mass, especially with future, more sensitive surveys.

Abstract: We develop a full-covariance formalism for joint pulsar timing array (PTA) and astrometric analyses of a nanohertz stochastic gravitational-wave background and apply it to forecasts of graviton-mass constraints. Analytic covariance expressions are derived for auto- and cross-channel overlap reduction function estimators, including signal-signal, noise-noise, and signal-noise contributions, and are validated against numerical simulations. In a current-like forecast with sensitivities comparable to NANOGrav 15 yr and Gaia, the constraint remains PTA-dominated, while a future-like forecast with sensitivities comparable to the SKA and Theia/Gaia-NIR improves the joint graviton-mass bound by about one order of magnitude. These results demonstrate that PTA-astrometry multichannel inference provides a viable avenue for placing stronger constraints on the graviton mass.

### [22] [A Complete Invariant Analysis of the Kerr Spacetime and its Photon Region](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23389)
*Nicholas Layden,Dipanjan Dey,Alan Coley*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper presents an invariant characterization of the Kerr spacetime and uses this to derive a function that identifies a special family of null geodesics, which are tangent to every photon surface in the Kerr photon region. This provides a method for characterizing photon surfaces in axially symmetric spacetimes and a tool for efficiently computing the geodesic equations. The paper also discusses how the invariant determines the constants of motion for all spherical orbits in the photon region and derives invariants for other geometrically important surfaces like ergosurfaces and local horizons.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to provide an invariant characterization of the Kerr spacetime and use it to identify a special family of null geodesics. This allows for an invariant way to characterize photon surfaces in axially symmetric spacetimes and to efficiently compute the geodesic equations for any part of the photon region. Additionally, the paper aims to determine the constants of motion for all spherical orbits in the photon region and to derive invariants for other geometrically significant surfaces.

Method: The authors present an invariant characterization of the Kerr spacetime and use this invariant structure to derive a function whose zeros identify a special family of null geodesics. These null geodesics are tangent to every photon surface in the Kerr photon region. The invariant is parameterized by a Lorentz parameter, which effectively acts as an inclination angle of the spherical photon orbits through the equatorial plane. The paper also shows how the invariant determines the constants of motion for all spherical orbits in the photon region and briefly derives invariants for other geometrically important surfaces such as ergosurfaces and local horizons.

Result: The result is a function whose zeros identify a special family of null geodesics that are tangent to every photon surface in the Kerr photon region. This provides a method for invariantly characterizing photon surfaces in axially symmetric spacetimes and a computational tool for efficiently computing the geodesic equations. The invariant also determines the constants of motion for all spherical orbits in the photon region, and invariants for other geometrically important surfaces such as ergosurfaces and local horizons are derived.

Conclusion: The paper concludes that the invariant characterization of the Kerr spacetime provides a powerful tool for identifying and characterizing null geodesics, particularly those tangent to photon surfaces. This approach not only offers a new way to understand the geometry of the Kerr spacetime but also provides a practical computational method for studying the geodesic equations and the constants of motion in the photon region. The derived invariants for other geometrically important surfaces further enhance the utility of this invariant approach.

Abstract: We present an invariant characterization of the Kerr spacetime, and utilize the invariant structure of the spacetime to derive a function whose zeros identify a special family of null geodesics. Each member of this family is tangent to every photon surface in the Kerr photon region, offering a method of invariantly characterizing photon surfaces in axially symmetric spacetimes and thereby a providing a computational tool for efficiently computing the geodesic equations for any part of the photon region. The invariant that identifies all of the spherical photon orbits is parameterized by a Lorentz parameter, where the parameter is effectively an inclination angle of the spherical photon orbits through the equatorial plane. We also show how the invariant determines the constants of motion for all spherical orbits in the photon region. Finally, we briefly derive invariants which identify the other geometrically important surfaces such as the ergosurfaces and local horizons.
