### [23] [Gravitational Collapse of an Inhomogeneous Fluid in Rastall Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23592)
*Akbar Jahan,Naser Sadeghnezhad,Amir Hadi Ziaie*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper studies spherically symmetric gravitational collapse of an inhomogeneous, anisotropic fluid in Rastall gravity. By setting the Rastall parameter to make the effective radial pressure vanish, the authors find a class of exact nonsingular solutions where the matter shells first collapse, then bounce, and finally expand. The study also examines the formation of trapped surfaces and the validity of the weak energy condition (WEC).


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore non-singular collapse scenarios in Rastall gravity for an inhomogeneous, anisotropic fluid. The aim is to avoid the spacetime singularity that appears in the homogeneous case by carefully choosing the Rastall parameter and investigating the resulting dynamics.

Method: The method involves considering a linear equation of state (EoS) for the fluid profiles, $p_r=w_r\rho$ and $p_\theta=w_\theta\rho$, and setting the Rastall parameter such that the effective radial pressure vanishes. This allows the authors to derive a class of exact nonsingular solutions. The dynamics of the collapsing body are analyzed, including the formation of trapped surfaces and the validity of the weak energy condition (WEC).

Result: The results show that the obtained solutions allow for a collapse process followed by a bounce and subsequent expansion. Additionally, the formation of trapped surfaces can be avoided, and the bounce event does not get covered by the apparent horizon. The weak energy condition (WEC) is also found to be valid for these solutions.

Conclusion: The conclusion is that by carefully choosing the Rastall parameter, it is possible to construct non-singular collapse scenarios in Rastall gravity. These scenarios include a bounce and expansion phase, and they avoid the formation of trapped surfaces, while satisfying the weak energy condition (WEC).

Abstract: We study spherically symmetric gravitational collapse of an inhomogeneous fluid with anisotropic energy momentum tensor (EMT) in Rastall gravity. Considering a linear equation of state (EoS) for the fluid profiles, i.e., $p_r=w_rρ$ and $p_θ=w_θρ$, we try to build and investigate non-singular collapse scenarios for which, the spacetime singularity that appears in the homogeneous case~\cite{ahz2019}, is absent. We therefore set the Rastall parameter in such a way that the effective radial pressure vanishes. This helps us to obtain a class of exact nonsingular solutions in which the matter shells undergo a {collapse} process in a contracting regime, reach a bounce point, and then enter an expanding phase. We further investigate formation of trapped surfaces during the dynamical evolution of the collapsing body. {It is found} that for the obtained solutions, {the} trapped surface formation can be avoided and consequently, the bounce event is not covered by the apparent horizon. Validity of weak energy condition (WEC) is also examined for the obtained solutions.

</details>


### [24] [Physics informed operator learning of parameter dependent spectra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23625)
*Haohao Gu,Sensen He,Hanlin Song,Bo Liang,Zhenwei Lyu,Xiaoguang Hu,Minghui Du,Peng Xu,Bo-Qiang Ma*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper introduces DeepOPiraKAN, a physics-informed neural network for spectral analysis. It efficiently computes the quasinormal modes of Kerr black holes with high accuracy, demonstrating its potential for parameter-dependent spectral problems in complex physical systems.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Spectral problems, which are governed by differential operators, are fundamental to many physical systems but are computationally challenging due to their sensitivity to continuous parameters and the need for repeated evaluations across parameter space. The motivation is to develop a more efficient and accurate method to solve these problems, particularly for applications like black hole spectroscopy and ringdown modeling.

由微分算子控制的谱问题在许多物理系统中是基础性的，但由于它们对连续参数的敏感性和需要在整个参数空间内进行重复评估，因此在计算上具有挑战性。动机是开发一种更高效和准确的方法来解决这些问题，特别是应用于黑洞光谱学和振铃模型。

Method: The authors present DeepOPiraKAN, an open-source physics-informed neural network (PINN) architecture designed for spectral analysis. This approach combines operator learning with enhanced optimization stability, allowing it to capture the mapping from parameters to spectra in a single model. The framework is applied to the computation of quasinormal modes of Kerr black holes, using a trained network to resolve modes with $(\ell, m) \in \{(2,0), (2,1)\}$ and overtones up to $n=7$ across the full spin range.

作者提出了DeepOPiraKAN，这是一种用于谱分析的开源物理信息神经网络（PINN）架构。该方法结合了算子学习和增强的优化稳定性，使其能够在单个模型中捕捉从参数到谱的映射。该框架应用于克尔黑洞准正规模的计算，使用训练好的网络解析$(\ell, m) \in \{(2,0), (2,1)\}$模式及其在全自旋范围内的$n=7$阶泛音。

Result: The trained DeepOPiraKAN network accurately resolves the quasinormal modes of Kerr black holes, achieving relative errors of $\mathcal{O}(10^{-6})$ for the fundamental mode and gradually increasing to $\mathcal{O}(10^{-4})$ for higher overtones. These results are benchmarked against the Leaver's method, a well-established technique for computing quasinormal modes. The high accuracy achieved is significant for black hole spectroscopy and practical ringdown modeling for current and future observatories.

经过训练的DeepOPiraKAN网络准确地解析了克尔黑洞的准正规模，基本模式的相对误差达到$\mathcal{O}(10^{-6})$，而更高阶泛音的相对误差逐渐增加到$\mathcal{O}(10^{-4})$。这些结果与Leaver方法进行了基准测试，Leaver方法是一种成熟的计算准正规模的技术。所达到的高精度对于当前和未来的观测站的黑洞光谱学和实际振铃模型具有重要意义。

Conclusion: DeepOPiraKAN demonstrates significant potential as a general and scalable framework for solving parameter-dependent spectral problems in complex physical systems. The high accuracy and efficiency achieved in the computation of quasinormal modes for Kerr black holes highlight its applicability to black hole spectroscopy and ringdown modeling, making it a valuable tool for both theoretical and observational astrophysics.

DeepOPiraKAN展示了作为解决复杂物理系统中参数依赖谱问题的一般和可扩展框架的巨大潜力。在克尔黑洞准正规模计算中实现的高精度和效率突显了其在黑洞光谱学和振铃模型中的适用性，使其成为理论天体物理学和观测天体物理学的宝贵工具。

Abstract: Spectral problems governed by differential operators underpin a wide range of physical systems, yet remain computationally challenging because their spectra depend sensitively on continuous parameters and often demand repeated evaluations across parameter space. Here we present $\texttt{DeepOPiraKAN}$, an open source physics informed neural network architecture for spectral analysis. By combining operator learning with enhanced optimization stability, it captures the underlying parameter-to-spectrum mapping in a single model, avoiding repeated spectral solutions at isolated points in parameter space. As a representative and stringent benchmark, we apply this framework to the computation of quasinormal modes of Kerr black holes. A single trained network accurately resolves modes with $(\ell,m)\in \{(2,0),(2,1)\}$ and overtones up to $n=7$ across the full spin range, achieving relative errors of $\mathcal{O}(10^{-6})$ for the fundamental mode and gradually increasing to $\mathcal{O}(10^{-4})$ for higher overtones, benchmarked against the Leaver's method. This level of accuracy is already significant for black hole spectroscopy and practical ringdown modelling for current and future observatories. More broadly, these results highlight the potential of $\texttt{DeepOPiraKAN}$ as a general and scalable framework for parameter dependent spectral problems across complex physical systems.

</details>


### [25] [Stationary solutions in the small-$c$ expansion of GR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23677)
*Enes Bal,Ertuğrul Ekiz,Emre Onur Kahya,Utku Zorba*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper explores the small-$c$ expansion of general relativity in ADM variables up to NNLO, revealing richer stationary vacuum solutions in both strong- and weak-gravity branches. The results show that the full NLO/NNLO theory has a more diverse stationary vacuum sector compared to the magnetic Carroll truncation, and the ADM formulation provides a practical framework for constructing and analyzing these backgrounds.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to study the small-$c$ expansion of general relativity in ADM variables to make the field equations more tractable for explicit solution building, particularly in the stationary sector. The goal is to explore the structure of the strong- and weak-gravity branches and to construct exact vacuum solutions at NLO and NNLO, which can be relevant for compact astrophysical objects such as slowly rotating black holes and neutron stars.

动机是研究ADM变量下的广义相对论的小$c$展开，以使场方程在显式解构建中更易于处理，特别是在静止部分。目标是探索强引力和弱引力分支的结构，并在NLO和NNLO构造精确的真空解，这些解对于缓慢旋转黑洞和中子星等致密天体物理对象具有相关性。

Method: The method involves expanding general relativity in ADM variables up to next-to-next-to-leading order (NNLO) in the small-$c$ limit. The authors focus on the stationary sector and derive the field equations in this context. They then solve these equations to obtain exact vacuum solutions, including Lense--Thirring and rotating C-metric backgrounds at NLO, and their corresponding geometries at NNLO. The analysis also extends to the weak-gravity branch, where they find Hartle--Thorne-type solutions with an independent quadrupole moment, along with spin-squared corrections and a mixed quadrupolar-rotating solution. Higher multipoles up to $\ell=4$ are included in the analysis.

方法涉及将广义相对论在ADM变量下扩展到小$c$极限的次次领头阶（NNLO）。作者专注于静止部分，并在此背景下推导场方程。然后他们求解这些方程以获得精确的真空解，包括NLO下的Lense--Thirring和旋转C度量背景，以及它们在NNLO下的相应几何结构。分析还扩展到弱引力分支，在那里他们发现了具有独立四极矩的Hartle--Thorne型解，以及自旋平方修正和混合四极-旋转解。分析中还包括了直到$\ell=4$的高阶多极矩。

Result: The results include exact vacuum solutions at NLO and NNLO, which exhibit a richer structure in both strong- and weak-gravity branches. In the strong-gravity branch, the authors obtain Lense--Thirring and rotating C-metric solutions at NLO, and their corresponding geometries at NNLO. In the weak-gravity branch, they find Hartle--Thorne-type solutions with an independent quadrupole moment, along with spin-squared corrections and a mixed quadrupolar-rotating solution. The analysis also includes higher multipoles up to $\ell=4$. These results demonstrate that the full NLO/NNLO theory has a more diverse stationary vacuum sector than the magnetic Carroll truncation.

结果包括在NLO和NNLO下的精确真空解，这些解在强引力和弱引力分支中都表现出更丰富的结构。在强引力分支中，作者在NLO获得了Lense--Thirring和旋转C度量解，并在NNLO获得了相应的几何结构。在弱引力分支中，他们发现了具有独立四极矩的Hartle--Thorne型解，以及自旋平方修正和混合四极-旋转解。分析还包括直到$\ell=4$的高阶多极矩。这些结果表明，完整的NLO/NNLO理论比磁Carroll截断具有更多样化的静止真空部分。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the ADM formulation provides a practical framework for constructing and analyzing stationary backgrounds in the small-$c$ expansion of general relativity. The full NLO/NNLO theory admits a richer stationary vacuum sector, with exact solutions in both strong- and weak-gravity branches. This framework may also be useful for organizing rotational and higher-multipole deformations relevant to compact astrophysical objects such as slowly rotating black holes and neutron stars.

结论是ADM公式提供了一个实用的框架，用于构建和分析广义相对论的小$c$展开中的静止背景。完整的NLO/NNLO理论允许一个更丰富的静止真空部分，包括强引力和弱引力分支中的精确解。该框架也可能有助于组织与缓慢旋转黑洞和中子星等致密天体物理对象相关的旋转和高阶多极变形。

Abstract: We study the small-$c$ expansion of general relativity in ADM variables up to next-to-next-to-leading order (NNLO). We show that, in the stationary sector, this formulation renders the field equations more tractable for explicit solution building. The stationary sector exhibits both strong- and weak-gravity branches, whose structure becomes richer at NNLO. In the strong-gravity branch, we first obtain exact vacuum solutions of NLO Carroll gravity, including the Lense--Thirring and rotating C-metric backgrounds. At NNLO, we then construct the corresponding Lense--Thirring-type and C-metric-type exact vacuum geometries. These solutions also arise from the small-$c$ expansion of the Kerr and rotating C-metric geometries around the strong-gravity background, up to $\mathcal{O}(J)$ at NLO and up to $\mathcal{O}(J^3)$ at NNLO. In the weak-gravity branch, we find exact Hartle--Thorne-type solutions with an independent quadrupole moment, together with exact spin-squared corrections and a mixed quadrupolar-rotating solution. We further extend the $\ell=0,2$ sector by including higher multipoles up to $\ell=4$, where $\ell$ denotes the multipole index. These results show that the full NLO/NNLO theory admits a richer stationary vacuum sector than the magnetic Carroll truncation. More broadly, the ADM formulation provides a practical framework for constructing and analyzing stationary backgrounds in the small-$c$ expansion of general relativity, and may also offer a useful framework for organizing rotational and higher-multipole deformations relevant to compact astrophysical objects such as slowly rotating black holes and neutron stars.

</details>


### [26] [Photon regions, shadow observables and constraints from M87* of a Kerr-Newman-like black hole in Bumblebee gravity surrounded by plasma](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23721)
*Jian-Peng Zhang,Yu Zhang,Li Han*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates the photon regions, shadow, and observational constraints of a Kerr-Newman-like black hole in Bumblebee gravity within a plasma medium. The effects of spin, charge, Lorentz-violating parameter, and plasma parameter on the shadow geometry are analyzed, and the physical parameters are constrained using EHT observations of M87*.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore the characteristics of a Kerr-Newman-like black hole in Bumblebee gravity surrounded by a plasma medium, specifically focusing on its photon regions, shadow, and how these features are influenced by various physical parameters. The study aims to provide a deeper understanding of the interplay between the black hole's properties and the surrounding plasma, as well as to assess the viability of such a model in explaining real astrophysical black holes like M87*.

动机是探索在Bumblebee引力中被等离子体介质包围的Kerr-Newman类黑洞的特性，特别关注其光子区域、阴影以及这些特征如何受到各种物理参数的影响。该研究旨在更深入地理解黑洞特性和周围等离子体之间的相互作用，并评估这种模型在解释真实的天体物理黑洞（如M87*）方面的可行性。

Method: The method involves deriving the null geodesic equations for a Kerr-Newman-like black hole in Bumblebee gravity within a non-homogeneous power-law plasma model. The Hamilton-Jacobi equation is separated to obtain the geodesics, and the photon regions and black hole shadow are then analyzed. Two sets of shadow observables are introduced to quantify the effects of the spin $a$, charge $Q_0$, Lorentz-violating parameter $\ell$, and plasma parameter $k$ on the shadow geometry. The energy emission rate is also evaluated. Finally, the physical parameters are constrained using the angular diameter, circularity deviation, and axis ratio from EHT observations of M87*.

方法包括在一个非均匀幂律等离子体模型中导出Bumblebee引力中Kerr-Newman类黑洞的零测地线方程。通过分离Hamilton-Jacobi方程来获得测地线，然后分析光子区域和黑洞阴影。引入了两组阴影可观测量来量化自旋$a$、电荷$Q_0$、洛伦兹违反参数$\ell$和等离子体参数$k$对阴影几何形状的影响。还评估了能量发射率。最后，使用EHT对M87*观测得到的角度直径、圆形偏差和轴比来约束物理参数。

Result: The results show that the spin $a$ and Lorentz-violating parameter $\ell$ mainly enhance the distortion of the black hole shadow, while the charge $Q_0$ and plasma parameter $k$ primarily lead to its radial shrinkage. The energy emission rate is generally suppressed with an increase in these parameters. Using EHT observations of M87*, the viable parameter space is narrowed, and the circularity deviation $\Delta C \lesssim 0.1$ and axis ratio $1 < D_x \lesssim 4/3$ are found to be consistent with the EHT limits.

结果表明，自旋$a$和洛伦兹违反参数$\ell$主要增强了黑洞阴影的扭曲，而电荷$Q_0$和等离子体参数$k$主要导致其径向收缩。随着这些参数的增加，能量发射率通常会受到抑制。利用EHT对M87*的观测，可行的参数空间被缩小，发现圆形偏差$\Delta C \lesssim 0.1$和轴比$1 < D_x \lesssim 4/3$与EHT限制一致。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the charged rotating black hole in Bumblebee gravity surrounded by a plasma medium can produce a shadow and photon region that are consistent with the observed properties of M87*. The distinct effects of the physical parameters on the shadow geometry and the suppression of the energy emission rate suggest that this model could be a viable candidate for real astrophysical black holes. The constraints from EHT observations provide a range of possible values for the parameters, which can guide future theoretical and observational studies.

结论是，在Bumblebee引力中被等离子体介质包围的带电旋转黑洞可以产生与M87*观测到的性质一致的阴影和光子区域。物理参数对阴影几何形状的不同影响以及能量发射率的抑制表明，该模型可能是真实天体物理黑洞的可行候选者。EHT观测提供的约束为参数提供了可能的取值范围，这可以指导未来的理论和观测研究。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the photon regions, shadow, and observational constraints of a Kerr-Newman-like black hole in Bumblebee gravity within a plasma medium. By employing a specific non-homogeneous power-law plasma model to ensure the separability of the Hamilton-Jacobi equation, we derive the null geodesic equations, analyze the photon regions, and construct the black hole shadow. Furthermore, we introduce two sets of shadow observables to systematically analyze the distinct effects of each physical parameter (spin $a$, charge $Q_0$, Lorentz-violating parameter $\ell$, and plasma parameter $k$) on the shadow geometry. Specifically, we find that $a$ and $\ell$ mainly enhance the distortion of the shadow, whereas $Q_0$ and $k$ primarily lead to its radial shrinkage. Additionally, a brief evaluation of the energy emission rate shows that an increase in these parameters generally suppresses the emission peak. Finally, by modeling M87* as a charged rotating black hole in Bumblebee gravity surrounded by plasma, we can constrain the physical parameters using observations from the Event Horizon Telescope (EHT). While the angular diameter $θ_d = 42 \pm 3 \, μ\text{as}$ narrows the viable parameter space, the circularity deviation $ΔC \lesssim 0.1$ and axis ratio $1 < D_x \lesssim 4/3$ obey the EHT limits. This suggests that the charged rotating black hole in Bumblebee gravity surrounded by plasma might be a candidate for real astrophysical black holes.

</details>


### [27] [On gravitating dyonic configurations in nonlinear electrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23741)
*K. A. Bronnikov,S. V. Bolokhov,G. S. Nurbakova,B. Tynyshbay*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper examines static, spherically symmetric configurations of nonlinear electromagnetic fields with Lagrangians $L(f)$ in general relativity and other metric theories of gravity. It focuses on the special case of equal electric and magnetic charges, showing that there exists a configuration where the invariant $f$ is zero everywhere, leading to simple solutions in GR and extended theories of gravity.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of the paper is to explore the properties of dyonic systems (systems with both nonzero electric and magnetic charges) in the context of nonlinear electromagnetic fields within general relativity (GR) and other metric theories of gravity. The authors aim to find exact solutions for such systems, which are not well-known, especially when both charges are present. They focus on the special case where the electric and magnetic charges are equal, and they seek to understand the behavior of these systems under the assumption of a correct Maxwell limit of the Lagrangian $L(f)$. 

该论文的动机是探索在广义相对论（GR）和其他度量引力理论中非线性电磁场背景下，带有电荷和磁荷的双子系统（dyonic systems）的性质。作者旨在找到这些系统的精确解，尤其是当两种电荷都存在时，这些解并不为人所熟知。他们专注于电荷和磁荷相等的特殊情况，并试图理解在假设拉格朗日量 $L(f)$ 具有正确的麦克斯韦极限的情况下这些系统的行为。

Method: The method involves considering static, spherically symmetric configurations of nonlinear electromagnetic fields with Lagrangians $L(f)$, where $f = F_{μν} F^{μν}$, in the context of general relativity (GR) and other metric theories of gravity. The authors specifically study the case where the electric charge ($q_e$) and magnetic charge ($q_m$) are equal. By assuming a correct Maxwell limit of $L(f)$, they show that there exists a configuration of the electromagnetic field such that the invariant $f$ is zero throughout the entire space. This leads to the existence of corresponding families of solutions in GR and in a wide range of extended theories of gravity, such as scalar-tensor and $F(R)$ gravity.

该方法涉及在广义相对论（GR）和其他度量引力理论的背景下考虑具有拉格朗日量 $L(f)$ 的非线性电磁场的静态、球对称构型，其中 $f = F_{μν} F^{μν}$。作者特别研究了电荷 ($q_e$) 和磁荷 ($q_m$) 相等的情况。通过假设 $L(f)$ 具有正确的麦克斯韦极限，他们证明存在一种电磁场构型，使得不变量 $f$ 在整个空间中为零。这导致在GR和广泛的扩展引力理论（如标量-张量和 $F(R)$ 引力）中存在相应的解族。

Result: The result of the paper is the demonstration that for static, spherically symmetric configurations of nonlinear electromagnetic fields with equal electric and magnetic charges, there exists a specific configuration where the invariant $f = F_{μν} F^{μν}$ is zero throughout the entire space. This finding leads to the existence of new families of solutions in general relativity (GR) and in a wide range of extended theories of gravity, such as scalar-tensor and $F(R)$ gravity. These solutions are particularly simple and can coexist with other sources of gravity, like fluids or scalar fields.

该论文的结果是在具有相等电荷和磁荷的非线性电磁场的静态、球对称构型中，存在一种特定的构型，使得不变量 $f = F_{μν} F^{μν}$ 在整个空间中为零。这一发现导致在广义相对论（GR）和广泛的扩展引力理论（如标量-张量和 $F(R)$ 引力）中存在新的解族。这些解特别简单，并且可以与其他引力源（如流体或标量场）共存。

Conclusion: The conclusion of the paper is that for dyonic systems with equal electric and magnetic charges, there always exists a configuration of the electromagnetic field where the invariant $f$ is zero in the whole space. This leads to the existence of new, simple families of solutions in general relativity (GR) and in a wide range of extended theories of gravity, such as scalar-tensor and $F(R)$ gravity. These solutions can coexist with other gravitational sources, providing a new avenue for understanding the behavior of nonlinear electromagnetic fields in various gravitational theories.

该论文的结论是，对于具有相等电荷和磁荷的双子系统，总是存在一种电磁场构型，使得不变量 $f$ 在整个空间中为零。这导致在广义相对论（GR）和广泛的扩展引力理论（如标量-张量和 $F(R)$ 引力）中存在新的简单解族。这些解可以与其他引力源共存，为理解各种引力理论中的非线性电磁场行为提供了新的途径。

Abstract: We consider static, spherically symmetric configurations of nonlinear electromagnetic fields with Lagrangians $L(f)$, where $f = F_{μν} F^{μν}$, in general relativity (GR) and other metric theories of gravity. The corresponding exact solutions are well known in the framework of GR in cases where only an electric charge ($q_e$) or a magnetic charge ($q_m$) are present, but only a few solutions in particular examples of $L(f)$ are known for dyonic systems with both nonzero $q_e$ and $q_m$. We study the properties of such systems in the special case of equal electric and magnetic charges and, assuming a correct Maxwell limit of $L(f)$, show that there always exists such a configuration of the electromagnetic field that the invariant $f$ is zero in the whole space. It leads to the existence of the corresponding families of solutions both in GR in the presence of other sources of gravity (like fluids or scalar fields) and in a wide range of extended theories of gravity (e.g., scalar-tensor and $F(R)$ gravity), in which the nonlinear electromagnetic field behaves in an especially simple manner.

</details>


### [28] [From Big Bang Nucleosynthesis to Late-Time Acceleration in $f(Q,L_m)$ Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23793)
*Rajdeep Mazumdar,Kalyan Malakar,Kalyan Bhuyan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper investigates the cosmic evolution in $f(Q, L_m)$ gravity, a model with non-minimal coupling between non-metricity and matter. Using observational data and MCMC, it places constraints on the model parameters, showing consistency with early-Universe physics and observations. The model exhibits quintessence-like behavior and is a viable alternative to $\Lambda$CDM.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to explore the viability of $f(Q, L_m)$ gravity as an alternative to the standard $\Lambda$CDM model. This is achieved by examining the model's ability to describe the transition from decelerated to accelerated expansion and its consistency with various observational data sets and early-Universe constraints.

本文的动机是探索$f(Q, L_m)$引力作为标准$\Lambda$CDM模型的替代方案的可行性。通过考察该模型描述从减速膨胀到加速膨胀过渡的能力以及与各种观测数据集和早期宇宙约束的一致性来实现这一目标。

Method: The method involves a comprehensive analysis using a Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) approach to test the $f(Q, L_m)$ gravity model against a combined set of observational data, including DESI DR2 BAO, previous BAO measurements, cosmic chronometers (CC), and gravitational-wave (GW) standard sirens. Additionally, the Big Bang Nucleosynthesis (BBN) freeze-out constraint is incorporated to place stringent limits on the model parameters.

方法涉及使用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）方法对$f(Q, L_m)$引力模型进行全面分析，结合观测数据集进行测试，包括DESI DR2 BAO、之前的BAO测量、宇宙计时器（CC）和引力波（GW）标准警报。此外，还结合了大爆炸核合成（BBN）冻结约束，对模型参数施加严格的限制。

Result: The results show that the $f(Q, L_m)$ gravity model successfully describes the transition from decelerated to accelerated expansion and is consistent with observational data. The effective equation-of-state parameter, statefinder diagnostics, and energy conditions reveal a quintessence-like nature, confirming the physical viability of the model. The constraints on the model parameters are stringent and consistent with early-Universe physics.

结果表明，$f(Q, L_m)$引力模型成功地描述了从减速膨胀到加速膨胀的过渡，并且与观测数据一致。有效状态方程参数、状态发现诊断和能量条件揭示了类五次性质，确认了模型的物理可行性。对模型参数的限制是严格的，并且与早期宇宙物理学一致。

Conclusion: The $f(Q, L_m)$ gravity framework is presented as a viable alternative to the $\Lambda$CDM model, closely reproducing its predictions while allowing for controlled deviations in the expansion history. The model's consistency with observational data and early-Universe constraints, along with its quintessence-like behavior, supports its physical viability.

$f(Q, L_m)$引力框架被提出为$\Lambda$CDM模型的可行替代方案，紧密重现其预测的同时允许在膨胀历史中存在可控偏差。该模型与观测数据和早期宇宙约束的一致性，以及其类五次行为，支持了其物理可行性。

Abstract: We perform a comprehensive investigation of the early-to-late time cosmic evolution within the framework of $f(Q,L_m)$ gravity, characterized by a non-minimal coupling between non-metricity and matter. The model is further tested against a combined set of observational data, including DESI DR2 BAO, previous BAO measurements, cosmic chronometers (CC), and gravitational-wave (GW) standard sirens, using a Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) approach. Further by incorporating the Big Bang Nucleosynthesis (BBN) freeze-out constraint, we place stringent limits on the model parameters, ensuring consistency with early-Universe physics. The resulting constraints exhibit strong agreement with observations, with the model successfully describing the transition from decelerated to accelerated expansion. The evolution of the effective equation-of-state parameter, together with statefinder diagnostics and energy conditions, reveals a quintessence-like nature and confirms the physical viability of the model. Overall, the $f(Q,L_m)$ framework emerges as a viable alternative to $Λ$CDM, closely reproducing its predictions while allowing controlled deviations in the expansion history.

</details>

### [30] [Primordial black hole production in scalar field inflation within $f(T)$ gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24011)

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper investigates inflation in modified teleparallel gravity, focusing on power-law and exponential models. It uses a string-inspired fiber inflation potential to realize a transient ultra slow-roll (USR) phase, leading to an amplified primordial curvature power spectrum on small scales while remaining consistent with CMB constraints at large scales. The modified gravity sector introduces corrections to slow-roll parameters, tensor spectral index, and tensor-to-scalar ratio, providing distinct signatures from canonical inflation. The study also explores the implications for primordial black hole (PBH) formation.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore inflation within modified teleparallel gravity, specifically through viable extensions of the Teleparallel Equivalent of General Relativity. The aim is to understand how these modifications affect the inflationary dynamics and the resulting cosmological perturbations, particularly in the context of ultra slow-roll (USR) phases and primordial black hole (PBH) formation.

动机是探索在修正的远程平行引力框架下的膨胀，特别是通过远程平行等效于广义相对论的可行扩展。目的是理解这些修正如何影响膨胀动力学和由此产生的宇宙扰动，特别是在超慢滚（USR）阶段和原初黑洞（PBH）形成的情境中。

Method: The authors use a scalar-tensor framework to investigate two viable extensions of the Teleparallel Equivalent of General Relativity: a power-law model and an exponential model. They introduce a correction parameter $\alpha$ to control deviations from standard teleparallel gravity. Inflation is driven by a string-inspired fiber inflation potential that naturally realizes a USR phase. The background equations are solved numerically, and the evolution of cosmological perturbations is computed within the modified teleparallel framework.

作者使用标量-张量框架研究了远程平行等效于广义相对论的两个可行扩展：幂律模型和指数模型。他们引入了一个修正参数 $\alpha$ 来控制与标准远程平行引力的偏差。膨胀由一个弦理论启发的纤维膨胀势驱动，该势自然地实现了超慢滚（USR）阶段。背景方程通过数值方法求解，并在修正的远程平行框架内计算宇宙扰动的演化。

Result: The results show that both the power-law and exponential models generate an amplification of the primordial curvature power spectrum on small scales due to the USR phase, while remaining compatible with cosmic microwave background (CMB) constraints at large scales. The modified gravity sector introduces corrections to the slow-roll parameters, tensor spectral index, and tensor-to-scalar ratio, leading to potentially observable signatures distinct from canonical inflation. The enhanced scalar perturbations have implications for primordial black hole (PBH) formation.

结果表明，幂律模型和指数模型由于超慢滚（USR）阶段，在小尺度上产生了原始曲率功率谱的放大，同时在大尺度上仍然与宇宙微波背景（CMB）约束兼容。修正的引力部分对慢滚参数、张量谱指数和张量-标量比进行了修正，导致了与规范膨胀不同的潜在可观测特征。增强的标量扰动对原初黑洞（PBH）的形成有影响。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that modified teleparallel gravity, through its viable extensions, provides a theoretically consistent and phenomenologically rich framework for studying inflation. The USR phase leads to an amplification of the primordial curvature power spectrum on small scales, which can have significant implications for PBH formation. The distinct signatures in the slow-roll parameters, tensor spectral index, and tensor-to-scalar ratio offer a way to distinguish these models from canonical inflation.

论文得出结论，通过其可行的扩展，修正的远程平行引力为研究膨胀提供了一个理论上一致且现象丰富的方法。超慢滚（USR）阶段导致小尺度上的原始曲率功率谱放大，这对原初黑洞（PBH）的形成具有重要意义。慢滚参数、张量谱指数和张量-标量比中的不同特征提供了区分这些模型与规范膨胀的方法。

Abstract: We investigate inflation in modified teleparallel gravity within a scalar-tensor framework. We focus on two viable extensions of the Teleparallel Equivalent of General Relativity: a power-law model and an exponential model, which introduce controlled deviations from standard teleparallel gravity through a correction parameter $α$. Inflation is driven by a string-inspired fiber inflation potential that naturally realizes a transient ultra slow-roll (USR) phase. We solve the background equations numerically and compute the evolution of cosmological perturbations within the modified teleparallel framework. We show that both models generate an amplification of the primordial curvature power spectrum on small scales due to the USR phase, while remaining compatible with cosmic microwave background constraints at large scales. The modified gravity sector introduces corrections to the slow-roll parameters, tensor spectral index, and tensor-to-scalar ratio through derivatives of the torsion function, leading to potentially observable signatures distinct from canonical inflation. We further analyze the implications of enhanced scalar perturbations for primordial black hole (PBH) formation and demonstrate that modified teleparallel gravity provides a theoretically consistent and phenomenologically rich framework for producing PBHs during inflation.

### [31] [$g_{tt}g_{rr} =-1$ black hole thermodynamics in extended quasi-topological gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24101)
*Johanna Borissova*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper introduces a unified framework for the thermodynamics of $d$-dimensional static black holes with various topologies, using an integrable 2D effective dilaton theory. The framework allows for the computation of thermodynamic mass and Wald entropy, applicable to both singular and regular black holes with flat or AdS asymptotics.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to provide a general and unified approach to the study of black hole thermodynamics for $d$-dimensional static black holes with different horizon topologies, by considering them as solutions to an integrable 2D effective dilaton theory. This approach aims to generalize the first law of black hole thermodynamics and compute the entropy via the Wald formula.

动机是为$d$维静态黑洞的热力学研究提供一个通用和统一的方法，这些黑洞具有不同的视界拓扑。通过将这些黑洞视为可积的2维有效标量理论的解，该方法旨在推广黑洞热力学的第一定律，并通过Wald公式计算熵。

Method: The authors develop a unified framework based on an integrable 2-dimensional effective dilaton theory, which allows any $d$-dimensional static black hole with spherical, toroidal, or compact hyperbolic horizon topology to be treated as a vacuum solution in an extended notion of $d$-dimensional quasi-topological gravity. They show that the generating function determining $f(r) = -g_{tt}$ in the integrated equation of motion provides the thermodynamic mass, and the entropy is computed using the Wald entropy formula.

作者基于可积的2维有效标量理论开发了一个统一框架，这使得任何具有球形、环形或紧致双曲视界拓扑的$d$维静态黑洞都可以被视为扩展的$d$维准拓扑引力中的真空解。他们表明，在积分运动方程中决定$f(r) = -g_{tt}$的生成函数提供了热力学质量，并且熵通过Wald熵公式计算。

Result: The framework successfully unifies the thermodynamic treatment of black holes with different horizon topologies, providing a method to compute the thermodynamic mass and Wald entropy. It is applicable to both singular and regular black holes, and can handle flat or anti-de Sitter (AdS) asymptotics.

该框架成功地统一了不同视界拓扑的黑洞的热力学处理方法，提供了一种计算热力学质量和Wald熵的方法。它既适用于奇异黑洞也适用于规则黑洞，并且可以处理平坦或反德西特（AdS）渐近。

Conclusion: The paper presents a novel and unified framework for the thermodynamics of $d$-dimensional static black holes with various topologies, using an integrable 2D effective dilaton theory. This framework allows for the computation of thermodynamic mass and entropy, and is applicable to a wide range of black hole solutions, including those with flat or AdS asymptotics.

论文提出了一种新颖且统一的框架，用于处理各种拓扑结构的$d$维静态黑洞的热力学，该框架基于可积的2维有效标量理论。该框架允许计算热力学质量和熵，并适用于广泛的黑洞解，包括具有平坦或AdS渐近的黑洞。

Abstract: We present a unified framework for the discussion of black hole thermodynamics of $d$-dimensional static black holes with spherical, toroidal or compact hyperbolic horizon topology satisfying $g_{tt}g_{rr}=-1$ in Schwarzschild gauge. To that end, we consider any such black hole as a solution to an integrable $2$-dimensional effective dilaton theory and thereby as a vacuum solution to an extended notion of $d$-dimensional quasi-topological gravity. We show that the generating function determining $f(r) = -g_{tt} $ in the integrated equation of motion provides the thermodynamic mass in a generalised first law with entropy computed as the Wald entropy. The framework presented here can be applied to singular and regular black holes with flat or anti-de Sitter asymptotics.

### [32] [Photon Surfaces in Higher-Curvature Gravity: Implications for Quasinormal Modes and Gravitational Lensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24115)
*Takamasa Kanai*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper explores the effects of higher-curvature corrections in an EFT framework on quasinormal modes and gravitational lensing, showing that strong-field observables can probe EFT corrections and constrain couplings beyond general relativity.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to use effective field theory (EFT) to systematically describe deviations from general relativity through higher-curvature corrections. The goal is to understand how these corrections, which represent low-energy effects of an underlying fundamental theory, modify key observables such as the photon sphere radius, critical impact parameter, and coefficients governing the strong deflection expansion. This work aims to provide a sensitive probe of EFT corrections and potentially place constraints on EFT couplings beyond general relativity using precision measurements of gravitational lensing and QNM spectra.

动机是使用有效场论（EFT）系统地描述通过高曲率修正对广义相对论的偏离。目标是理解这些修正，即基础理论的低能效应，如何修改关键可观测量，如光子球半径、临界撞击参数和强偏折展开的系数。这项工作旨在提供一个对EFT修正的敏感探测，并可能通过引力透镜和准正规模谱的精确测量来约束超出广义相对论的EFT耦合。

Method: The method involves investigating quasinormal modes (QNMs) and both weak and strong gravitational lensing in static, spherically symmetric spacetimes. The authors adopt the strong deflection limit formalism developed by Bozza to derive the logarithmic divergence structure of the deflection angle and separate the divergent and regular contributions. They analyze the behavior of null geodesics near the photon sphere and examine how deviations from general relativity, parametrized in an EFT framework, affect key observables such as the photon sphere radius, critical impact parameter, and the coefficients governing the strong deflection expansion.

方法涉及在静态、球对称时空中的准正规模（QNMs）以及弱和强引力透镜的研究。作者采用Bozza开发的强偏折极限形式来推导偏折角的对数发散结构，并分离出发散和规则贡献。他们分析了光子球附近零测地线的行为，并研究了在EFT框架中参数化的广义相对论偏离如何影响关键可观测量，如光子球半径、临界撞击参数和强偏折展开的系数。

Result: The results show that the photon sphere radius, critical impact parameter, and the coefficients governing the strong deflection expansion are modified by the EFT corrections. These modifications encode direct information about the higher-curvature corrections to the gravitational action. The analysis demonstrates that strong-field observables, such as gravitational lensing and QNM spectra, provide a sensitive probe of EFT corrections and could be used to place constraints on EFT couplings beyond general relativity.

结果表明，光子球半径、临界撞击参数和强偏折展开的系数受到EFT修正的影响。这些修正直接编码了关于引力作用量的高曲率修正的信息。分析表明，强场可观测量，如引力透镜和准正规模谱，提供了对EFT修正的敏感探测，并可以用来约束超出广义相对论的EFT耦合。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that strong-field observables, such as gravitational lensing and QNM spectra, are sensitive probes of EFT corrections and can be used to place constraints on EFT couplings beyond general relativity. Precision measurements of these observables offer a novel observational window into quantum gravity-inspired effects, providing a potential avenue for testing the predictions of EFTs with higher-curvature corrections.

结论是，强场可观测量，如引力透镜和准正规模谱，是对EFT修正的敏感探测器，可以用来约束超出广义相对论的EFT耦合。这些可观测量的精确测量为观测量子引力启发效应提供了新的窗口，为测试具有高曲率修正的EFT预测提供了一条潜在途径。

Abstract: Effective field theory (EFT) provides a systematic framework to describe possible deviations from general relativity through higher-curvature corrections to the gravitational action, capturing low-energy effects of an underlying fundamental theory.
  In this work, we investigate quasinormal modes (QNMs) and both weak and strong gravitational lensing in static, spherically symmetric spacetimes, focusing on the behavior of null geodesics near the photon sphere. Adopting the strong deflection limit formalism developed by Bozza, we derive the logarithmic divergence structure of the deflection angle and explicitly separate the divergent and regular contributions.
  Within a simplified setup with $2M=1$, we analyze how deviations from general relativity, parametrized in an EFT framework, modify key observables such as the photon sphere radius, the critical impact parameter, and the coefficients governing the strong deflection expansion. We show that these quantities encode direct information about higher-curvature corrections to the gravitational action.
  Our results demonstrate that strong-field observables provide a sensitive probe of EFT corrections, and that precision measurements of gravitational lensing and QNM spectra could place constraints on EFT couplings beyond general relativity, offering a novel observational window into quantum gravity-inspired effects.

</details>


### [33] [BMS transformed Quantum String Dynamics near a Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24145)
*Nihar Ranjan Ghosh,Malay K. Nandy*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper examines the impact of BMS supertranslations on the dynamics of a closed bosonic string near the horizon of a five-dimensional Schwarzschild black hole. The analysis reveals that the angular sector of the worldsheet dynamics is particularly sensitive to these deformations, breaking the original SO(4) symmetry, while the radial and temporal sectors remain unaffected. The study provides a dynamical probe of BMS-induced deformations in higher-dimensional black hole spacetimes.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation for this work is to understand how asymptotic symmetries, specifically BMS supertranslations, affect the dynamics of quantum probes such as strings near the horizon of black holes. Asymptotic symmetries are believed to leave subtle but significant imprints on quantum gravity, and their effects on extended objects like strings can provide deeper insights into the near-horizon geometry and the underlying symmetry structures.

这项工作的动机是理解渐近对称性，特别是BMS超平移，如何影响黑洞视界附近的量子探针（如弦）的动力学。渐近对称性被认为在量子引力上留下了微妙但重要的印记，它们对扩展物体（如弦）的影响可以提供对视界附近几何结构和潜在对称结构的更深入的理解。

Method: The authors consider a closed bosonic string propagating in the near-horizon geometry of a five-dimensional Schwarzschild black hole. They apply a generalized BMS supertranslation to the background and analyze the resulting deformations. The method involves examining the worldsheet dynamics, focusing on the angular, temporal, and radial sectors. The angular sector is found to be most sensitive to the supertranslation, leading to anisotropic geometric distortions and breaking the original SO(4) symmetry. The radial equation is governed by modified Bessel modes, with a nonvanishing radial conserved current, indicating transport-like propagation.

作者考虑了一个封闭的玻色弦在五维Schwarzschild黑洞的近视界几何中传播。他们对背景应用广义BMS超平移，并分析由此产生的变形。该方法涉及检查世界面动力学，重点关注角、时间以及径向部分。发现角部分对超平移最为敏感，导致各向异性几何畸变并打破原始SO(4)对称性。径向方程由修正的贝塞尔模式控制，具有非零径向守恒流，表明类似于传输的传播。

Result: The key results include the observation that the angular sector of the worldsheet dynamics is significantly affected by the BMS supertranslation, leading to anisotropic geometric distortions and the breaking of the original SO(4) symmetry. The temporal and radial sectors remain unaffected. The radial equation is governed by modified Bessel modes, and there is a nonvanishing radial conserved current, indicating transport-like propagation. The study also demonstrates radial squeezing driven by gravity and anisotropic angular spreading induced by supertranslations, providing a dynamical realization of string spreading near the horizon.

主要结果包括观察到世界面动力学的角部分受到BMS超平移的显著影响，导致各向异性几何畸变并打破原始SO(4)对称性。时间部分和径向部分不受影响。径向方程由修正的贝塞尔模式控制，并且存在非零径向守恒流，表明类似于传输的传播。研究还展示了由引力驱动的径向挤压和由超平移引起的各向异性角扩散，提供了弦在视界附近扩散的动力学实现。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that the dynamics of a closed bosonic string near the horizon of a five-dimensional Schwarzschild black hole encodes nontrivial signatures of BMS-induced deformations. This provides a new dynamical probe of symmetry structures in higher-dimensional black hole spacetimes, offering a deeper understanding of the interplay between asymptotic symmetries and the near-horizon geometry of black holes.

论文得出结论，五维Schwarzschild黑洞视界附近的封闭玻色弦动力学编码了BMS诱导变形的非平凡特征。这为高维黑洞时空中的对称结构提供了一种新的动力学探测手段，有助于更深入地理解渐近对称性和黑洞视界几何之间的相互作用。

Abstract: Asymptotic symmetries are expected to leave subtle but physically meaningful imprints on quantum probes of gravity, yet their manifestation in near-horizon dynamics remains incompletely understood. We examine this question for a closed bosonic string propagating in the near-horizon geometry of a five-dimensional Schwarzschild black hole subjected to a generalized Bondi-van der Burg-Metzner-Sachs (BMS) supertranslation. The extended nature of the string makes it especially sensitive to the resulting anisotropic geometric distortions, and this sensitivity appears most clearly in the angular sector of the worldsheet dynamics. Under the gauge and falloff conditions adopted here, the temporal and radial sectors remain unaffected by the supertranslation, while the angular deformation breaks the original SO(4) symmetry of the background. The radial equation is governed by modified Bessel modes, with a nonvanishing radial conserved current, indicating transport-like propagation. Radial squeezing driven by gravity and anisotropic angular spreading induced by supertranslations provide a dynamical realization of string spreading near the horizon. Thus this analysis demonstrates that probe string dynamics encodes nontrivial signatures of BMS-induced deformations, providing a dynamical probe of symmetry structures in higher-dimensional black hole spacetimes.

方法是确定因果锥层次结构与围绕正能量种子的负能量引力云的屏蔽机制之间的联系。作者将这一想法应用于球对称物质分布，以说明他们的概念。

Abstract: In a previous paper by some of the authors (Gen. Rel. Grav. 56, 116, 2024), we introduced a novel paradigm with which to understand gravitational phenomena. We called it the Harmonic Background Paradigm (HBP). In this paradigm, gravity amounts to an effective causality deformation with respect to a more fundamental causality, which always encompasses the former through a causal cone hierarchy. In that paper, the fundamental idea was described in detail but fully elaborated only when restricted to the linear gravitational approximation. In this work, we discuss and conjecture how this idea could be extended to the full non-linear regime. We identify a connection between the cone hierarchy and a property of gravity that can be described as a screening mechanism of negative-energy gravitational clouds surrounding (but never overcoming) positive-energy seeds. We illustrate our ideas by applying them to spherically symmetric matter distributions. The paper concludes with a discussion of some key implications and directions for future research, including some remarks beyond General Relativity.

### [35] [Pre-localization of Massive Black Hole Binaries in the Millihertz Band](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24330)
*Xue-Ting Zhang,Jonathan Gair,Chris Messenger,Natalia Korsakova,Yi-Ming Hu,Hong-Yu Chen*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper presents a fast, normalizing flow-based inference pipeline for early-warning analysis of massive black hole binary (MBHB) signals in space-borne gravitational-wave (GW) detectors, achieving accurate parameter estimation and sky localization within a minute, suitable for rapid electromagnetic (EM) follow-up.

  <summary>Details</summary>

This is crucial for triggering EM follow-up observations of MBHBs, which are expected to produce both GW and EM counterparts. The goal is to enable the continuous tracking of MBHBs through joint GW and EM observations.

该研究的动机是开发一个低延迟、高吞吐量的数据分析管道，能够快速从空间引力波数据中提取可靠的源参数和天空定位。这对于触发大质量黑洞双星（MBHB）的电磁后续观测至关重要，因为这些系统预计会产生引力波和电磁对应体。目标是通过联合引力波和电磁观测实现对MBHB的连续跟踪。

Method: The method involves developing a fast, normalizing flow-based inference pipeline designed for early-warning analysis of MBHB signals in a TianQin-like configuration. It combines a learned embedding of the detector time series with a neural spline flow (NSF) to perform amortized Bayesian inference. This approach generates posterior samples for the main source parameters in about one minute per event.

方法涉及为天琴类似配置中的MBHB信号早期预警分析开发一个基于归一化流的快速推理管道。它将探测器时间序列的学习嵌入与神经样条流(NSF)结合起来，以执行摊销贝叶斯推断。这种方法大约每分钟生成一次主要源参数的后验样本。

Result: The results show that the pipeline achieves pre-merger sky localizations of order $\sim 20~\mathrm{deg}^2$ for a representative MBHB, recovers the same number of sky modes as a reference parallel-tempered Markov chain Monte Carlo (PTMCMC) analysis, and yields parameter uncertainties of comparable scale, all while operating within a practically useful pre-merger warning window. These results indicate that NSF-based inference can deliver accurate, near-real-time parameter estimation and sky localization for space-borne MBHB GW signals.

结果表明，对于一个典型的MBHB，该管道实现了约$\sim 20~\mathrm{deg}^2$的合并前天空定位，恢复了与参考并行温度马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛(PTMCMC)分析相同数量的天空模式，并产生了规模相当的参数不确定性，所有这些都在一个实际有用的合并前预警窗口内完成。这些结果表明，基于NSF的推断可以为空间引力波MBHB信号提供准确的近乎实时的参数估计和天空定位。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the NSF-based inference pipeline can provide accurate and timely parameter estimation and sky localization for space-borne MBHB GW signals, enabling rapid EM follow-up. This capability is essential for realizing the potential of joint GW and EM observations of MBHBs.

结论是，基于NSF的推断管道可以为太空中的MBHB引力波信号提供准确及时的参数估计和天空定位，从而实现快速的电磁后续观测。这一能力对于实现MBHB的联合引力波和电磁观测潜力至关重要。

Abstract: The space-borne gravitational-wave (GW) detectors will open a new mass and redshift regime, allowing us to observe massive black hole binaries (MBHBs) throughout the Universe. A subset of these systems is expected to produce electromagnetic (EM) counterparts, offering a unique opportunity to follow the continuous evolution of massive black holes through joint GW and EM observations. Realizing this potential, however, requires low-latency, high-throughput data-analysis pipelines that can extract reliable source parameters and sky localizations from space-borne data streams fast enough to trigger EM follow-up. In this work we develop a fast, normalising flow-based inference pipeline designed for early-warning analysis of MBHB signals in a TianQin-like configuration. Our method combines a learned embedding of the detector time series with a neural spline flow (NSF) to perform amortized Bayesian inference, producing posterior samples for the main source parameters in roughly one minute per event. For a representative MBHB whose merger occurs $\sim 15$ minutes after the end of the analyzed GW observation, the pipeline achieves pre-merger sky localizations of order $\sim 20~\mathrm{deg}^2$, recovers the same number of sky modes as a reference parallel-tempered Markov chain Monte Carlo (PTMCMC) analysis, and yields parameter uncertainties of comparable scale, while still operating within a practically useful pre-merger warning window. These results demonstrate that NSF-based inference can deliver accurate, near-real-time parameter estimation for space-borne MBHB GW signals, and that the resulting early-warning localizations are sufficiently precise to make rapid EM follow-up.

### [36] [Scalar, electromagnetic, and Dirac perturbations of a regular black hole supported by primordial dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24349)
*Bekir Can Lütfüoğlu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper investigates the impact of regularity on the quasinormal modes of a regular black hole supported by a phantom Dirac--Born--Infeld scalar, using the Padé-improved WKB method and time-domain Prony analysis. The results show that increased regularity shifts the spectrum towards smaller oscillation frequencies and damping rates, with a weak change in the quality factor, indicating a robust spin-dependent imprint on ringdown.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand how the regularity of a black hole, specifically one supported by a phantom Dirac--Born--Infeld (DBI) scalar, affects its quasinormal mode spectrum. This is important for characterizing the black hole's response to perturbations and for identifying signatures of the DBI regularity scale in the ringdown phase, which could be observed in gravitational wave signals.

Method: The authors use the Padé-improved WKB method to compute the quasinormal frequencies of massless scalar, electromagnetic, and Dirac perturbations of the black hole. Additionally, they perform a time-domain Prony analysis to check the accuracy of the fundamental mode for the scalar case. This combination of methods allows for a detailed and reliable computation of the quasinormal modes and their dependence on the regularity of the black hole.

Result: The results indicate that an increase in the regularity of the black hole leads to a shift in the quasinormal mode spectrum towards smaller oscillation frequencies and damping rates. The quality factor, which is a measure of the sharpness of the resonance, changes only weakly. These spectral shifts are found to be well above the estimated numerical uncertainty, suggesting that the DBI regularity scale has a significant and observable effect on the ringdown spectrum.

Conclusion: The study concludes that the regularity of the black hole, as characterized by the DBI regularity scale, leaves a robust and spin-dependent imprint on the quasinormal mode spectrum. This finding is important for interpreting future gravitational wave observations and for understanding the nature of black holes in theories beyond general relativity.

Abstract: We study massless scalar, electromagnetic, and Dirac perturbations of the exact asymptotically flat regular black hole supported by a phantom Dirac--Born--Infeld scalar. Using the Padé-improved WKB method, with a time-domain Prony check for the scalar fundamental mode, we compute representative quasinormal frequencies and find that larger regularity shifts the spectrum toward smaller oscillation frequencies and damping rates, whereas the quality factor changes only weakly. The spectral shifts remain well above the estimated numerical uncertainty, demonstrating that the DBI regularity scale leaves a robust spin-dependent imprint on ringdown.

### [37] [Gravitational waves of extreme-mass-ratio inspirals in a rotating black hole with Dehnen dark matter halo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24413)
*Kun Meng,Shao-Jun Zhang,Nan Yang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates the gravitational wave (GW) signatures of Extreme Mass Ratio Inspirals (EMRIs) in the backgrounds of a Kerr black hole and a rotating black hole with a Dehnen-type dark matter halo. The authors use the Teukolsky formalism to derive the perturbed equations, apply the Sasaki-Nakamura transformation, and compute the energy and angular momentum fluxes to study the orbital evolution. They find that the dark matter halo significantly alters the GW amplitude and phase, and the mismatch between the waveforms increases with the DM halo mass and the spin of the supermassive black hole.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation for this work is to explore how the presence of a Dehnen-type dark matter halo around a rotating supermassive black hole affects the gravitational wave (GW) signatures of Extreme Mass Ratio Inspirals (EMRIs). EMRIs are important sources for space-based GW detectors, and their waveforms can provide insights into the nature of the central supermassive black hole and the background spacetime. By comparing the waveforms in the presence and absence of a dark matter halo, the authors aim to understand the detectability and potential astrophysical implications of such systems.

这项工作的动机是探索Dehnen型暗物质晕围绕旋转超大质量黑洞存在时，对极端质量比旋进（EMRIs）的引力波（GW）特征的影响。EMRIs是空间引力波探测器的重要来源，它们的波形可以提供关于中心超大质量黑洞和背景时空性质的见解。通过比较有无暗物质晕的波形，作者旨在理解这类系统的可探测性和潜在天体物理意义。

Method: The authors employ the Teukolsky formalism to derive the perturbed equations for the curvature tensor from the Newman-Penrose (NP) equations. For the rotating black hole with a Dehnen-type dark matter halo (DMBH), they obtain the radial and angular equations through separation of variables. To solve these equations numerically, they apply the Sasaki-Nakamura (SN) transformation to convert the Teukolsky-type equation into the SN equation. They then compute the energy flux and angular momentum flux at infinity and at the horizon to study the radiation reaction of GWs. The orbital evolution is derived from the total fluxes, and the two polarizations of GWs are extracted by solving the equations numerically.

作者使用Teukolsky形式主义从Newman-Penrose（NP）方程中推导出曲率张量的扰动方程。对于具有Dehnen型暗物质晕的旋转黑洞（DMBH），他们通过分离变量得到径向和角向方程。为了数值求解这些方程，他们应用Sasaki-Nakamura（SN）变换将Teukolsky型方程转换为SN方程。然后，他们计算无穷远处和视界处的能量通量和角动量通量，以研究引力波的辐射反作用。轨道演化由总通量导出，并通过数值求解方程提取引力波的两种极化。

Result: The results show that the presence of a Dehnen-type dark matter halo significantly alters the gravitational wave (GW) signatures of EMRIs. Specifically, the dark matter halo induces noticeable changes in both the amplitude and phase of the GWs. The authors compute the strain of the GW detector using the response function and evaluate the mismatch between the waveforms of the Kerr black hole and the DMBH. The mismatch increases with the mass parameter of the DM halo and the spin of the supermassive black hole.

结果表明，Dehnen型暗物质晕的存在显著改变了EMRIs的引力波（GW）特征。具体来说，暗物质晕在GW的振幅和相位上都引起了明显的变化。作者使用响应函数计算了引力波探测器的应变，并评估了Kerr黑洞和DMBH波形之间的不匹配。不匹配随着暗物质晕的质量参数和超大质量黑洞的自旋增加。

Conclusion: The study concludes that the presence of a Dehnen-type dark matter halo around a rotating supermassive black hole has a significant impact on the gravitational wave (GW) signatures of EMRIs. The changes in the GW amplitude and phase, as well as the increasing mismatch with the DM halo mass and the spin of the supermassive black hole, suggest that the detection and analysis of EMRI waveforms could provide valuable information about the properties of the central supermassive black hole and the surrounding dark matter distribution.

研究表明，旋转超大质量黑洞周围存在Dehnen型暗物质晕对EMRIs的引力波（GW）特征有显著影响。GW振幅和相位的变化，以及随着暗物质晕质量和超大质量黑洞自旋增加的不匹配，表明EMRI波形的探测和分析可以提供关于中心超大质量黑洞及其周围暗物质分布特性的有价值信息。

Abstract: Extreme Mass Ratio Inspirals (EMRIs) are among the key targe sources for the space-based gravitational wave (GW) detectors. The waveforms of the EMRIs are highly sensitive to the types of the central supermassive black hole (SBH) and can serve as a novel sensitive tool to probe the background spacetime. In this work, we compute GWs radiated from EMRIs in the backgrounds of Kerr black hole and rotating black hole with Dehnen-type dark matter halo (DMBH). Following the Teukolsky prescription, we obtain the perturbed equations for curvature tensor from the Newman-Penrose (NP) equations, and for the DMBH we obtain the radial and angular equations through separation of variables. To solve the equations with numerical method we apply the Sasaki-Nakamura (SN) transformation to convert the Teykolsky-type equation into the SN equation. We study the radiation reaction of GWs by computing the energy flux and angular momentum flux at infinity and at the horizon. The orbital evolution is then derived from the total fluxes. We extract the two polarizations of GWs by solving the equation numerically. By comparing the waveforms of Kerr and DMBH, it is found that the DM halo induces noticeable changes in both the amplitude and phase of GWs. We compute the strain of GW detector with the response function and evaluate the mismatch between the waveforms of Kerr and DMBH. The results show that the mismatch increases with the mass parameter of DM halo and the spin of the SBH.

### [39] [Tests of scalar polarizations with multi-messenger events](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24526)
*Sk Md Adil Imam,Macarena Lagos*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper tests General Relativity (GR) using gravitational wave (GW) data from GW170817, incorporating polarization angle constraints from the gamma-ray burst afterglow. The analysis uses the parameterized post-Einsteinian (PPE) framework, introducing three non-GR parameters to extend the GR waveform. Bayesian inference is performed for both quadrupole and dipole angular harmonics, with the EM constraint on the polarization angle providing tight bounds on non-GR parameters, particularly for the $\ell = |m| = 2$ case. [English Text]\n\n这篇论文使用GW170817的引力波数据，结合伽马射线暴余辉的偏振角约束，通过参数化后爱因斯坦框架（PPE）来测试广义相对论（GR）。分析中引入了三个非GR参数以扩展GR波形，并对四极和偶极角谐波进行了贝叶斯推断。电磁约束下的偏振角对非GR参数提供了非常严格的限制，特别是在$\ell = |m| = 2$的情况下。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this work is to test the predictions of General Relativity (GR) in the strong-field regime using gravitational wave (GW) observations. While GR predicts only two tensor polarization modes, other metric theories can predict up to six independent modes. This study aims to use the parameterized post-Einsteinian (PPE) framework to incorporate additional scalar and tensor mode modifications, alongside electromagnetic (EM) counterpart information, to test the consistency of GR with observational data. [English Text]\n\n本研究的动机是利用引力波观测在强场区域检验广义相对论（GR）的预测。虽然GR仅预测了两种张量偏振模式，但其他度规理论可以预测多达六种独立模式。本研究旨在使用参数化后爱因斯坦框架（PPE），结合额外的标量和张量模式修正以及电磁对应体信息，来检验GR与观测数据的一致性。

Method: The method employed in this paper involves the use of the parameterized post-Einsteinian (PPE) framework to extend the GR waveform by adding a scalar breathing mode and modifications to the tensor modes. Three non-GR parameters are introduced to account for these modifications. Bayesian inference is then used to analyze the data for both quadrupole ($\ell = |m|= 2$) and dipole ($\ell = |m|= 1$) angular harmonics, with two different frequency evolution models. Additionally, the EM constraint on the polarization angle from the gamma-ray burst afterglow is incorporated into the analysis. [English Text]\n\n本文采用的方法是使用参数化后爱因斯坦框架（PPE）通过添加一个标量呼吸模式和对张量模式的修正来扩展GR波形。引入了三个非GR参数来解释这些修正。然后使用贝叶斯推断分析四极（$\ell = |m|= 2$）和偶极（$\ell = |m|= 1$）角谐波的数据，考虑了两种不同的频率演化模型。此外，还结合了伽马射线暴余辉提供的偏振角的电磁约束进行分析。

Result: For the quadrupole ($\ell = |m|= 2$) angular harmonic, there is a mild preference for a scalar mode, with the scalar amplitude deviating from zero at approximately $2 \sigma$. In contrast, for the dipole ($\ell = |m|= 1$) angular harmonic, no preference for a scalar mode is found. The inclusion of the EM constraint on the polarization angle results in very tight bounds on the non-GR parameters, improving the bound on the scalar (tensor) amplitude modification parameter by roughly $60\%$ ($30\%$) for the $\ell = |m| = 2$ case. [English Text]\n\n对于四极（$\ell = |m|= 2$）角谐波，发现对标量模式有轻微偏好，标量幅度偏离零大约为$2 \sigma$。相比之下，对于偶极（$\ell = |m|= 1$）角谐波，没有发现对标量模式的偏好。加入偏振角的电磁约束对非GR参数提供了非常严格的限制，在$\ell = |m| = 2$的情况下，标量（张量）幅度修正参数的界限提高了约$60\%$（$30\%$）。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that the parameterized post-Einsteinian (PPE) framework, when applied to GW170817 along with EM counterpart information, can provide stringent tests of GR. The results show a mild preference for a scalar mode in the $\ell = |m| = 2$ case but no preference in the $\ell = |m| = 1$ case. The EM constraint on the polarization angle significantly improves the bounds on non-GR parameters, emphasizing the importance of long-term follow-up of GW events for testing gravity. [English Text]\n\n研究表明，当应用于GW170817并结合电磁对应体信息时，参数化后爱因斯坦框架（PPE）能够对GR提供严格的检验。结果表明，在$\ell = |m| = 2$的情况下对标量模式有轻微偏好，而在$\ell = |m| = 1$的情况下则没有偏好。偏振角的电磁约束显著提高了对非GR参数的限制，强调了对引力波事件长期跟踪在检验引力理论中的重要性。

Abstract: Gravitational wave (GW) observations provide a unique opportunity to test Einstein's General Relativity (GR) in the strong-field regime. While GR predicts only two tensor polarization modes, generic metric theories allow up to six independent modes. We perform a parameterized test of GR using the parameterized post-Einsteinian (PPE) framework applied to GW170817, incorporating for the first time the polarization angle constraints from the gamma-ray burst afterglow alongside other electromagnetic (EM) counterpart information. We extend the GR waveform by adding a scalar breathing mode and modifications to the tensor modes, introducing three non-GR parameters. We perform Bayesian inference for both quadrupole $\ell = |m|= 2$ and dipole $\ell = |m|= 1$ angular harmonics, with two frequency evolution models. For $\ell = |m|= 2$ , we find mild preference for a scalar mode (scalar amplitude deviates from zero at $\sim 2 σ$), while for the $\ell = |m|= 1$, we find no preference for a scalar mode. The EM constraint on the polarization angle places very tight bounds on non-GR parameters; for instance, in the case $\ell = |m| = 2$, the bound on the scalar (tensor) amplitude modification parameter improves by roughly $60\%$ $(30\%)$, highlighting the impact that long-term follow up of GW events can have on tests of gravity.

### [40] [Pair-Dependent Drift of Kerr Neighboring-Overtone Gap Minima](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24584)
*Yuye Wu,Hong-Bo Jin*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper investigates the complex-frequency gap between adjacent quasinormal modes (QNMs) of Kerr black holes, revealing robust interior minima whose locations drift with spin. The authors reformulate the problem as a local zero-setting for the complex separation, providing a geometric picture and a real-projection diagnostic to explain the drift.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the behavior of quasinormal modes (QNMs) in the context of black-hole ringdown, particularly focusing on the complex-frequency gap between adjacent overtones. The study aims to track these gaps along a spin scan and explore the dynamics of their minima, which can provide insights into the structure and evolution of black-hole perturbations.\n\n动机是理解准正态模式（QNMs）在黑洞振铃背景下的行为，特别是关注相邻泛音之间的复频间隙。研究旨在沿着自旋扫描跟踪这些间隙，并探索其最小值的动态，这可以为黑洞扰动的结构和演化提供见解。

Method: The authors continuously track Kerr overtones along a spin scan and analyze the complex-frequency gap between adjacent overtones. They reformulate the minimum setting as a local zero-setting problem for the complex separation between the two modes. A real-projection diagnostic is derived by differentiating the squared gap, which helps in understanding the drift of the minima. This approach provides a geometric picture of the radial turning event of the separation vector and the angular motion in the complex plane.\n\n作者沿着自旋扫描连续跟踪Kerr泛音，并分析相邻泛音之间的复频间隙。他们将最小值设置重新表述为两个模式之间复分离的局部零点设置问题。通过微分平方间隙导出一个实投影诊断，有助于理解最小值的漂移。这种方法提供了分离向量径向转向事件和复平面上角运动的几何图像。

Result: The analysis reveals robust interior minima in the complex-frequency gap between adjacent overtones, whose spin locations drift from pair to pair, even within the same \((s,\\ell,m)\) sector. The real-projection diagnostic explains the drift as the movement of the dominant zero crossing. The geometric picture shows that the minimum corresponds to a local radial turning event, while angular motion may persist.\n\n分析揭示了相邻泛音之间的复频间隙中存在稳健的内部最小值，其自旋位置从一对到另一对漂移，即使在相同的\((s,\\ell,m)\)扇区也是如此。实投影诊断解释了这种漂移为主导零交叉的移动。几何图像显示，最小值对应于局部径向转向事件，而角运动可能持续存在。

Conclusion: The study provides a deeper understanding of the behavior of quasinormal modes in the complex-frequency plane, particularly the drift of the minima in the gap between adjacent overtones. The local zero-setting problem and the real-projection diagnostic offer a new perspective on the dynamics of these modes, and the geometric picture aids in visualizing the radial and angular components of the separation vector. These findings are supported by an expanded but deliberately restricted representative set, indicating that the local picture is consistent for the cases examined.\n\n该研究提供了对复频平面上准正态模式行为的更深入理解，特别是相邻泛音间隙中的最小值漂移。局部零点设置问题和实投影诊断为这些模式的动力学提供了新的视角，几何图像有助于可视化分离向量的径向和角分量。这些发现得到了扩展但故意限制的代表性集合的支持，表明局部图像与所检查的情况一致。

Abstract: Quasinormal modes (QNMs) underpin black-hole ringdown modeling and spectroscopy, where higher overtones can contribute at early times and neighboring modes can become locally organized in the complex-frequency plane. Motivated by this, we continuously track Kerr overtones along a spin scan and study a raw neighboring-overtone quantity: the complex-frequency gap between adjacent overtones. We find robust interior minima whose spin locations drift from pair to pair, even within the same \((s,\ell,m)\) sector. We explain this by reformulating minimum setting as a local zero-setting problem for the complex separation between the two modes. Differentiating the squared gap yields a denominator-free real-projection diagnostic (the real part of the product between the complex separation, with conjugation, and its spin derivative). The sampled minimum is governed by an approximate local zero of this diagnostic, so minimum drift becomes the drift of its dominant zero crossing. This also yields a geometric picture: the minimum is a local radial turning event of the separation vector, while angular motion in the complex plane may persist. Finally, an expanded but deliberately restricted representative set (including same-family continuations, external positive transfers, and smooth no-trigger controls) supports this local picture for the triggered cases examined here. At the same time, the detailed local crossing environment remains intrinsically pair dependent.

### [41] [Hawking Temperature, Sparsity and Energy Emission Rate of Dark Matter Halo Regular Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24659)
*Faizuddin Ahmed,Edilberto O. Silva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper explores the thermodynamic and radiative properties of a black hole influenced by a dark matter halo with an Einasto density profile. It finds that the presence of the dark matter halo reduces the Hawking temperature and energy emission rate, while allowing for a thermodynamically stable phase with positive specific heat capacity. The sparsity parameter is also increased, indicating more intermittent Hawking radiation.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to examine how the presence of a dark matter halo, described by the Einasto density profile, affects the thermodynamic and radiative properties of a regular black hole. This investigation aims to provide a deeper understanding of the interaction between dark matter and black holes, which could have implications for astrophysical observations and theoretical models.

本文的动机是研究由Einasto密度分布描述的暗物质晕如何影响普通黑洞的热力学和辐射性质。这项研究旨在更深入地了解暗物质与黑洞之间的相互作用，这对天文观测和理论模型都有潜在的影响。

Method: The authors derive closed-form expressions for key thermodynamic and radiative quantities, including the Hawking temperature $T_H$, specific heat capacity $C$, sparsity parameter of Hawking flux, and spectral energy emission rate. These expressions are then analyzed as functions of the characteristic scale parameter $\alpha$ of the dark matter distribution. The results are compared with those of a standard Schwarzschild black hole to highlight the differences caused by the dark matter halo.

作者推导了关键热力学和辐射量的封闭形式表达式，包括霍金温度 $T_H$、比热容 $C$、霍金通量稀疏参数以及光谱能量发射率。然后将这些表达式作为暗物质分布特征尺度参数 $\alpha$ 的函数进行分析。结果与标准史瓦西黑洞的结果进行了比较，以突出暗物质晕引起的差异。

Result: The presence of a dark matter halo around the black hole leads to a suppression of both the Hawking temperature and the energy emission rate compared to the standard Schwarzschild case. The specific heat capacity can be positive for a certain range of horizon radii, indicating a thermodynamically stable phase. The boundary of this stable region marks a Davies-type phase transition. Additionally, the sparsity parameter is found to be higher, suggesting that the Hawking flux is more intermittent in the presence of the dark matter environment.

黑洞周围的暗物质晕导致霍金温度和能量发射率相对于标准史瓦西情况有所降低。在一定范围内的视界半径内，比热容可以为正，表明存在一个热力学稳定相。这个稳定区域的边界标志着Davies型相变。此外，还发现稀疏参数更高，表明在暗物质环境中霍金通量更加间歇。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that the dark matter halo, characterized by the Einasto density profile, significantly alters the thermodynamic and radiative behavior of a black hole. The findings suggest that the presence of dark matter can lead to a more stable black hole configuration, with reduced Hawking radiation and more intermittent emission patterns. This work provides new insights into the interplay between dark matter and black hole physics, potentially impacting future observational and theoretical studies.

研究表明，具有Einasto密度分布特征的暗物质晕显著改变了黑洞的热力学和辐射行为。研究结果表明，暗物质的存在可以使黑洞构型更加稳定，减少霍金辐射并使其发射模式更加间歇。这项工作为暗物质与黑洞物理之间的相互作用提供了新的见解，可能对未来观测和理论研究产生影响。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the thermodynamic and radiative properties of a regular black hole sourced by a dark matter halo described by the Einasto density profile. The closed-form expressions for the Hawking temperature, specific heat capacity, sparsity parameter of Hawking flux, and the spectral energy emission rate were obtained. All these are examined as a function of the characteristic scale parameter $α$ of the dark matter distribution and compared with the standard Schwarzschild results. We show that the presence of a dark matter halo suppresses both the Hawking temperature and energy emission rate relative to the standard black hole result. Crucially, the specific heat capacity can be positive for a finite range of horizon radii, signaling a thermodynamically stable phase; the boundary of this stable region defines a Davies-type phase transition. The sparsity parameter is higher than in the standard black hole, indicating that the dark matter environment makes the Hawking flux even more intermittent.

</details>

### [42] [Physics-Informed Neural Networks for Solving Two-Flavor Neutrino Oscillations in Vacuum and Matter Environments for Atmospheric and Reactor Neutrinos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22862)
*Srinivasan T.,Kalyani Desikan*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper explores the use of Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs) to solve the differential equations governing neutrino oscillations in vacuum and matter, demonstrating high precision and potential advantages over traditional solvers.\n\n本文探讨了使用物理信息神经网络（PINNs）来解决真空和物质中中微子振荡的微分方程，展示了高精度和相对于传统求解器的潜在优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation for this work is to explore the application of Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs) to the problem of neutrino oscillations, which are fundamental in particle physics. The aim is to develop a more efficient and flexible computational tool for solving the differential equations that describe the evolution of neutrinos, especially in complex environments where traditional methods may be limited.\n\n这项工作的动机是探索物理信息神经网络（PINNs）在中微子振荡问题中的应用，这是粒子物理学中的基本问题。目标是开发一种更高效和灵活的计算工具，用于解决描述中微子演化的微分方程，特别是在传统方法可能受到限制的复杂环境中。

Method: The method involves the use of Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs) to solve the differential equations that govern the evolution of neutrinos in vacuum and matter. The theoretical framework includes vacuum mixing and the Mikheyev-Smirnov-Wolfenstein (MSW) effect. PINNs are implemented for both vacuum and constant-density profiles, and the results are compared with analytical solutions to assess the precision of the method.\n\n该方法涉及使用物理信息神经网络（PINNs）来解决控制真空和物质中中微子演化的微分方程。理论框架包括真空混合和Mikheyev-Smirnov-Wolfenstein (MSW) 效应。对于真空和恒定密度剖面都实现了PINNs，并将结果与解析解进行比较，以评估该方法的精度。

Result: The results show that PINNs can achieve high precision in solving the differential equations for neutrino evolution, with mean squared errors of the order of \(10^{-3}-10^{-4}\). This precision is comparable to that of analytical solutions, indicating that PINNs are a viable alternative to traditional solvers. The method is particularly advantageous in its ability to handle high-dimensional problems and complex geometries without the need for a mesh.\n\n结果显示，PINNs 在解决中微子演化的微分方程时可以达到很高的精度，均方误差为 \(10^{-3}-10^{-4}\) 的量级。这种精度与解析解相当，表明PINNs 是传统求解器的可行替代方案。该方法在处理高维问题和复杂几何形状方面特别具有优势，无需网格。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs) are a promising and highly accurate method for solving the differential equations governing neutrino evolution in both vacuum and matter. The approach shows significant potential advantages over traditional solvers, including no mesh requirements, high-dimensionality reduction, and applicability to complex geometries. Future work will extend this method to three-flavor effects.\n\n论文得出结论，物理信息神经网络（PINNs）是一种有前景且高度准确的方法，可以解决真空和物质中中微子演化的微分方程。该方法显示出比传统求解器显著的优势，包括无需网格要求、高维降维以及适用于复杂几何形状。未来的工作将把这种方法扩展到三味效应。

Abstract: Neutrino oscillations provide crucial insights into fundamental particle physics, with two-flavor approximations effectively describing reactor and atmospheric phenomena. This paper explores the use of Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs) to solve the governing differential equations for neutrino evolution in both vacuum and matter environments. We review the theoretical framework, including vacuum mixing and the Mikheyev-Smirnov-Wolfenstein (MSW) effect in matter, and demonstrate PINN implementations for vacuum and constant-density profiles. This Machine learning based approach for reactor (low-energy) and atmospheric (high-energy) neutrinos shows high precision similar to analytical solutions, with mean squared errors of the order of \(10^{-3}-10^{-4)\). Although this work focuses on solving the evolution equation in general cases, we discuss the significant potential advantages of PINNs over traditional solvers, without any mesh requirements, high-dimensionality reduction, and applicability to complex geometries, along with future extensions to three-flavor effects.
