### [44] [Amplitude-Based Analysis of QED Radiative Corrections to Electroproduction of $η$-Mesons on Protons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22943)
*Isabella Illari,Andrei Afanasev,William J. Briscoe,Victor L. Kashevarov,Axel Schmidt,Igor I. Strakovsky*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper presents a formalism for radiative correction calculations in exclusive $\eta$ electroproduction on the proton, using the EXCLURAD code and EtaMAID-2023 multipole amplitudes. The cross-section correction factor $\delta$ varies significantly across the resonance region, with a local maximum near $W \simeq 1.66$ GeV. The beam-spin asymmetry is also suppressed by 15-25% at the same kinematics. Numerical results are provided for a range of $Q^2$ and angles relevant to CLAS12 experiments at Jefferson Lab.

该论文提出了一个用于质子上独家$\eta$电产生辐射校正计算的形式主义，使用了EXCLURAD代码和EtaMAID-2023多极振幅。截面修正因子$\delta$在共振区域变化显著，在$W \simeq 1.66$ GeV附近有一个局部最大值。在同一运动学条件下，束流自旋不对称性也受到15-25%的抑制。提供了与Jefferson Lab的CLAS12实验相关的$Q^2$范围和全角度范围内的数值结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation for this work is to extend the treatment of radiative corrections from the pion channel to the $\eta$ channel, providing a more accurate description of the exclusive $\eta$ electroproduction process. This is important for understanding the underlying physics and for interpreting experimental data, particularly in the resonance region where significant variations in the cross-section correction factor $\delta$ are observed.

这项工作的动机是将辐射校正的处理从π介子通道扩展到$\eta$通道，从而更准确地描述独家$\eta$电产生的过程。这对于理解基础物理以及解释实验数据非常重要，特别是在共振区域，观察到截面修正因子$\delta$有显著的变化。

Method: The authors use the EXCLURAD code, which incorporates the EtaMAID-2023 multipole amplitudes, to perform the radiative correction calculations. The method involves evaluating the cross-section correction factor $\delta$ and the beam-spin asymmetry over a range of kinematic variables, including $Q^2$, $W$, and the angular distribution. The calculations are performed for the resonance region $W = 1.49$-$2.0$ GeV at $E_{\rm beam} = 6.535$ GeV, and numerical results are provided for a broader range of $Q^2$ and angles.

作者使用了包含EtaMAID-2023多极振幅的EXCLURAD代码来进行辐射校正计算。该方法涉及在包括$Q^2$、$W$和角分布在内的各种运动学变量范围内评估截面修正因子$\delta$和束流自旋不对称性。计算是在$E_{\rm beam} = 6.535$ GeV时的共振区域$W = 1.49$-$2.0$ GeV进行的，并提供了更广泛的$Q^2$和角度范围内的数值结果。

Result: The results show that the cross-section correction factor $\delta$ can vary by up to ${\sim}\,30\%$ across the resonance region, with a local maximum near $W \simeq 1.66$ GeV, driven by the $S_{11}(1535)$ and $S_{11}(1650)$ resonances. Additionally, the beam-spin asymmetry is suppressed by 15-25% at the same kinematics. The numerical results cover $Q^2 = 0.3$-$4.0$ GeV$^2$ and the full angular range, providing a comprehensive set of data for comparison with experimental measurements.

结果显示，截面修正因子$\delta$在共振区域内可以变化高达${\sim}\,30\%$，在$W \simeq 1.66$ GeV附近有一个局部最大值，这是由$S_{11}(1535)$和$S_{11}(1650)$共振驱动的。此外，在相同的运动学条件下，束流自旋不对称性被抑制了15-25%。数值结果覆盖了$Q^2 = 0.3$-$4.0$ GeV$^2$和全角度范围，为与实验测量进行比较提供了一整套数据。

Conclusion: The study provides a detailed framework for calculating radiative corrections in exclusive $\eta$ electroproduction, extending the existing formalism from the pion channel. The significant variation in the cross-section correction factor $\delta$ and the suppression of the beam-spin asymmetry highlight the importance of including radiative corrections in the analysis of experimental data. The numerical results will be useful for the interpretation of future CLAS12 experiments at Jefferson Lab.

该研究为独家$\eta$电产生的辐射校正计算提供了一个详细的框架，扩展了现有的π介子通道形式主义。截面修正因子$\delta$的显著变化和束流自旋不对称性的抑制突显了在实验数据分析中包含辐射校正的重要性。数值结果将有助于解释Jefferson Lab未来CLAS12实验的数据。

Abstract: A formalism for radiative correction calculations in exclusive $η$ electroproduction on the proton is presented, extending the treatment developed for the pion channel. The EXCLURAD code is used in the radiative correction procedure with EtaMAID-2023 multipole amplitudes. The cross-section correction factor $δ$ varies by up to ${\sim}\,30\%$ across the resonance region $W = 1.49$-$2.0$ GeV at $E_{\rm beam} = 6.535$ GeV, with a local maximum near $W \simeq 1.66$ GeV driven by the $S_{11}(1535)$ and $S_{11}(1650)$ resonances. The beam-spin asymmetry is suppressed by 15-25% at the same kinematics. Numerical results covering $Q^2 = 0.3$-$4.0$ GeV$^2$ and the full angular range are provided for kinematics relevant to CLAS12 experiments at Jefferson Lab.

</details>


### [45] [Light-front mass operator with dressed quarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22953)
*J. A. O. Marinho,J. P. B. C. de Melo,T. Frederico,W. de Paula*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper constructs an effective light-front mass-squared operator for quark-antiquark systems, incorporating quark dressing effects through a running quark mass. It derives the disconnected light-front resolvent and projects it onto a constituent-quark helicity basis to obtain an effective dressed mass-squared operator. The momentum dependence of the effective light-front quark self-energy is analyzed, and the framework is applied to study pion structure, showing significant infrared modifications while maintaining controlled ultraviolet behavior.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to incorporate nonperturbative QCD dynamics into light-front descriptions of hadrons by constructing an effective light-front mass-squared operator that accounts for quark dressing effects. This is achieved by using a Minkowski-space quark propagator constrained by lattice-QCD-inspired parametrization and deriving the disconnected light-front resolvent.

动机是通过构建一个考虑夸克着装效应的有效轻前质量平方算符，将非微扰QCD动力学纳入到强子的轻前描述中。这是通过使用受格点QCD启发参数化的闵可夫斯基空间夸克传播子并导出不连接的轻前预解式来实现的。

Method: The method involves starting from a Minkowski-space quark propagator with a lattice-QCD-inspired parametrization, then deriving the disconnected light-front resolvent using a generalized spectral representation of the quark propagator. The instantaneous contributions are separated out, and the resolvent is projected onto a constituent-quark helicity basis to obtain the effective dressed mass-squared operator. An effective light-front quark self-energy is introduced, and its momentum dependence is analyzed. The framework is applied to pion structure using light-front wave-function models.

方法包括从具有格点QCD启发参数化的闵可夫斯基空间夸克传播子开始，然后使用夸克传播子的广义谱表示导出不连接的轻前预解式。瞬时贡献被分离出来，并将预解式投影到组成夸克螺旋度基上以获得有效着装质量平方算符。引入了有效的轻前夸克自能，并分析了其动量依赖性。该框架使用轻前波函数模型应用于π介子结构的研究。

Result: The results show that the inclusion of quark dressing effects induces significant infrared modifications in the pion structure, while the ultraviolet behavior remains controlled. The framework allows for the computation of unpolarized transverse-momentum-dependent distributions, unpolarized parton distribution functions, and distribution amplitudes, providing a way to incorporate nonperturbative QCD dynamics into light-front descriptions of hadrons.

结果表明，包含夸克着装效应在π介子结构中引起了显著的红外修正，而紫外行为仍然可控。该框架允许计算非极化横向动量依赖分布、非极化部分子分布函数和分布幅度，为将非微扰QCD动力学纳入强子的轻前描述提供了一种方法。

Conclusion: The construction of an effective light-front mass-squared operator incorporating quark dressing effects provides a promising framework for including nonperturbative QCD dynamics in the description of hadron structure. This approach shows significant improvements in the infrared region while maintaining good control over the ultraviolet behavior, making it a valuable tool for future studies in light-front Hamiltonian approaches.

构建一个包含夸克着装效应的有效轻前质量平方算符为在强子结构描述中纳入非微扰QCD动力学提供了一个有前景的框架。这种方法在红外区域显示出显著改进，同时对紫外行为保持良好的控制，使其成为未来轻前哈密顿方法研究中的宝贵工具。

Abstract: We construct an effective light-front mass-squared operator for quark-antiquark systems that incorporates quark dressing effects through a running quark mass. Starting from a Minkowski-space quark propagator constrained by lattice-QCD-inspired parametrization, we derive the disconnected light-front resolvent for a light quark-antiquark system using a generalized spectral representation of an individual quark propagator separating out the instantaneous contributions. By projecting the resolvent onto a constituent-quark helicity basis, we obtain an effective dressed mass-squared operator suitable for light-front Hamiltonian approaches. We introduce an effective light-front quark self-energy and analyze its momentum dependence. As an application, we study pion structure using representative light-front wave-function models and compute unpolarized transverse-momentum-dependent distributions, unpolarized parton distribution functions and distribution amplitudes. Our results show that quark dressing induces sizable infrared modifications while preserving controlled ultraviolet behavior, providing a framework to incorporate nonperturbative QCD dynamics into light-front descriptions of hadrons.

</details>


### [46] [Mono-Z' Signatures in the B-L Supersymmetric Standard Model at the LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23038)
*Ali Cici,Shaaban Khalil,Stefano Moretti,Cem Salih Un*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper explores the B-L Supersymmetric Standard Model with Inverse Seesaw (BLSSM-IS), which extends the MSSM by adding a gauged B-L symmetry, right-handed neutrinos, and an extra neutral gauge boson Z'. The LHC searches constrain the Z' mass to be around 2.2 TeV. The study focuses on mono-Z' events from the production of a Z' boson and a singlet Higgs h', where h' decays into a pair of LSPs (neutralino or right-handed sneutrino) as DM candidates. The analysis aims to extract a signal for this process, independent of the DM nature, by examining leptonic decays of Z' and the missing transverse energy.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore the phenomenology of the B-L Supersymmetric Standard Model with Inverse Seesaw (BLSSM-IS) at the LHC, particularly focusing on the associated production of a Z' boson and a singlet Higgs h'. The study aims to identify a signal that is independent of the specific nature of the Dark Matter (DM) candidate, which can be either a neutralino or a right-handed sneutrino. This is important for understanding the constraints on the model and for potentially discovering new physics beyond the Standard Model.

动机是探索B-L超对称标准模型与逆跷跷板机制（BLSSM-IS）在LHC上的现象学，特别是关注Z'玻色子和单重希格斯h'的联合产生。研究旨在识别一个与暗物质（DM）候选者的具体性质无关的信号，该候选者可以是中性微子或右手中微子。这对于理解对该模型的约束以及可能发现超出标准模型的新物理非常重要。

Method: The method involves analyzing the kinematic distributions of the final-state leptons (electrons and muons) and the missing transverse energy in the context of the BLSSM-IS. The focus is on mono-Z' events, where a Z' boson is produced in association with a singlet Higgs h', and h' decays into a pair of Lightest Supersymmetric Particles (LSPs), which are either neutralinos or right-handed sneutrinos. The analysis aims to extract a signal that is independent of the nature of the DM candidate, thereby providing a robust test of the model.

方法涉及分析BLSSM-IS框架下的最终态轻子（电子和μ子）和缺失横向能量的动力学分布。重点是单Z'事件，其中Z'玻色子与单重希格斯h'联合产生，h'衰变为一对最轻超对称粒子（LSP），这些LSP可以是中性微子或右手中微子。分析旨在提取一个与暗物质候选者性质无关的信号，从而为模型提供一个稳健的检验。

Result: The result of the analysis shows that it is possible to extract a signal for the mono-Z' events in the BLSSM-IS, independent of the nature of the DM candidate. The kinematic distributions of the final-state leptons and the missing transverse energy provide a distinctive signature for this process. This allows for a more general search strategy for new physics, not limited by the specific properties of the DM candidate.

分析结果表明，在BLSSM-IS中可以提取出与暗物质候选者性质无关的单Z'事件信号。最终态轻子和缺失横向能量的动力学分布为此过程提供了独特的特征。这使得可以采用更通用的新物理搜索策略，而不受暗物质候选者特定属性的限制。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the analysis of mono-Z' events in the BLSSM-IS, focusing on leptonic decays and missing transverse energy, provides a viable method to search for new physics signals. This approach is independent of the specific nature of the DM candidate, making it a powerful tool for exploring the parameter space of the model and constraining its predictions.

结论是，在BLSSM-IS中对单Z'事件的分析，重点放在轻子衰变和缺失横向能量上，提供了一种可行的方法来搜索新物理信号。这种方法独立于暗物质候选者的具体性质，使其成为探索模型参数空间并约束其预测的强大工具。

Abstract: The B-L Supersymmetric Standard Model with Inverse Seesaw (BLSSM-IS) extends the Minimal Supersymmetric Standard Model (MSSM) by incorporating a gauged B-L symmetry, right-handed neutrinos and an additional neutral gauge boson Z'. Searches at the Large Hadron Collider (LHC) constrain the mass of this gauge boson to be as low as only ~ 2.2 TeV in the BLSSM-IS, owing to interference effects with the SM. In this framework, mono-Z' events can arise from the associated production of a Z' boson and a singlet Higgs boson h', where h' subsequently decays into missing energy carried by a pair of the Lightest Supersymmetric Particle (LSP) - either a neutralino or a right-handed sneutrino - which serves as a Dark Matter (DM) candidate. Focusing on leptonic decays of the Z' (electrons and muons), we analyse the kinematic distributions of the final-state leptons and the missing transverse energy in order to extract a signal for this process which is independent of the nature of the BLSSM-IS DM.

</details>


### [47] [$D\bar{D}^\ast$-$πJ/ψ$ scatterings of coupled channels for $Z_c(3900)$ channel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23078)
*Yukihiro Abe,Yasuhiro Yamaguchi,Atsushi Hosaka*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper performs a coupled channel analysis for $Z_c(3900)$, incorporating meson and quark exchanges. It finds that quark exchange at short distances, particularly for $D\bar D^*$-$J/\psi\pi$ transitions, is crucial for the scattering amplitudes, consistent with HALQCD lattice simulations.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to understand the nature of the $Z_c(3900)$ resonance through a coupled channel analysis in an effective model of hadrons and quarks. The authors aim to determine the contributions of different types of interactions, such as meson exchange and quark exchange, to the scattering amplitudes of the $Z_c(3900)$ channel.

本文的动机是通过在强子和夸克的有效模型中进行耦合通道分析来理解$Z_c(3900)$共振的本质。作者旨在确定不同类型相互作用（如介子交换和夸克交换）对$Z_c(3900)$通道散射振幅的贡献。

Method: The method used in this paper involves a coupled channel analysis for the $D \bar D^*$, $J/\psi\pi$, and related meson pairs in the $Z_c(3900)$ channel. The model includes meson exchange potentials (one pion and $D^{(*)}$ meson exchanges) and quark exchanges. The authors calculate the scattering amplitudes, focusing on the role of off-diagonal interactions by quark exchanges at short distances, especially for transitions between $D\bar D^*$ and $J/\psi\pi$.

本文采用的方法是对$Z_c(3900)$通道中的$D \bar D^*$、$J/\psi\pi$及相关介子对进行耦合通道分析。该模型包括介子交换势（单个π介子和$D^{(*)}$介子交换）和夸克交换。作者计算了散射振幅，特别关注短距离处夸克交换引起的非对角相互作用的作用，尤其是在$D\bar D^*$和$J/\psi\pi$之间的跃迁。

Result: The results show that the meson exchange potential is small, while the off-diagonal interactions by quark exchanges at short distances, particularly for transitions between $D\bar D^*$ and $J/\psi\pi$, are strong. These strong quark exchange interactions play a main role in the scattering amplitudes for the $Z_c(3900)$ channel, which is consistent with the results from the lattice simulations of the HALQCD group.

结果显示，介子交换势很小，而短距离处夸克交换引起的非对角相互作用，特别是在$D\bar D^*$和$J/\psi\pi$之间的跃迁，非常强。这些强烈的夸克交换相互作用在$Z_c(3900)$通道的散射振幅中起主要作用，这与HALQCD组的晶格模拟结果一致。

Conclusion: The conclusion of this paper is that the quark exchange interactions at short distances, particularly for transitions between $D\bar D^*$ and $J/\psi\pi$, play a dominant role in the scattering amplitudes for the $Z_c(3900)$ channel. This finding is consistent with the results from the HALQCD lattice simulations, providing a deeper understanding of the nature of the $Z_c(3900)$ resonance.

本文的结论是，在$Z_c(3900)$通道的散射振幅中，短距离处夸克交换相互作用，特别是在$D\bar D^*$和$J/\psi\pi$之间的跃迁，起主导作用。这一发现与HALQCD晶格模拟的结果一致，为理解$Z_c(3900)$共振的本质提供了更深入的认识。

Abstract: We perform coupled channel analysis for $D \bar D^*$, $J/ψπ$ and related meson pairs for the $Z_c(3900)$ channel in an effective model of hadrons and quarks. The model incorporates meson exchange potential such as one pion and $D^{(*)}$ meson exchanges, and quark exchanges. It turns out that the meson exchange potential is small, while the off-diagonal interactions by the quark exchanges at short distances, particularly for transitions between $D\bar D^*$-$J/ψπ$ are strong, which plays a main role for the scattering amplitudes for the $Z_c(3900)$ channel, in consistent with the results of the lattice simulations of the HALQCD group.

### [48] [Baryon enhancement in jets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23189)
*Antonio Ortiz,Robert Vertesi*

TL;DR: The study reports a baryon enhancement in high-$p_{\rm T}^{\rm ch,\, jet}$ jets in pp collisions at $\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV, which challenges the conventional interpretation of baryon enhancement in terms of medium expansion and quark recombination.

  <summary>Details</summary>

The study aims to challenge the current understanding of baryon enhancement, which is often linked to collective expansion and quark recombination in the medium.

Method: The method involves simulating pp collisions at $\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV with PYTHIA8, focusing on jets with $p_{\rm T}^{\rm ch,\, jet}>15$ GeV/$c$. The analysis examines the transition from quark-initiated to gluon-initiated jets as a function of jet multiplicity, to explain the observed baryon enhancement.

This finding challenges the traditional interpretation of baryon enhancement in terms of medium expansion and quark recombination.

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the baryon enhancement in pp collisions at high $p_{\rm T}^{\rm ch,\, jet}$ can be attributed to the transition from quark-initiated to gluon-initiated jets, rather than to the collective expansion of the medium and quark recombination, thus providing a new perspective on the underlying mechanism.

Abstract: The enhancement of the baryon production relative to mesons in small-collision systems is considered a breakthrough result of the Large Hadron Collider since a similar effect in heavy-ion collisions is understood by invoking the formation of the strongly-interacting quark--gluon plasma. In this letter, a baryon enhancement is reported for $p_{\rm T}^{\rm ch,\, jet}>15$\,GeV/$c$ jets produced in pp collisions at $\sqrt{s}=13$\,TeV simulated with PYTHIA8. The effect can be explained as a transition between quark-initiated jets (low jet multiplicities) to gluon-initiated jets (high jet multiplicities). The present result challenges the interpretation about the multiplicity dependence of the baryon enhancement in terms of collective expansion of the medium and quark recombination.

### [49] [Coupled-channel study of the three-body $DDK$ and $D^{*}D^{*}K$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23298)
*Hai-Peng Xie,Si-Yi Chen,Ning Li,Wei Chen*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper investigates the three-body $DDK$ system with quantum numbers $I(J^P) = \frac{1}{2}(0^-)$ using a coupled-channel framework. The interactions are described by the one-boson-exchange model and chiral effective theory, and the three-body problem is solved using the Gaussian expansion method. A deeply bound state is found in the $DDK$ system, and an additional shallow state may appear near the particle-dimer threshold. No clear resonance poles are identified.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to explore the dynamics of the three-body $DDK$ system with specific quantum numbers within a coupled-channel framework that includes both $DDK$ and $D^{*}D^{*}K$ configurations. The goal is to understand the nature of possible bound states and resonances in such systems, which can provide insights into few-body dynamics involving charmed mesons and kaons.\n\n本文的动机是探索具有特定量子数的三体$DDK$系统在耦合通道框架内的动力学，该框架包括$DDK$和$D^{*}D^{*}K$配置。目标是理解这种系统中可能的束缚态和共振态的性质，这可以为涉及粲介子和kaon的少体动力学提供见解。

Method: The method employed in this paper involves a coupled-channel framework that incorporates both $DDK$ and $D^{*}D^{*}K$ configurations. The $D^{(*)}D^{(*)}$ interactions are described using the one-boson-exchange model, constrained by heavy-quark symmetry and fitted to the pole positions of $X(3872)$, $T_{cc}^+$, and $Z_c(3900)$. The $D^{(*)}K$ interaction is derived from the chiral effective theory, motivated by the molecular interpretation of $D_{s0}^*(2317)$, and is further constrained by lattice-QCD results for the $DK$ scattering lengths. The three-body problem is solved using the Gaussian expansion method, and the complex scaling method is used to search for possible resonant states.\n\n本文采用的方法是一个耦合通道框架，该框架包括$DDK$和$D^{*}D^{*}K$配置。$D^{(*)}D^{(*)}$相互作用使用单玻色子交换模型描述，该模型受重夸克对称性的约束，并拟合到$X(3872)$、$T_{cc}^+$和$Z_c(3900)$的极点位置。$D^{(*)}K$相互作用源自手征有效理论，受到$D_{s0}^*(2317)$分子解释的启发，并进一步受到格点QCD对于$DK$散射长度结果的约束。三体问题通过高斯展开方法解决，并使用复标度方法寻找可能的共振态。

Result: The results show that the $DDK$ system supports a deeply bound state across a wide range of parameters. An additional shallow state may emerge near the particle-dimer ($D$-$DK$) threshold, depending on the long-range behavior of the $DK$ interaction. The deeply bound state has a compact three-body structure, while the shallow state exhibits features of a three-body halo configuration. No clear resonance poles are identified within the explored parameter region. Similar results are obtained for the $D^{*}D^{*}K$ system.\n\n结果显示，在广泛的参数范围内，$DDK$系统支持一个深束缚态。根据$DK$相互作用的长程行为，粒子-二聚体（$D$-$DK$）阈值附近可能出现一个浅束缚态。深束缚态具有紧凑的三体结构，而浅束缚态表现出三体晕构型的特征。在所探索的参数区域内没有发现明显的共振极点。对于$D^{*}D^{*}K$系统也得到了类似的结果。

Conclusion: The study concludes that the $DDK$ system supports a deeply bound state and potentially an additional shallow state, depending on the long-range behavior of the $DK$ interaction. The coupled-channel effects from $D^{*}D^{*}K$ are negligible. These findings contribute to the understanding of few-body dynamics in systems involving charmed mesons and kaons.\n\n研究得出结论，$DDK$系统支持一个深束缚态，并且根据$DK$相互作用的长程行为，可能存在一个额外的浅束缚态。来自$D^{*}D^{*}K$的耦合通道效应可以忽略不计。这些发现有助于理解涉及粲介子和kaon系统的少体动力学。

Abstract: We investigate the three-body $DDK$ system with quantum numbers $I(J^P) = \frac{1}{2}(0^-)$ within a coupled-channel framework that incorporates both $DDK$ and $D^{*}D^{*}K$ configurations. The $D^{(*)}D^{(*)}$ interactions are described using the one-boson-exchange model constrained by the heavy-quark symmetry and fitted to the pole positions of $X(3872)$, $T_{cc}^+$, and $Z_c(3900)$. The $D^{(*)}K$ interaction is from the chiral effective theory, motivated by the molecular interpretation of $D_{s0}^*(2317)$, and is further constrained by lattice-QCD results for the $DK$ scattering lengths. The resulting three-body problem is solved using the Gaussian expansion method, while the complex scaling method is employed to search for possible resonant states. We find that coupled-channel effects from $D^{*}D^{*}K$ are negligible, and the $DDK$ system supports a deeply bound state across a wide range of parameters. Depending on the long-range behavior of the $DK$ interaction, an additional shallow state may emerge near the particle-dimer ($D$-$DK$) threshold. The deeply bound state exhibits a compact three-body structure, whereas the shallow state displays characteristic features of a three-body halo configuration. No clear resonance poles are identified within the explored parameter region. Similar results are obtained for the $D^{*}D^{*}K$ system. These findings may provide new insight into few-body dynamics in systems involving charmed mesons and kaons.

### [51] [Some approximate renormalization group invariants for supersymmetric extensions of the Standard Model and the Yukawa unification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23329)
*Kirill Krylov,Daniil Rystsov,Konstantin Stepanyantz*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper constructs expressions for Yukawa couplings in supersymmetric extensions of the Standard Model, which are approximate renormalization group invariants. These invariants are used to analyze relations between Yukawa couplings at the unification scale and predict values for $\mbox{tg}\,β$ and $α(M_X)$. The authors suggest two possible relations and test them against experimental data. They find that adding exotic superfields can achieve Yukawa unification, suggesting a possible underlying $E_6$ gauge symmetry.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to construct expressions for Yukawa couplings in supersymmetric models that have small quantum corrections, making them nearly scale-independent. This allows for the analysis of possible relations between these couplings at the unification scale and predictions for $\mbox{tg}\,β$ and $α(M_X)$. The goal is to explore whether such relations are consistent with experimental data on elementary particle masses.

动机是构建在超对称模型中具有小量子修正的Yukawa耦合表达式，使其几乎与尺度无关。这使得可以在统一尺度上分析这些耦合之间的可能关系，并预测$\mbox{tg}\,β$和$α(M_X)$。目标是探索这些关系是否与基本粒子质量的实验数据一致。

Method: The authors construct expressions for Yukawa couplings that are approximate renormalization group invariants. Using these invariants, they analyze possible relations between the Yukawa couplings at the unification scale $M_X$ and make predictions for $\mbox{tg}\,β$ and $α(M_X)$. They then test two variants of these relations against experimental data on elementary particle masses. To achieve Yukawa unification, they add exotic superfields forming 3 representations $5+\bar{5}$ of the group $SU(5)$ to the MSSM field content.

作者构建了近似的重整化群不变量的Yukawa耦合表达式。利用这些不变量，他们分析了在统一尺度$M_X$上的Yukawa耦合之间的可能关系，并预测了$\mbox{tg}\,β$和$α(M_X)$。然后，他们将这两种关系的变体与基本粒子质量的实验数据进行了对比。为了实现Yukawa统一，他们在MSSM场内容中添加了形成$SU(5)$群的3个表示$5+\bar{5}$的奇异超场。

Result: The results show that the constructed expressions for Yukawa couplings are indeed approximate renormalization group invariants. Two variants of possible relations between the Yukawa couplings at the unification scale are suggested and tested. The addition of exotic superfields forming 3 representations $5+\bar{5}$ of the group $SU(5)$ to the MSSM field content can achieve Yukawa unification for the third and second generations. This suggests a possible underlying $E_6$ gauge symmetry.

结果表明，构建的Yukawa耦合表达式确实是近似的重整化群不变量。提出了两种可能的统一尺度下的Yukawa耦合关系并进行了测试。通过在MSSM场内容中添加形成$SU(5)$群的3个表示$5+\bar{5}$的奇异超场，可以实现第三代和第二代的Yukawa统一。这暗示了一个可能的基本$E_6$规范对称性。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that the proposed Yukawa coupling expressions are approximate renormalization group invariants and can be used to analyze possible relations between the couplings at the unification scale. The suggested relations, when tested against experimental data, show consistency. The addition of exotic superfields to the MSSM field content can achieve Yukawa unification, indicating a possible underlying $E_6$ gauge symmetry.

研究表明，提出的Yukawa耦合表达式是近似的重整化群不变量，可以用来分析统一尺度下的耦合关系。建议的关系在与实验数据进行比较时显示出一致性。在MSSM场内容中添加奇异超场可以实现Yukawa统一，这表明可能存在一个基本的$E_6$规范对称性。

Abstract: For supersymmetric extensions of the Standard Model we construct some expressions that include Yukawa couplings for the third and second generations and receive relatively small quantum corrections. This implies that they slightly depend on scale and are therefore approximate renormalization group invariants. Using these invariants we try to analyse possible relations between the Yukawa couplings at the unification scale $M_X$ as well as the predictions for values of $\mbox{tg}\,β$ and $α(M_X)$. In particular, we suggest two variants of such relations and investigate whether they agree with the experimental values of elementary particle masses. It is demonstrated that the Yukawa unification for the third and second generations consistent with them can be achieved by adding exotic superfields forming 3 representations $5+\bar{5}$ of the group $SU(5)$ to the MSSM field content. We argue that this may indicate the possible underlying $E_6$ gauge symmetry.

### [52] [Possible Evidence for Neutral Color-Singlet $q\bar q$ Quark Matter from High-Energy Pb-Emulsion Collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23473)
*Cheuk-Yin Wong*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The invariant mass spectrum of $e^+e^-$ pairs from Pb-emulsion collisions at 160 A GeV shows a complex structure, including a broad enhancement and several resonances. This is interpreted as evidence for neutral color-singlet $q\bar q$ quark matter in both deconfined and confined phases, with the 19 $\pm$1 MeV resonance supporting the hypothetical X17 particle. Theoretical estimates and experimental observations are in approximate agreement, suggesting the production of both QED(U(1))-confined and -deconfined quark matter.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to provide a coherent theoretical framework to explain the observed complex structure in the invariant mass spectrum of $e^+e^-$ pairs produced in high-energy Pb-emulsion collisions. The authors aim to interpret the broad enhancement and multiple resonances, particularly the 19 $\pm$1 MeV resonance, as signatures of neutral color-singlet $q\bar q$ quark matter in different phases, thereby providing support for the existence of the hypothetical X17 particle.

本文的动机是为在高能Pb-乳胶碰撞中产生的$e^+e^-$对不变质量谱中观察到的复杂结构提供一个连贯的理论框架。作者旨在解释宽增强和多个共振，特别是19 $\pm$1 MeV共振，作为不同相态下的中性单色$q\bar q$夸克物质的特征，从而支持假设的X17粒子的存在。

Method: The method involves analyzing the invariant mass spectrum of $e^+e^-$ pairs from Pb-emulsion collisions at 160 A GeV. The authors use a theoretical model to describe the broad enhancement and resonances in terms of neutral color-singlet $q\bar q$ quark matter in both deconfined and confined phases. They estimate the phase transition temperature $T_c$(QED) theoretically and compare it with the observed spectrum. The 3$\pm$1 MeV and 7$\pm$1 MeV resonances are associated with QED(U(1))-deconfined $d\bar d$ and $u\bar u$ Coulomb bound states, while the 19 $\pm$1 MeV resonance is linked to the QED(U(1))-confined isoscalar QED meson.

该方法涉及分析160 A GeV下Pb-乳胶碰撞产生的$e^+e^-$对的不变质量谱。作者使用理论模型来描述宽增强和共振，这些特征用处于解禁闭相和禁闭相的中性单色$q\bar q$夸克物质来解释。他们从理论上估计了QED相变温度$T_c$(QED)，并将其与观测到的谱进行比较。3$\pm$1 MeV和7$\pm$1 MeV共振与QED(U(1))解禁闭$d\bar d$和$u\bar u$库仑束缚态相关联，而19 $\pm$1 MeV共振则与QED(U(1))禁闭标量QED介子相关。

Result: The results show that the observed complex structure in the invariant mass spectrum can be coherently described by the presence of neutral color-singlet $q\bar q$ quark matter in both deconfined and confined phases. The broad enhancement is attributed to thermal annihilation of QED(U(1))-deconfined quarks and antiquarks into $e^+e^-$ pairs at the phase transition temperature $T_c$(QED), estimated to be 4.75 $\pm$ 1.2 MeV. The 3$\pm$1 MeV and 7$\pm$1 MeV resonances correspond to QED(U(1))-deconfined $d\bar d$ and $u\bar u$ Coulomb bound states, while the 19 $\pm$1 MeV resonance corresponds to the QED(U(1))-confined isoscalar QED meson. The agreement between the theoretical and experimental spectra suggests the production of both QED(U(1))-confined and -deconfined quark matter in these collisions.

结果表明，不变质量谱中的观察到的复杂结构可以通过解禁闭相和禁闭相中的中性单色$q\bar q$夸克物质的存在来连贯地描述。宽增强归因于QED(U(1))解禁闭夸克和反夸克在相变温度$T_c$(QED)下的热湮灭，估计该温度为4.75 $\pm$ 1.2 MeV。3$\pm$1 MeV和7$\pm$1 MeV共振对应于QED(U(1))解禁闭$d\bar d$和$u\bar u$库仑束缚态，而19 $\pm$1 MeV共振对应于QED(U(1))禁闭标量QED介子。理论谱和实验谱之间的吻合表明，在这些碰撞中可能产生了QED(U(1))禁闭和解禁闭夸克物质。

Conclusion: The conclusion of the paper is that the observed complex structure in the invariant mass spectrum of $e^+e^-$ pairs from Pb-emulsion collisions at 160 A GeV can be explained by the presence of neutral color-singlet $q\bar q$ quark matter in both deconfined and confined phases. The 19 $\pm$1 MeV resonance provides independent support for the hypothetical X17 particle. The authors propose further experiments to confirm or refute their findings.

论文的结论是，160 A GeV下Pb-乳胶碰撞产生的$e^+e^-$对不变质量谱中的观察到的复杂结构可以通过解禁闭相和禁闭相中的中性单色$q\bar q$夸克物质的存在来解释。19 $\pm$1 MeV共振为假设的X17粒子提供了独立的支持。作者建议进一步的实验来确认或反驳他们的发现。

Abstract: The invariant mass spectrum of $e^+e^-$ pairs produced in high-energy Pb-emulsion collisions at 160 A GeV at CERN SPS exhibits a complex structure of many resonances resting on top of a broad enhancement at invariant masses below 50 MeV, with the prominent resonance at 19 $\pm$1 MeV providing independent support for the hypothetical X17 particle. We show that this complex structure may be coherently described as signatures for the neutral color-singlet $q\bar q$ quark matter in both its deconfined and confined phases. That is, the broad enhancement may arise from thermal annihilation of QED(U(1))-deconfined quarks and antiquarks into $e^+e^-$ pairs at the phase transition temperature $T_c$(QED), theoretically estimated to be 4.75 $\pm$ 1.2 MeV from the transitional equilibrium condition. The observed 3$\pm$1 and 7$\pm$1 MeV resonances may correspond to the QED(U(1))-deconfined $d\bar d$ and $u\bar u$ Coulomb bound states near their quark rest masses, respectively, whereas the observed 19 $\pm$ 1 MeV resonance may correspond to the QED(U(1))-confined isoscalar QED meson. The approximate agreement between the theoretical and the experimental spectrum suggests that both QED(U(1))-confined and QED(U(1))-deconfined neutral color-singlet $q\bar q$ quark matter may have been produced in these high-energy Pb-emulsion collisions. We propose future experiments to confirm or refute these findings.

TL;DR: The paper reviews the QCD phase diagram at small chemical potentials and increasing temperature, identifying three distinct regimes: the hadron gas, the stringy fluid, and the quark-gluon plasma, each characterized by different symmetries, degrees of freedom, and N_c scaling.

Understanding these phases and their transitions is essential for a complete description of QCD matter.

Abstract: We review recent developments on the QCD phase diagram at small chemical potentials and increasing temperature. There are three regimes/phases in QCD which differ by symmetries, degrees of freedom and N_c scaling: the hadron gas below the chiral restoration temperature T_ch, the stringy fluid between T_ch and the deconfinement temperature T_d and the quark-gluon plasma above T_d.

Abstract: We study the kaon quasi-distribution amplitude (quasi-DA) and distribution amplitude (DA) within the large-momentum effective theory (LaMET) combined with the first-principles functional QCD. Using quark correlation functions and the kaon Bethe-Salpeter amplitude in the Euclidean space from the 2+1 flavour functional QCD [1] as inputs, we obtain the kaon quasi DA in the large longitudinal momentum region with the contour deformation method [2] in the complex plane of momentum. By performing $1/P_z^2$ and $1/P_z^4$ order extrapolations of the kaon quasi-DA for the choices of the maximal longitudinal momentum $P_z^{\max}\in[2,2.5]$ GeV, we obtain a single-peaked and asymmetric kaon DA with the uncertainties arising from the extrapolation interval and ansatz. Conclusion: The paper concludes that the proposed experimental setups offer a promising avenue for detecting long-range interactions mediated by ultralight bosons, with the potential to uncover new physics at previously unexplored length scales. The ability to probe these interactions with high sensitivity opens up new opportunities for fundamental physics research.

### [56] [Probing the electron Yukawa coupling via resonant Higgs boson production at FCC-ee via $e^+e^- \to H \to WW^*$ in lepton-plus-jets final states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24152)
*Apranik Fatehi,Reza Jafari Seyedabad,Amir Amiri,Kazem Azizi,David d'Enterria,Louis Portales,Michele Selvaggi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: A detailed simulation study of $s$-channel Higgs boson production in $e^+e^-$ collisions at $\sqrt{s}=125\,\\mathrm{GeV}$ at the FCC-ee is presented. The analysis aims to constrain the electron Yukawa coupling, $y_e$, by considering four different $WW^*$ final states. Using a multiclass gradient boosted decision tree and assuming specific experimental conditions, the study achieves a combined statistical significance of 2.0 standard deviations, leading to an upper limit on the coupling modifier $κ_e \\lesssim 1.35$ at 95% confidence level, providing the most stringent constraint on $y_e$ in simulation-based studies.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to explore the feasibility of constraining the electron Yukawa coupling, $y_e$, through the $s$-channel Higgs boson production in $e^+e^-$ collisions at the CERN Future Circular Collider (FCC-ee). By simulating the process $e^+e^- \\to H \\to WW^* \\to \\ell^\\pm ν + jj$ with various final states, the authors aim to set stringent limits on the electron Yukawa coupling, which is a fundamental parameter in the Standard Model of particle physics.\n\n本文的动机是通过在CERN未来环形对撞机（FCC-ee）上进行的$e^+e^-$碰撞中的$s$通道希格斯玻色子产生过程来探索约束电子Yukawa耦合$y_e$的可行性。通过模拟过程$e^+e^- \\to H \\to WW^* \\to \\ell^\\pm ν + jj$及其各种最终态，作者旨在对电子Yukawa耦合设置严格的限制，这是粒子物理学标准模型中的一个基本参数。

Method: The method involves a detailed simulation study of the $s$-channel Higgs boson production in $e^+e^-$ collisions at a center-of-mass energy of $\\sqrt{s}=125\\,\\mathrm{GeV}$. The authors consider four different $WW^*$ final states, including both on- and off-shell $W$ bosons decaying into dileptons or dijets. A multiclass gradient boosted decision tree is used to discriminate between signal and background events using a comprehensive set of kinematic and topological variables. The analysis assumes a monochromatized c.m. energy spread of 4.1 MeV, a resonant cross section of $σ_{e^+e^- \\to H} = 280\\,\\mathrm{ab}$, and an integrated luminosity of $10\\,\\mathrm{ab}^{-1}$.\n\n该方法涉及对中心质量能量为$\\sqrt{s}=125\\,\\mathrm{GeV}$的$e^+e^-$碰撞中$s$通道希格斯玻色子产生的详细模拟研究。作者考虑了四种不同的$WW^*$最终态，包括在壳和离壳$W$玻色子衰变为二轻子或二喷注。使用多类梯度提升决策树，利用一系列全面的运动学和拓扑变量来区分信号和背景事件。分析假设单色化的c.m.能量分布为4.1 MeV，共振截面为$σ_{e^+e^- \\to H} = 280\\,\\mathrm{ab}$，以及积分亮度为$10\\,\\mathrm{ab}^{-1}$。

Result: The analysis achieves a combined statistical significance of 2.0 standard deviations. This corresponds to an upper limit on the coupling modifier $κ_e = y_e/y_e^{\\rm SM} \\lesssim 1.35$ at 95% confidence level. This result provides the most stringent constraint on the electron Yukawa coupling achieved in simulation-based studies to date.\n\n分析达到了2.0标准偏差的综合统计显著性。这对应于在95%置信水平下，耦合修正因子$κ_e = y_e/y_e^{\\rm SM} \\lesssim 1.35$的上限。这一结果提供了迄今为止基于模拟研究中对电子Yukawa耦合最严格的限制。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates the potential of the FCC-ee to provide stringent constraints on the electron Yukawa coupling, $y_e$, through the $s$-channel Higgs boson production in $e^+e^-$ collisions. The results show that with the assumed experimental conditions, a 95% confidence level upper limit of $κ_e \\lesssim 1.35$ can be achieved, representing the most stringent constraint on the electron Yukawa coupling in simulation-based studies to date.\n\n研究表明，通过$e^+e^-$碰撞中的$s$通道希格斯玻色子产生过程，FCC-ee有可能对电子Yukawa耦合$y_e$提供严格的限制。结果显示，在假设的实验条件下，可以达到95%置信水平的上限$κ_e \\lesssim 1.35$，这是迄今为止基于模拟研究中对电子Yukawa耦合最严格的限制。

Abstract: We report a detailed simulation study of the search for $s$-channel Higgs boson production in $e^+e^-$ collisions at a center-of-mass (c.m.) energy of $\sqrt{s}=125\,\mathrm{GeV}$ at the CERN Future Circular Collider (FCC-ee), as a means to constrain the electron Yukawa coupling, $y_e$. The process of interest is $e^+e^-\to H\to WW^*\to \ell^\pmν+ jj$ with four different $WW^*$ final states considered, involving both on- and off-shell $W$ bosons decaying either into dileptons ($\ell^\pm = e^\pm$ and $μ^\pm$, including those from $τ^\pm$ decays) or into dijets ($jj$). Signal and background events are discriminated through a multiclass gradient boosted decision tree exploiting a comprehensive set of kinematic and topological variables across the four final-state categories. Assuming a monochromatized c.m. energy spread of 4.1 MeV, yielding a $σ_{e^+e^-\to H} = 280\,\mathrm{ab}$ resonant cross section, and an integrated luminosity of $10\,\mathrm{ab}^{-1}$, the analysis achieves a combined statistical significance of 2.0 standard deviations. This corresponds to an upper limit on the coupling modifier $κ_e = y_e/y_e^{\rm SM} \lesssim 1.35$ at 95\% confidence level, and provides the most stringent constraint on the electron Yukawa coupling achieved in simulation-based studies to date.

### [57] [Selected Topics in Quark-Hadron Physics: From Scalar Nonets to Topological Glueballs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24177)
*Chihiro Sasaki*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper reviews the classification and properties of low-lying scalar mesons and glueballs, proposes a new classification for the scalar nonet, and uses a topological soliton model to describe glueballs, which is consistent with lattice QCD and experimental data.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to provide a clearer understanding of the nature and classification of low-lying scalar mesons and glueballs, particularly by proposing a new classification for the scalar nonet and identifying $f_0(1500)$ as a primary glueball candidate. The paper aims to reconcile the production yields of these states in heavy-ion collisions across different theoretical frameworks and to offer a non-perturbative framework that can predict the properties of exotic scalar states, such as the anomalously long lifetime of $f_0(2470)$. 

本文旨在更清晰地理解低能标量介子和胶球的性质和分类，特别是通过提出一个新的标量非特态分类，并将$f_0(1500)$识别为主要胶球候选者。文章旨在调和这些状态在重离子碰撞中的产额在不同理论框架下的结果，并提供一个可以预测奇异标量态性质的非微扰框架，例如$f_0(2470)$异常长的寿命。

Method: The method involves a review of recent progress in the field, proposing a new classification for the scalar nonet, and using a topological soliton model to describe the internal structure of glueballs. The authors demonstrate consistency between the proposed classification and the observed production yields in heavy-ion collisions through statistical, coalescence, and S-matrix frameworks. The energy spectrum derived from the topological soliton model is compared with lattice QCD and experimental data.

方法包括对领域内最新进展的回顾，提出新的标量非特态分类，并使用拓扑孤子模型来描述胶球的内部结构。作者通过统计、凝聚和S矩阵框架展示了所提出的分类与重离子碰撞中观察到的产额之间的一致性。从拓扑孤子模型得到的能量谱与格点QCD和实验数据进行了比较。

Result: The results show that the new classification of the scalar nonet, including $f_0(980)$ and $a_0(980)$ as the lowest states and $f_0(1500)$ as a primary glueball candidate, is consistent with the production yields in heavy-ion collisions. The topological soliton model provides an energy spectrum in excellent agreement with both lattice QCD and experimental data, and it explains the anomalously long lifetime of $f_0(2470)$ as a tightly bound glueballonium.

结果显示，新的标量非特态分类，包括$f_0(980)$和$a_0(980)$作为最低状态以及$f_0(1500)$作为主要胶球候选者，与重离子碰撞中的产额一致。拓扑孤子模型提供的能量谱与格点QCD和实验数据非常吻合，并且解释了$f_0(2470)$作为紧密结合的胶球偶素的异常长寿命。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the new classification of the scalar nonet and the identification of $f_0(1500)$ as a primary glueball candidate are supported by the consistency of production yields in heavy-ion collisions. The topological soliton model offers a promising non-perturbative framework for predicting the properties of exotic scalar states, which can be further tested experimentally.

结论是，新的标量非特态分类及$f_0(1500)$作为主要胶球候选者的识别得到了重离子碰撞中产额一致性的支持。拓扑孤子模型为预测奇异标量态的性质提供了一个有前景的非微扰框架，这可以通过进一步的实验进行验证。

Abstract: This contribution reviews recent progress in the low-lying scalar mesons and glueballs. We propose a new classification for the scalar nonet that includes $f_0(980)$ and $a_0(980)$ as the lowest states, while we identify $f_0(1500)$ as a primary glueball candidate. We demonstrate that the production yields of these states in heavy-ion collisions are mutually consistent across statistical, coalescence, and S-matrix frameworks. To investigate their internal structure, we move beyond standard phenomenology by describing glueballs as topological solitons. This approach yields an energy spectrum in excellent agreement with lattice QCD and experimental data, while interpreting $f_0(2470)$ as a tightly bound glueballonium to explain its anomalously long lifetime. This non-perturbative framework provides a predictive basis for the future experimental verification of exotic scalar states.

### [58] [How to understand $ρ$ Resonance from the Quark Model and $ππ$ $P$-wave phase shift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24270)
*Wen-Ze Zhao,Ru-Hui Ni,Jia-Jun Wu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper presents a unified framework for studying the structure and resonant properties of the $\rho$ meson, combining quark-gluon and hadronic degrees of freedom. The authors use a chiral quark model to determine the bare mass of the $\rho$ meson and then apply inverse scattering theory to analyze the coupling between the bare state and the $\pi\pi$ continuum, extracting the $\rho_0-\pi\pi$ interaction and calculating the width of the $\rho$ meson.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to provide a more comprehensive understanding of the $\rho$ meson's physical properties, which cannot be fully characterized by the conventional constituent quark model due to its strong coupling to the $\pi\pi$ channel and large decay width. The authors aim to establish a unified framework that incorporates both quark-gluon and hadronic degrees of freedom to better describe the $\rho$ meson's structure and resonant properties.

本文的动机是提供对$\rho$介子物理性质更全面的理解。由于其与$\pi\pi$通道的强耦合及其较大的衰变宽度，传统的组分夸克模型无法完全描述$\rho$介子的物理性质。作者旨在建立一个统一的框架，该框架结合了夸克-胶子和强子自由度，以更好地描述$\rho$介子的结构和共振特性。

Method: The method involves two main steps: first, at the quark-gluon level, the parameters of the chiral quark model are determined by refitting a set of narrow mesons without or with strongly suppressed open OZI-allowed strong-decay channels. This provides the bare mass of the $\rho$ meson. Second, at the hadronic level, inverse scattering theory is used to construct a model that includes the coupling between the bare state and the $\pi\pi$ continuum. The $\rho_0-\pi\pi$ interaction is extracted using $P$-wave $\pi\pi$ scattering phase-shift data, and the width of the $\rho$ meson and the bare-state component in the physical state are calculated.

方法包括两个主要步骤：首先，在夸克-胶子层面，通过重新拟合一组没有或具有强烈抑制的开放OZI允许强衰变通道的窄介子来确定手征夸克模型的参数。这提供了$\rho$介子的裸质量。其次，在强子层面，使用逆散射理论构建了一个模型，该模型包括裸态和$\pi\pi$连续谱之间的耦合。使用$P$波$\pi\pi$散射相移数据提取$\rho_0-\pi\pi$相互作用，并计算$\rho$介子的宽度以及物理态中的裸态成分。

Result: The results include the determination of the bare mass of the $\rho$ meson from the chiral quark model, the extraction of the $\rho_0-\pi\pi$ interaction, and the calculation of the width of the $\rho$ meson. Additionally, the bare-state component in the physical state is quantified, providing insights into the structure and resonant properties of the $\rho$ meson.

结果包括从手征夸克模型中确定$\rho$介子的裸质量、提取$\rho_0-\pi\pi$相互作用以及计算$\rho$介子的宽度。此外，还量化了物理态中的裸态成分，为理解$\rho$介子的结构和共振特性提供了洞见。

Conclusion: The conclusion of this paper is that the unified framework combining quark-gluon and hadronic degrees of freedom successfully characterizes the $\rho$ meson's physical properties, including its structure and resonant behavior. The analytical framework developed in this work can be generalized to study other hadronic resonances with significant channel-coupling effects.

本文的结论是，结合夸克-胶子和强子自由度的统一框架成功地描述了$\rho$介子的物理性质，包括其结构和共振行为。本文开发的分析框架可以推广到研究其他具有显著通道耦合效应的强子共振态。

Abstract: As the lightest isovector vector meson, the $ρ$ meson is an important object for investigating the structure of resonant states in strong interactions. Owing to its strong coupling to the $ππ$ channel and its large decay width, the conventional constituent quark model treatment, in which it is simply regarded as a pure $q\bar q$ bound state while the hadronic-channel coupling effects are neglected, is insufficient to fully characterize its physical properties. To this end, in the present work we establish a unified framework for studying the structure and resonant properties of the $ρ$ meson by combining the quark-gluon and hadronic degrees of freedom. At the quark-gluon level, we first determine the parameters of the chiral quark model by refitting a set of narrow mesons for which open OZI-allowed strong-decay channels are absent or strongly suppressed. With these parameters fixed, the bare mass of the $ρ$ meson is obtained and used as the input for the subsequent hadronic-level analysis. At the hadronic level, based on inverse scattering theory, we construct a model including the coupling between the bare state and the $ππ$ continuum, extract the $ρ_0-ππ$ interaction using the $P$-wave $ππ$ scattering phase-shift data, and further calculate the width of the $ρ$ meson as well as the bare-state component in the physical state. The present work also provides a generalizable analytical framework for further studies of other hadronic resonances with significant channel-coupling effects.

### [59] [Role of heavy neutral lepton in lepton number violating $B$ meson decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24305)
*Dhiren Panda,Manas Kumar Mohapatra,Rukmani Mohanta*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper investigates the phenomenology of heavy neutral leptons (HNLs) in B-meson decays, focusing on the channels $B \to \mu N$ and $B \to \tau N$. It constrains the allowed regions in the $M_N$--$|U_{\ell N}|^2$ plane and predicts branching ratios for lepton-number violating processes. The channel $B_c^- \to \pi^+ \mu^- \mu^-$ shows the largest enhancement, indicating enhanced sensitivity to HNL effects and promising avenues for future searches.

该论文研究了重中性轻子（HNLs）在B介子衰变中的现象学，重点研究了$B \to \mu N$和$B \to \tau N$通道。它约束了$M_N$--$|U_{\ell N}|^2$平面上的允许区域，并预测了轻子数违反过程的分支比。$B_c^- \to \pi^+ \mu^- \mu^-$通道显示出最大的增强，表明对HNL效应的敏感度增强，并为未来的搜索提供了有希望的途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore the phenomenology of heavy neutral leptons (HNLs) as probes of physics beyond the Standard Model. By studying the leptonic decays of B-mesons, the authors aim to constrain the parameter space of HNLs and investigate lepton-number violating processes, which could provide evidence for new physics.

动机是探索重中性轻子（HNLs）作为超出标准模型物理的探针的现象学。通过研究B介子的轻子衰变，作者旨在约束HNLs的参数空间并研究轻子数违反过程，这可能为新物理提供证据。

Method: The authors use current experimental data to constrain the allowed regions in the $M_N$--$|U_{\ell N}|^2$ plane for the leptonic channels $B \to \mu N$ and $B \to \tau N$. They then investigate lepton-number violating ($\Delta L=2$) processes mediated by on-shell HNLs, such as $B_{(c)}^- \to \pi^+ \mu^- \mu^-$ and $B_c^- \to J/\psi\, \pi^+ \mu^- \mu^-$. The analysis involves calculating the branching ratios for these processes and comparing them with the experimental constraints.

作者使用当前的实验数据来约束$B \to \mu N$和$B \to \tau N$轻子通道在$M_N$--$|U_{\ell N}|^2$平面上的允许区域。然后，他们研究由在壳HNLs介导的轻子数违反（$\Delta L=2$）过程，例如$B_{(c)}^- \to \pi^+ \mu^- \mu^-$和$B_c^- \to J/\psi\, \pi^+ \mu^- \mu^-$。分析包括计算这些过程的分支比，并将它们与实验约束进行比较。

Result: For benchmark values $|U_{\mu N}|^2 = 10^{-6}$ and $M_N = 2$--$3\,\mathrm{GeV}$, the predicted branching ratios for the lepton-number violating processes lie in the range $\mathcal{O}(10^{-13})$--$\mathcal{O}(10^{-8})$. Among the channels, $B_c^- \to \pi^+ \mu^- \mu^-$ shows the largest enhancement, while $B_c^- \to J/\psi\, \pi^+ \mu^- \mu^-$ is strongly suppressed. These results indicate a clear channel dependence, with $B_c$ modes providing enhanced sensitivity to HNL effects.

对于基准值$|U_{\mu N}|^2 = 10^{-6}$和$M_N = 2$--$3\,\mathrm{GeV}$，轻子数违反过程的预测分支比在$\mathcal{O}(10^{-13})$--$\mathcal{O}(10^{-8})$范围内。在这些通道中，$B_c^- \to \pi^+ \mu^- \mu^-$显示出最大的增强，而$B_c^- \to J/\psi\, \pi^+ \mu^- \mu^-$则被强烈抑制。这些结果表明明显的通道依赖性，$B_c$模式对HNL效应的敏感度增强。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that the $B_c$ decay modes provide enhanced sensitivity to HNL effects, particularly in the $B_c^- \to \pi^+ \mu^- \mu^-$ channel. This indicates promising avenues for future searches of lepton number violation and further exploration of physics beyond the Standard Model through the study of HNLs in B-meson decays.

研究表明，$B_c$衰变模式对HNL效应的敏感度增强，特别是在$B_c^- \to \pi^+ \mu^- \mu^-$通道中。这表明了未来寻找轻子数违反和通过研究B介子衰变中的HNLs进一步探索超出标准模型物理的有希望的途径。

Abstract: We study the phenomenology of heavy neutral leptons (HNLs) in $B$-meson decays as probes of physics beyond the Standard Model. Focusing on the leptonic channels $B \to μN$ and $B \to τN$, we constrain the allowed regions in the $M_N$--$|U_{\ell N}|^2$ plane using current experimental data. Using these constraints, we investigate lepton-number violating ($ΔL=2$) processes mediated by on-shell HNLs, including $B_{(c)}^- \to π^+ μ^- μ^-$ and $B_c^- \to J/ψ\, π^+ μ^- μ^-$. For benchmark values $|U_{μN}|^2 = 10^{-6}$ and $M_N = 2$-- $3\,\mathrm{GeV}$, the predicted branching ratios lie in the range $\mathcal{O}(10^{-13})$--$\mathcal{O}(10^{-8})$. Among the channels, $B_c^- \to π^+ μ^- μ^-$ shows the largest enhancement, while $B_c^- \to J/ψ\, π^+ μ^- μ^-$ is strongly suppressed. These results indicate a clear channel dependence, with $B_c$ modes providing enhanced sensitivity to HNL effects and offering promising avenues for future searches of lepton number violation.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Additionally, the paper considers the same for the dielectron mode $\Sigma^+ \to p e^+ e^-$ and the radiative mode $\Sigma^+ \to p \gamma$.

方法包括对稀有超子衰变 $\Sigma^+ \to p \mu^+ \mu^-$ 及其反超子对应物的理论分析，重点在于长程贡献与潜在新物理贡献之间的干涉。作者计算了衰变率不对称性，考虑了来自长程贡献的大吸收相位。他们还考虑了介电子模式 $\Sigma^+ \to p e^+ e^-$ 和辐射模式 $\Sigma^+ \to p \gamma$，以全面理解可能的 $CP$ 破坏效应。

Result: The results show that the decay rate asymmetry in the rare hyperon decay $\Sigma^+ \to p \mu^+ \mu^-$ can be as high as tens of percent, which is within the reach of the LHCb experiment. This suggests that there is a significant potential for observing $CP$ violation in this decay mode. 结果表明，稀有超子衰变 $\Sigma^+ \to p \mu^+ \mu^-$ 的衰变率不对称性可以高达百分之几十，这在 LHCb 实验的探测范围内。这表明在这种衰变模式中观测到 $CP$ 破坏具有显著潜力。研究还提供了介电子模式 $\Sigma^+ \to p e^+ e^-$ 和辐射模式 $\Sigma^+ \to p \gamma$ 的见解，表明这些模式也可能表现出显著的 $CP$ 破坏效应。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the rare hyperon decay $\Sigma^+ \to p \mu^+ \mu^-$ and its antihyperon counterpart have the potential to reveal significant $CP$ violation due to the large absorptive phases from long-distance contributions. Abstract: The LHCb collaboration has recently observed the rare hyperon decay $Σ^+\to pμ^+μ^-$. A detailed simulation is performed to identify the promising region for this signature at μTRISTAN.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore the phenomenological implications of the low scale seesaw mechanism, which naturally explains tiny neutrino masses through the coupling of a heavy neutral lepton $N$ with a neutrinophilic Higgs doublet $Φ_ν$. The focus is on the new Yukawa interaction $y \overline{L}\tildeΦ_νN$, which can lead to observable signatures at colliders, specifically the 2 TeV same-sign muon mode of μTRISTAN.

Method: The method involves the investigation of two distinct channels that generate the same-sign tetralepton signature. The first channel is the pair production of charged Higgs bosons, resulting in the decay chain $μ^+μ^+\to H^+ H^+\to μ^+N +μ^+ N\to μ^+ μ^+ jj + μ^+ μ^+ jj\to 4μ^+ + 4j$. The second channel is the single production of a charged Higgs boson, leading to the decay chain $μ^+μ^+ \to μ^+ N H^+ \to μ^+N +μ^+ N\to μ^+ μ^+ jj + μ^+ μ^+ jj\to 4μ^+ + 4j$. A detailed simulation of these processes is carried out to determine the feasibility of detecting the signature at μTRISTAN.

Result: The result is the identification of a promising region for the same-sign tetralepton signature at μTRISTAN, based on the detailed simulation of the two distinct channels. The analysis demonstrates the potential of observing this signature, which could provide evidence for the low scale seesaw mechanism and the existence of a neutrinophilic Higgs doublet.

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the proposed same-sign tetralepton signature at μTRISTAN, generated by the pair and single production of charged Higgs bosons, offers a promising avenue for probing the low scale seesaw mechanism and the associated neutrinophilic Higgs doublet. The detailed simulation indicates that this signature is detectable within the expected parameter space, thus providing a valuable experimental test for the model.

Abstract: Naturally tiny neutrino masses can be explained by the low scale seesaw with heavy neutral lepton $N$ coupling to the neutrinophilic Higgs doublet $Φ_ν$, which obtains a much smaller vacuum expectation value than the standard Higgs doublet $Φ$. Within this model, the neutrino masses originate from the new Yukawa interaction $y \overline{L}\tildeΦ_νN$. In this paper, we propose the novel same-sign tetralepton signature at the 2 TeV same-sign muon mode $μ^+μ^+$ of $μ$TRISTAN. We investigate two distinct channels of this signature, which are both generated by the Yukawa interaction $y \overline{L}\tildeΦ_νN$. One is from the pair production of charged Higgs $μ^+μ^+\to H^+ H^+\to μ^+N +μ^+ N\to μ^+ μ^+ jj + μ^+ μ^+ jj\to 4μ^+ + 4j$, and the other one is from the single production of charged Higgs $μ^+μ^+ \to μ^+ N H^+ \to μ^+N +μ^+ N\to μ^+ μ^+ jj + μ^+ μ^+ jj\to 4μ^+ + 4j$. We then perform a detailed simulation of this same-sign tetralepton signature, and obtain the promising region at $μ$TRISTAN.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: In this paper, we present the production of double SM-like Higgs $ (h) $ at the future electron positron colliders within the context of $ S_{3} $ model with three Higgs doublets (S3-3H) and no CP violation to describe beyond the Standard Model Higgs Physics. We focus first on the numerically allowed parameter space of the model, taking into account theoretical bounds from perturbative unitarity and vacuum stability, as well as by data at the Large Hadron Collider (LHC) and the Tevatron. The double Higgs production in the S3-3H model can deviate from the SM predictions up to a few orders of magnitude in both the $ e^+e^- \rightarrow hhZ $ and the $ e^+ e^- \rightarrow h hν_{e} \barν_{e}$ channels. Abstract: We study the magnetic fields produced in the early Universe during the electroweak symmetry breaking by considering random configurations of an inhomogeneous Higgs field. By exploiting the inherent randomness of the initial configurations the spectrum of the produced magnetic field is essentially analytic, which bypasses the need for costly lattice simulations. On the numerical side, we devise a simulation framework which results in continuous fields capable of resolving the small-scale structure of the fields that was inaccessible for the lattice-based calculation. Finally, by revisiting the effects of statistical isotropy and causality on the spectrum, we define general correlation functions that are then fitted to the simulation data and compared to the analytic results.

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper explores the production of scalar and vector dark matter during a cosmological first-order phase transition, coupled with the field undergoing the transition. It identifies regions where significant deviations from the normal freeze-out scenario occur, affecting dark matter abundances. The study also calculates the expected gravitational wave signal from these phase transitions.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand how the presence of a first-order phase transition in the dark sector, coupled with the dark matter, can alter the standard freeze-out mechanism for both scalar and vector dark matter. This is important for predicting the correct relic abundance and for identifying potential signatures, such as gravitational waves, that could be detected and provide evidence for new physics beyond the Standard Model.

动机是理解暗物质与发生相变的场耦合时，暗物质部门中的一级相变如何改变标量和矢量暗物质的标准冻结机制。这对于预测正确的遗迹丰度以及识别可能检测到的特征（如引力波）非常重要，这些特征可以为超出标准模型的新物理提供证据。

Method: The authors use a combination of analytical calculations and numerical simulations to model the dark matter production during the phase transition. They consider the effects of the phase transition on the dark matter annihilation cross-sections and the subsequent freeze-out process. The analysis includes the calculation of the gravitational wave signal generated by the phase transition, using the formalism of the energy density spectrum and the peak amplitude of the gravitational waves.

作者使用分析计算和数值模拟相结合的方法来模拟相变期间的暗物质产生。他们考虑了相变对暗物质湮灭截面及随后的冻结过程的影响。分析包括使用能量密度谱和引力波峰值幅度的形式来计算相变产生的引力波信号。

Result: The results show that for scalar dark matter, significant deviations from the standard freeze-out scenario occur when the phase transition happens around 1 GeV. For vector dark matter, the deviations are notable when the phase transition is around 10 MeV. Additionally, the paper provides predictions for the gravitational wave signals from these phase transitions, which could be detectable by future gravitational wave observatories.

结果表明，对于标量暗物质，当相变发生在1 GeV左右时，与标准冻结场景相比会出现显著偏差。对于矢量暗物质，当相变在10 MeV左右时，偏差显著。这些偏差导致与标准热冻结相比，预测的暗物质质量范围不同。此外，该论文还提供了这些相变产生的引力波信号的预测，这些信号可能被未来的引力波观测站探测到。

Conclusion: The study concludes that the presence of a first-order phase transition in the dark sector, coupled with the dark matter, can significantly affect the relic abundance of both scalar and vector dark matter. The deviations from the standard freeze-out scenario lead to different predictions for the dark matter mass range. Furthermore, the gravitational wave signals from these phase transitions provide a potential observational signature for future experiments.

Abstract: Both scalar and vector dark matter can be produced during a cosmological first order phase transition if the dark matter is coupled to the field undergoing the transition. Both kinds of particle are also produced by the plasma through the normal freeze out scenario. For different dark matter masses, we identify the regions of parameter space where there are significant deviations from the normal freeze out scenario and discover there are some rather general predictions. For dark matter particles in the traditional thermal relic GeV-TeV window, dark sector phase transitions around a GeV affect scalar dark matter and dark sector phase transitions around 10 MeV affect vector dark matter abundances (and therefore should take place in a dark sector). When the phase transitions are in the interesting temperature range, the normal range of dark matter masses are different to those predicted by thermal freeze out. We calculate the expected gravitational wave signal of these phase transitions.

### [65] [Non-perturbative heavy quark diffusion coefficients in arbitrarily magnetized quark-gluon plasma](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24535)
*Debarshi Dey,Aritra Bandyopadhyay,Yifeng Sun,Santosh K. Das*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper computes the heavy quark momentum and spatial diffusion coefficients in a non-perturbative thermal QCD medium under an arbitrary strength magnetic field, revealing anisotropic diffusion and two distinct spatial diffusion coefficients. Non-perturbative effects are significant at low temperatures, which is crucial for Langevin-based calculations of heavy quark directed flow at RHIC and LHC energies.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to provide a more accurate and consistent description of heavy quark (HQ) diffusion in a thermal QCD medium, especially in the presence of a strong magnetic field. This is important for understanding the behavior of heavy quarks in high-energy collisions, such as those at RHIC and LHC, where the medium properties can significantly affect the diffusion process. The study aims to incorporate both perturbative and non-perturbative effects, which are essential for a comprehensive theoretical framework.

本文的动机是提供一个更准确和一致的描述，特别是在强磁场存在下热QCD介质中的重夸克扩散。这对于理解在高能碰撞（如RHIC和LHC）中重夸克的行为非常重要，因为在这些情况下介质的性质可以显著影响扩散过程。研究旨在结合微扰和非微扰效应，这对于一个全面的理论框架至关重要。

Method: The method employed in this paper involves the computation of the heavy quark (HQ) momentum ($\kappa$) and spatial diffusion ($D_s$) coefficients in a non-perturbative thermal QCD medium. The in-medium HQ potential, derived from the resummed gluon propagator, is used to incorporate both perturbative and non-perturbative effects. The presence of a background magnetic field of arbitrary strength introduces anisotropy in the diffusion coefficients, leading to two distinct spatial diffusion coefficients, $D_s^L$ and $D_s^T$. The analysis also highlights the dominance of non-perturbative effects at low temperatures.

本文采用的方法涉及计算非微扰热QCD介质中的重夸克动量（$\kappa$）和空间扩散（$D_s$）系数。通过重整化胶子传播子得到的介质中重夸克势用于结合微扰和非微扰效应。任意强度背景磁场的存在使得扩散系数各向异性，从而导致两个不同的空间扩散系数$D_s^L$和$D_s^T$。分析还强调了低温下非微扰效应的主导作用。

Result: The results show that the heavy quark momentum diffusion coefficients become anisotropic even in the static heavy quark limit, with the magnetic field direction defining the axis of anisotropy. This anisotropy arises from restrictions on longitudinal momentum diffusion in the gluon spectral function, leading to two distinct spatial diffusion coefficients, $D_s^L$ and $D_s^T$. Additionally, non-perturbative effects are found to be dominant at low temperatures, which has implications for the heavy quark dynamics in the early stages of heavy-ion collisions.

结果显示，即使在静态重夸克极限下，重夸克动量扩散系数也变得各向异性，磁场方向定义了各向异性的轴。这种各向异性起源于胶子谱函数中对纵向动量扩散的限制，导致两个不同的空间扩散系数$D_s^L$和$D_s^T$。此外，发现在低温下非微扰效应占主导地位，这对重离子碰撞早期阶段的重夸克动力学有重要影响。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that the inclusion of both perturbative and non-perturbative effects, along with the presence of a magnetic field, leads to anisotropic diffusion of heavy quarks in a thermal QCD medium. The identification of two spatial diffusion coefficients, $D_s^L$ and $D_s^T$, and the dominance of non-perturbative effects at low temperatures, provides a more consistent input for Langevin-based calculations of heavy quark directed flow at RHIC and LHC energies.

论文得出结论，结合微扰和非微扰效应以及磁场的存在，导致了热QCD介质中重夸克的各向异性扩散。识别出两个空间扩散系数$D_s^L$和$D_s^T$，以及低温下非微扰效应的主导作用，为RHIC和LHC能量下的重夸克定向流的朗之万计算提供了更一致的输入。

Abstract: Heavy quark (HQ) momentum ($κ$) and spatial diffusion ($D_s$) coefficients are computed in a non-perturbative thermal QCD medium in the presence of a background magnetic field of arbitrary strength. Both perturbative and non-perturbative effects are incorporated via the in-medium HQ potential, obtained from the resummed gluon propagator. We find that the momentum diffusion coefficients become anisotropic even in the static heavy quark limit, with the magnetic field direction defining the axis of anisotropy. This anisotropy originates from restrictions on longitudinal momentum diffusion in the gluon spectral function, and naturally leads to two spatial diffusion coefficients ($D_s^L$, $D_s^T$). Non-perturbative effects are found to be dominant at low temperatures. These results provide a more consistent input for Langevin based calculations of the heavy quark directed flow at RHIC and LHC energies.

</details>


### [66] [Mass spectra of charged mesons and the quenching of vector meson condensation via exact phase-space diagonalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24595)
*Jingyi Chao,Kun Xu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper investigates the dynamics and mass spectra of charged pseudoscalar ($π^+$) and vector ($ρ^+$) mesons in a magnetic field at finite temperature using the NJL model. It introduces a non-commutative phase-space framework that allows for the algebraic diagonalization of Bethe-Salpeter equations. The study finds that the $π^+$ mass tracks the zero-point energy, while the $ρ^+$ state avoids tachyonic instability. The chiral condensate's magnetic catalysis prevents vector meson condensation, and thermal effects suppress meson masses without Mott dissociation.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the behavior of charged pseudoscalar and vector mesons in a strong magnetic field at finite temperature, which is relevant for high-energy physics and astrophysical environments such as neutron stars and heavy-ion collisions. The study aims to provide a theoretical framework that can accurately describe the mass spectra and stability of these mesons under such conditions.

动机是理解在强磁场和有限温度下带电伪标量和矢量介子的行为，这对于高能物理和天体物理环境（如中子星和重离子碰撞）具有重要意义。研究旨在提供一个能够准确描述这些介子在这种条件下的质量谱和稳定性的理论框架。

Method: The method involves the use of the two-flavor Nambu-Jona-Lasinio (NJL) model with a quark propagator that isolates the Schwinger phase from its Landau level expansion. The authors formulate an exact non-commutative phase-space framework using the Wigner-Weyl transform and the Moyal star product. This approach enables the algebraic diagonalization of the Bethe-Salpeter equations for composite states with asymmetric fractional constituent charges. The analysis includes both the pseudoscalar and vector channels, with a focus on the dynamical random phase approximation and the Zeeman spin-splitting.

方法涉及使用双味Nambu-Jona-Lasinio (NJL) 模型，其中夸克传播子将Schwinger相位从Landau能级展开中分离出来。作者利用Wigner-Weyl变换和Moyal星积构建了一个精确的非交换相空间框架。这种方法使得具有不对称分数组分电荷的复合态的Bethe-Salpeter方程可以进行代数对角化。分析包括伪标量通道和矢量通道，重点关注动力学随机相位近似和Zeeman自旋分裂。

Result: The results show that for the pseudoscalar channel, the $π^+$ pole mass strictly tracks the kinematic zero-point energy drift at order of $eB$. In the vector channel, the Zeeman spin-splitting emerges dynamically, and the tachyonic instability of the spin-aligned $ρ^+$ state is quenched. The magnetic catalysis of the chiral condensate drives the continuum threshold upwards, preventing vector meson condensation. Finite-temperature evaluations indicate a monotonic thermal suppression of the meson masses, but all modes remain bound without undergoing Mott dissociation prior to chiral symmetry restoration.

结果表明，在伪标量通道中，$π^+$极点质量严格跟踪零点动能漂移，其阶数为$eB$。在矢量通道中，Zeeman自旋分裂动态出现，且自旋对齐的$ρ^+$状态的类时性不稳定性被抑制。手征凝聚物的磁催化使连续阈值上升，从而阻止了矢量介子凝聚。有限温度评估表明介子质量单调热抑制，但在手征对称性恢复之前，所有模式保持束缚而不会发生Mott解离。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the non-commutative phase-space framework provides a robust theoretical tool for understanding the dynamics and mass spectra of charged mesons in a background magnetic field at finite temperature. The study confirms the generalized Goldstone theorem for the $π^+$ meson and elucidates the role of magnetic catalysis and Zeeman splitting in the stability of vector mesons. The results suggest that the meson masses are thermally suppressed, but the mesons remain bound up to the chiral symmetry restoration temperature.

结论是非交换相空间框架为理解有限温度下背景磁场中带电介子的动力学和质量谱提供了强大的理论工具。该研究确认了$π^+$介子的广义Goldstone定理，并阐明了磁催化和Zeeman分裂在矢量介子稳定性中的作用。结果表明，介子质量受到热抑制，但在手征对称性恢复温度之前，介子仍然保持束缚。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamics and mass spectra of charged pseudoscalar ($π^+$) and vector ($ρ^+$) mesons in a background magnetic field at finite temperature using the two-flavor Nambu-Jona--Lasinio (NJL) model. By employing a quark propagator that isolates the Schwinger phase from its Landau level expansion, we formulate an exact non-commutative phase-space framework utilizing the Wigner-Weyl transform and the Moyal star product. This approach enables the algebraic diagonalization of the Bethe-Salpeter equations for composite states with asymmetric fractional constituent charges. For the pseudoscalar channel, we analytically verify the exact cancellation between the dynamical random phase approximation spatial sum rules and the vacuum gap equation. This identity preserves the generalized Goldstone theorem, causing the $π^+$ pole mass to strictly track the kinematic zero-point energy drift at order of $eB$. In the vector channel, our full phase-space evaluation reveals that the Zeeman spin-splitting emerges dynamically from microscopic threshold truncations governed by the chiral Dirac algebra. Notably, we find that the tachyonic instability of the spin-aligned $ρ^+$ state is quenched. The magnetic catalysis of the chiral condensate drives the continuum threshold ($2M$) upwards, overtaking the Zeeman attraction and preventing vector meson condensation within this mean-field framework. Furthermore, finite-temperature evaluations show a monotonic thermal suppression of the meson masses driven by Pauli blocking, yet all modes remain bound without undergoing Mott dissociation prior to chiral symmetry restoration.

</details>


### [67] [Nucleon decays into one lepton plus two non-strange mesons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24613)
*Wei-Qi Fan,Yi Liao,Xiao-Dong Ma*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper presents a model-independent analysis of nucleon decays into a lepton and two pseudoscalar mesons, using low-energy effective field theory. The study derives improved bounds on 15 three-body decay modes, with partial lifetimes for charged-lepton modes exceeding current PDG values by over three orders of magnitude. For (anti)neutrino modes, the first constraints are established at $\Gamma^{-1} \gtrsim 10^{34}\,\rm yr$. Additionally, the constraints on two-body processes are also improved by a factor of 2 compared to PDG limits.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to probe baryon number violation through nucleon decays into a lepton and two pseudoscalar mesons, which complement conventional two-body decay modes. By avoiding the single-operator-dominance assumption and leveraging correlations among different processes, the authors aim to set more stringent constraints on experimentally challenging processes, thus better probing new physics beyond the Standard Model.

动机是通过核子衰变为一个轻子和两个伪标量介子来探测重子数破坏，这补充了传统的两体衰变模式。通过避免单算符主导假设并利用不同过程之间的相关性，作者旨在对实验上难以测量的过程设置更严格的限制，从而更好地探测标准模型之外的新物理。

Method: The method involves a model-independent correlation of two- and three-body nucleon decay processes within the framework of low-energy effective field theory. The global analysis avoids the single-operator-dominance assumption, allowing for a comprehensive examination of the decay channels. The approach enables the derivation of significantly improved bounds on 15 three-body decay modes involving a lepton and two non-strange mesons, as well as enhanced constraints on two-body processes.

方法涉及在低能有效场论框架内，对两体和三体核子衰变过程进行模型无关的相关性分析。全局分析避免了单算符主导假设，允许对衰变通道进行全面检查。该方法能够推导出涉及一个轻子和两个非奇异介子的15种三体衰变模式的显著改进的界限，以及对两体过程的增强约束。

Result: The results include significantly improved bounds on 15 three-body nucleon decay modes with a lepton and two non-strange mesons. For charged-lepton modes, the lower limits on partial lifetimes ($\Gamma^{-1}$) surpass current PDG values by more than three orders of magnitude. For (anti)neutrino modes, the first constraints are established at $\Gamma^{-1} \gtrsim 10^{34}\,\rm yr$. Additionally, the constraints on two-body processes $n\to e^+\pi^-$, $n\to \mu^+\pi^-$, and $p\to \hat{\nu}\pi^+$ are improved by approximately a factor of 2 compared to the PDG limits.

结果包括对涉及一个轻子和两个非奇异介子的15种三体核子衰变模式的显著改进的界限。对于带电轻子模式，部分寿命的下限（$\Gamma^{-1}$）超过当前PDG值三个数量级以上。对于(反)中微子模式，首次建立了$\Gamma^{-1} \gtrsim 10^{34}\,\rm yr$的约束。此外，与PDG限制相比，对两体过程$n\to e^+\pi^-$, $n\to \mu^+\pi^-$, 和 $p\to \hat{\nu}\pi^+$的约束提高了约两倍。

Conclusion: The conclusion emphasizes the importance of leveraging correlations among different nucleon decay processes to set more stringent constraints on experimentally challenging processes. The analysis provides significantly improved bounds on both three-body and two-body nucleon decay modes, highlighting the potential for better probing new physics beyond the Standard Model.

结论强调了利用不同核子衰变过程之间的相关性来对实验上难以测量的过程设置更严格的限制的重要性。该分析为三体和两体核子衰变模式提供了显著改进的界限，突显了更好地探测标准模型之外新物理的潜力。

Abstract: Nucleon decays into a lepton and two pseudoscalar mesons represent key channels for probing baryon number violation, complementing conventional two-body modes. In this Letter, we model-independently correlate two- and three-body processes within the framework of low-energy effective field theory, performing a global analysis that avoids single-operator-dominance assumption. We derive significantly improved bounds on 15 three-body modes with a lepton ($e^+,\,μ^+,\hatν=ν/\barν$) and two non-strange mesons ($π,η$). For charged-lepton modes, our lower limits on partial lifetimes ($Γ^{-1}$) surpass current Particle Data Group (PDG) values by more than three orders of magnitude. For 5 (anti)neutrino modes, we establish for the first time $Γ^{-1}\gtrsim 10^{34}\,\rm yr$. Additionally, our analysis improves constraints on two-body processes $n\to e^+π^-$, $n\to μ^+π^-$, and $p\to \hatνπ^+$ by approximately a factor of 2 compared to the PDG limits. These results highlight the importance of leveraging correlations among different processes to better probe new physics, enabling more stringent constraints on experimentally challenging processes from well-measured ones.
