### [68] [On the Two $R$-Factors in the Small-$x$ Shockwave Formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24629)
*Yuri V. Kovchegov,M. Gabriel Santiago,Huachen Sun*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper proposes two theoretical advancements to eliminate the need for $R$-factors in the phenomenology of exclusive processes at small $x$. The first advancement involves modifying the rapidity argument of the dipole and odderon amplitudes, while the second involves a more careful treatment of the initial conditions for non-linear small-$x$ evolution, thus accounting for the real part of the scattering amplitude.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to improve the theoretical framework for describing exclusive processes at small $x$ by eliminating the need for phenomenological $R$-factors. These factors are used to account for non-zero longitudinal momentum transfer and the real part of the elastic scattering amplitude, which are not included in the standard dipole scattering amplitude.

动机是通过消除对现象学$R$-因子的需求，改进描述小$x$下的独占过程的理论框架。这些因子用于考虑非零纵向动量转移和弹性散射振幅的实部，而这些在标准偶极散射振幅中是没有包括的。

Method: The authors propose two methods: (i) Modifying the rapidity argument $Y = \ln (1/x)$ of the eikonal dipole amplitude $N$ and the odderon dipole amplitude $\cal O$ to $Y = \ln \min \left\{ 1/|x|, 1/|ξ|\right\}$, to account for non-zero skewness $ξ$. (ii) Carefully evaluating the initial conditions for the non-linear small-$x$ evolution and writing the non-linear evolution equation in an integral form to account for the real part of the scattering amplitude, which is proportional to Im~$N$.

作者提出了两种方法：(i) 修改偶极子振幅$N$和奇极子振幅$\cal O$的快度参数$Y = \ln (1/x)$为$Y = \ln \min \left\{ 1/|x|, 1/|ξ|\right\}$，以考虑非零偏斜度$ξ$。(ii) 仔细评估非线性小$x$演化的初始条件，并将非线性演化方程写成积分形式，以考虑与Im~$N$成正比的散射振幅的实部。

Result: The proposed modifications to the rapidity argument and the initial conditions for the non-linear evolution are expected to account for the effects of non-zero skewness and the real part of the scattering amplitude, respectively. This would eliminate the need for the phenomenological $R$-factors in calculations of elastic scattering cross sections, Generalized Parton Distributions, and Generalized Transverse Momentum Dependent parton distributions at small $x$ and small but non-zero skewness $ξ$.

对快度参数和非线性演化初始条件的修改预期可以分别考虑非零偏斜度的影响和散射振幅的实部，从而在计算小$x$和小但非零偏斜度$ξ$下的弹性散射截面、广义部分子分布和广义横向动量依赖部分子分布时，消除对现象学$R$-因子的需求。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that the proposed theoretical developments can potentially eliminate the need for the two $R$-factors in the phenomenology of exclusive processes at small $x$. Future work will focus on implementing these prescriptions in practical calculations.

论文得出结论，提出的理论发展有可能在小$x$下的独占过程现象学中消除对两个$R$-因子的需求。未来的工作将集中在将这些规定应用于实际计算中。

Abstract: There are two $R$-factors frequently used in the phenomenology of exclusive processes at small values of the Bjorken $x$ variable. One $R$-factor takes into account the effects of non-zero longitudinal momentum transfer, which is assumed to be zero in the dipole scattering amplitude. Another $R$-factor accounts for the real part of the elastic scattering amplitude which is often neglected, with the standard dipole scattering amplitude giving only the imaginary part of the elastic amplitude.
  In this work we present two new theoretical developments aimed at eliminating the need for the two $R$-factors. We argue that the $R$-factors can be replaced by (i) modifying the argument of the dipole scattering amplitude and by (ii) augmenting the initial conditions for its non-linear small-$x$ evolution. Specifically, we show that to account for the effects of non-zero skewness $ξ$, one has to replace the rapidity argument $Y = \ln (1/x)$ of the eikonal dipole amplitude $N$ and the odderon dipole amplitude $\cal O$ by $Y = \ln \min \left\{ 1/|x|, 1/|ξ|\right\}$. The prescription applies to the elastic scattering cross sections, as well as for calculations of the Generalized Parton Distributions and Generalized Transverse Momentum Dependent parton distributions at small $x$ and at small but non-zero skewness $ξ$. We also show that the real part of the scattering amplitude, proportional to Im~$N$, which is intimately connected to the signature factor of the amplitude, can be accounted for by a more careful evaluation of the initial condition for the evolution and by writing the non-linear evolution equation in an integral form. One can similarly construct Im~$\cal O$ for the odd-signature odderon amplitude. We hope that future implementation of our prescriptions presented here will eliminate the need for both phenomenological $R$-factors.

</details>

### [69] [Diffusion-based Galaxy Simulations for the Roman High Latitude Survey](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22917)
*Diana Scognamiglio,Jake H. Lee,Eric Huff,Sergi R. Hildebrandt,Shoubaneh Hemmati*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper introduces a diffusion-based framework for generating realistic galaxy image simulations, tailored for the weak lensing requirements of the Roman High Latitude Survey. The method uses multi-band JWST/NIRCam observations, transforming them into the Roman observing regime. A denoising diffusion probabilistic model is trained to generate multi-band galaxy images, which are validated against an independent dataset. The results show that the generated galaxies accurately reproduce key observables and their covariance, offering a scalable and physically motivated alternative to analytic simulations.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Future weak lensing analyses with the Nancy Grace Roman Space Telescope require highly realistic image simulations to control shear systematics at unprecedented precision. Existing approaches, relying on analytic light-profile models, fail to capture the complex, non-parametric morphologies revealed by high-resolution observations. 

未来使用南希·格雷斯·罗曼太空望远镜进行的弱引力透镜分析需要高度真实的图像模拟，以以前所未有的精度控制剪切系统误差。现有的方法依赖于解析光谱模型，无法完全捕捉高分辨率观测揭示的复杂、非参数形态。

Method: The authors present a diffusion-based framework for generating realistic galaxy image simulations. They construct Roman-like galaxy images from multi-band JWST/NIRCam observations in the GOODS-S and GOODS-N fields, transforming them into the Roman observing regime through point-spread-function matching, pixel-scale conversion, and interloper masking that preserves correlated noise properties. These data are used to train a denoising diffusion probabilistic model (DDPM) to generate multi-band galaxy postage stamps in the Roman Y, J, and H filters. 

作者提出了一种基于扩散的框架来生成真实的星系图像模拟。他们从GOODS-S和GOODS-N区域的多波段JWST/NIRCam观测中构建了类似Roman的星系图像，并通过点扩散函数匹配、像素尺度转换和保留相关噪声特性的干扰掩蔽将它们转换到Roman观测体制。这些数据用于训练去噪扩散概率模型（DDPM），以在Roman Y、J和H滤波器中生成多波段星系邮票图像。

Result: The generated galaxy images are validated against an independent dataset using a consistent photometric pipeline, comparing key galaxy observables including magnitude, size, ellipticity, peak surface brightness, and three-band colors. The generated galaxies reproduce both the marginal distributions and the covariance structure of these properties, with only modest deviations in low-occupancy regions of parameter space. 

生成的星系图像通过一致的光度测量管道与独立数据集进行了验证，比较了包括星等、大小、椭圆率、峰值表面亮度和三波段颜色在内的关键星系可观测属性。生成的星系不仅再现了这些属性的边缘分布，还再现了它们的协方差结构，在参数空间的低占用区域仅有适度的偏差。

Conclusion: The results demonstrate that diffusion models provide a scalable and physically motivated alternative to analytic simulations, enabling high-fidelity galaxy populations for Roman weak lensing calibration and, more generally, for survey preparation in upcoming cosmological experiments. 

结果表明，扩散模型提供了一种可扩展且物理上合理的替代方案，可以为Roman弱引力透镜校准以及更广泛地为即将进行的宇宙学实验的调查准备提供高保真度的星系群体。

Abstract: Future weak lensing analyses with the Nancy Grace Roman Space Telescope will require highly realistic image simulations to control shear systematics at unprecedented precision. A key limitation of existing approaches is their reliance on analytic light-profile models, which cannot fully capture the complex, non-parametric morphologies revealed by high-resolution observations. We present a diffusion-based framework for generating realistic galaxy image simulations tailored to the weak lensing requirements of the Roman High Latitude Survey. We construct Roman-like galaxy images from multi-band JWST/NIRCam observations in the GOODS-S and GOODS-N fields, transforming them into the Roman observing regime through point-spread-function matching, pixel-scale conversion, and interloper masking that preserves correlated noise properties. These data are used to train a denoising diffusion probabilistic model to generate multi-band galaxy postage stamps in the Roman Y, J, and H filters. We validate the generated sample against an independent dataset using a consistent photometric pipeline, comparing key galaxy observables including magnitude, size, ellipticity, peak surface brightness, and three-band colors. The generated galaxies reproduce both the marginal distributions and the covariance structure of these properties, with only modest deviations in low-occupancy regions of parameter space. These results demonstrate that diffusion models provide a scalable and physically motivated alternative to analytic simulations, enabling high-fidelity galaxy populations for Roman weak lensing calibration and, more generally, for survey preparation in upcoming cosmological experiments.

</details>


### [70] [The Oort Cloud as a Gravitational Detector for Primordial Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22961)
*Sohrab Rahvar*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper investigates the gravitational scattering of Oort cloud objects by primordial black holes (PBHs) as a potential component of dark matter. The authors find that for PBHs with masses around $10^3 M_\odot$, the ejection and injection rates of Oort cloud objects are significant, leading to constraints on the PBH dark matter fraction. For PBHs in the mass range $10^2 M_\odot \lesssim m_{\mathrm{PBH}} \lesssim 10^5 M_\odot$, the constraints exclude $f_{\mathrm{PBH}}=1$, and at $m_{\mathrm{PBH}} = 10^3 M_\odot$, $f_{\mathrm{PBH}} \lesssim 0.002$. These results complement other astrophysical probes of dark matter.

该论文研究了原初黑洞（PBHs）作为暗物质的潜在成分对奥尔特云天体的引力散射。作者发现，对于质量约为$10^3 M_\odot$的PBHs，奥尔特云天体的弹射和注入率是显著的，从而对PBH暗物质分数进行了限制。对于质量范围在$10^2 M_\odot \lesssim m_{\mathrm{PBH}} \lesssim 10^5 M_\odot$的PBHs，这些限制排除了$f_{\mathrm{PBH}}=1$的可能性，并且在$m_{\mathrm{PBH}} = 10^3 M_\odot$时，$f_{\mathrm{PBH}} \lesssim 0.002$。这些结果补充了其他暗物质的天文物理探测方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to use planetary systems, specifically the Oort cloud, as a sensitive gravitational detector for dark matter, particularly primordial black holes (PBHs). The aim is to set constraints on the PBH dark matter fraction by examining the gravitational scattering effects on Oort cloud objects and comparing these with observational data from long period comet fluxes and terrestrial impact records.

动机是将行星系统，特别是奥尔特云，用作暗物质的敏感引力探测器，尤其是原初黑洞（PBHs）。目的是通过检查奥尔特云天体的引力散射效应，并将其与长周期彗星通量和地球撞击记录的观测数据进行比较，来设定PBH暗物质分数的限制。

Method: The method involves calculating the rates of ejection and injection of Oort cloud objects due to gravitational scattering by PBHs. The authors use a linear scaling relationship $\Gamma \propto m_{\mathrm{PBH}}$ for $m_{\mathrm{PBH}} \gtrsim 10^{-10} M_\odot$. They then compare these calculated rates with observational constraints from long period comet fluxes and terrestrial impact records to derive upper limits on the PBH dark matter fraction $f_{\mathrm{PBH}}$.

方法包括计算由于PBHs的引力散射导致的奥尔特云天体的弹射和注入率。作者使用线性比例关系$\Gamma \propto m_{\mathrm{PBH}}$，适用于$m_{\mathrm{PBH}} \gtrsim 10^{-10} M_\odot$的情况。然后，他们将这些计算出的速率与来自长周期彗星通量和地球撞击记录的观测约束进行比较，以推导出PBH暗物质分数$f_{\mathrm{PBH}}$的上限。

Result: The results show that for $m_{\mathrm{PBH}} \sim 10^3 M_\odot$, if PBHs constitute all local dark matter, they would eject $\sim1.3\times10^{12}$ objects over the Solar System's lifetime, comparable to the total Oort cloud population, and inject $\sim2.6\times10^{10}$ objects into Earth-crossing orbits. The most stringent constraints derived from these rates exclude $f_{\mathrm{PBH}}=1$ for $10^2 M_\odot \lesssim m_{\mathrm{PBH}} \lesssim 10^5 M_\odot$, with $f_{\mathrm{PBH}} \lesssim 0.002$ at $m_{\mathrm{PBH}} = 10^3 M_\odot$. For the asteroid mass window ($10^{17}$-$10^{23}$ g), the scattering rates are too low to produce observable effects.

结果显示，对于$m_{\mathrm{PBH}} \sim 10^3 M_\odot$的情况，如果PBHs构成所有局部暗物质，则它们将在太阳系的生命周期内弹射约$1.3\times10^{12}$个天体，这与整个奥尔特云天体数量相当，并将约$2.6\times10^{10}$个天体注入到地球交叉轨道中。从这些速率得出的最严格的限制排除了$10^2 M_\odot \lesssim m_{\mathrm{PBH}} \lesssim 10^5 M_\odot$范围内$f_{\mathrm{PBH}}=1$的可能性，在$m_{\mathrm{PBH}} = 10^3 M_\odot$时，$f_{\mathrm{PBH}} \lesssim 0.002$。对于小行星质量窗口（$10^{17}$-$10^{23}$ g），散射率太低而无法产生可观察到的效果。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the gravitational scattering of Oort cloud objects by PBHs can be used to place constraints on the PBH dark matter fraction. The constraints are particularly strong for PBHs in the mass range $10^2 M_\odot \lesssim m_{\mathrm{PBH}} \lesssim 10^5 M_\odot$, where $f_{\mathrm{PBH}}=1$ is excluded. For $m_{\mathrm{PBH}} = 10^3 M_\odot$, the constraint is $f_{\mathrm{PBH}} \lesssim 0.002$. These findings complement existing astrophysical probes and demonstrate the potential of planetary systems as gravitational detectors for compact dark matter.

结论是，通过PBHs对奥尔特云天体的引力散射可以用来设定PBH暗物质分数的限制。对于质量范围在$10^2 M_\odot \lesssim m_{\mathrm{PBH}} \lesssim 10^5 M_\odot$的PBHs，这些限制特别强，排除了$f_{\mathrm{PBH}}=1$的可能性。对于$m_{\mathrm{PBH}} = 10^3 M_\odot$，限制为$f_{\mathrm{PBH}} \lesssim 0.002$。这些发现补充了现有的天文物理探测方法，并展示了行星系统作为紧凑暗物质的引力探测器的潜力。

Abstract: Planetary systems can act as sensitive gravitational detectors for dark matter. We investigate the gravitational scattering of Oort cloud objects by primordial black holes (PBHs) as a potential component of the Galactic dark matter halo. Calculating the rates at which PBH encounters eject objects from the Oort cloud or inject them into Earth crossing orbits, we find a linear scaling $Γ\propto m_{\mathrm{PBH}}$ for $m_{\mathrm{PBH}} \gtrsim 10^{-10} M_\odot$. For $m_{\mathrm{PBH}} \sim 10^3 M_\odot$, PBHs constituting all local dark matter would eject $\sim1.3\times10^{12}$ objects over the Solar System's lifetime, comparable to the total Oort cloud population and inject $\sim2.6\times10^{10}$ objects into Earth-crossing orbits. Comparing these rates with observational constraints from long period comet fluxes and terrestrial impact records, we derive upper limits on the PBH dark matter fraction $f_{\mathrm{PBH}}$. Our most stringent constraints exclude $f_{\mathrm{PBH}}=1$ for $10^2 M_\odot \lesssim m_{\mathrm{PBH}} \lesssim 10^5 M_\odot$, with $f_{\mathrm{PBH}} \lesssim 0.002$ at $m_{\mathrm{PBH}} = 10^3 M_\odot$. For the asteroid mass window ($10^{17}$-$10^{23}$ g), scattering rates are far too low to produce observable effects. These Solar System-based constraints complement existing astrophysical probes and demonstrate that planetary systems can serve as sensitive gravitational detectors for compact dark matter.

</details>


### [71] [Cosmological evolution of interacting dark energy with a CPL equation of state](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22970)
*Gerald Neumann,Nelson Videla,Dorian Araya*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper analyzes interacting dark energy models within the CPL parametrization, deriving exact analytic solutions and performing a Bayesian analysis using current cosmological observations. The model with $Q = \beta H \rho_{de}$ shows a modestly improved fit, while the interaction model depending on dark matter density is not supported. The preferred model suggests a dynamic evolution of the dark energy equation of state, with implications for future cosmic acceleration.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore the theoretical structure and observational viability of interacting dark energy models within the Chevallier-Polarski-Linder (CPL) parametrization. The study aims to derive exact analytic solutions and assess the models' consistency with current cosmological data, including OHD, SNIa, BAO, and CMB. [动机是探讨Chevallier-Polarski-Linder (CPL)参数化框架下相互作用暗能量模型的理论结构和观测可行性。研究旨在推导出精确的解析解，并评估这些模型与当前宇宙学数据（包括OHD、SNIa、BAO 和 CMB）的一致性。]

Method: The method involves deriving exact analytic solutions for the evolution of the dark sector in interacting dark energy models, considering two interaction terms: $Q = \beta H \rho_{de}$ and $Q = \beta H \rho_c$. A Bayesian analysis is performed using current cosmological observations, including OHD, SNIa, BAO, and CMB data. [方法涉及推导相互作用暗能量模型中暗部门演化的精确解析解，考虑两种相互作用项：$Q = \beta H \rho_{de}$ 和 $Q = \beta H \rho_c$。使用当前的宇宙学观测数据（包括OHD、SNIa、BAO 和 CMB 数据）进行贝叶斯分析。]

Result: The results show that the interacting model with $Q = \beta H \rho_{de}$ yields a modestly improved fit compared to the non-interacting CPL scenario, as indicated by the Akaike Information Criterion (AIC). However, the Bayesian Information Criterion (BIC) penalizes increased model complexity, leading to a continued preference for $\Lambda$CDM. The interaction model depending on dark matter density does not provide observational support. [结果表明，与非相互作用的CPL情景相比，$Q = \beta H \rho_{de}$ 的相互作用模型在Akaike信息准则（AIC）下显示出适度改善的拟合度。然而，贝叶斯信息准则（BIC）惩罚了模型复杂性的增加，导致对$\Lambda$CDM的持续偏好。依赖于暗物质密度的相互作用模型没有得到观测支持。]

Conclusion: The conclusion is that interacting dark energy models within the CPL framework can introduce more diverse phenomenology while maintaining consistency with current observations. The preferred interacting scenario indicates a dynamic evolution of the dark energy equation of state, transitioning from an effective phantom regime at high redshift to quintessence-like behavior at late times. [结论是，在CPL框架内的相互作用暗能量模型可以在保持与当前观测一致的同时引入更多样化的现象学。首选的相互作用情景表明暗能量状态方程的动态演化，从高红移时的有效幻影态转变为晚期的精质类行为。]

Abstract: This paper examines interacting dark energy models within the Chevallier-Polarski-Linder (CPL) parametrization, emphasizing both theoretical structure and observational viability. Two commonly adopted interaction terms are considered: $Q = βH ρ_{de}$ and $Q = βH ρ_c$. We derive exact analytic solutions that describe how the dark sector evolves. These solutions involve incomplete gamma functions and reveal a non-trivial mathematical structure that is often missed in numerical analyses. We perform a Bayesian analysis using current cosmological observations, including the Hubble parameter (OHD), Type Ia supernovae (SNIa), baryon acoustic oscillations (BAO), and cosmic microwave background (CMB) data. Relative to the non-interacting CPL scenario, the interacting model with $Q = βH ρ_{de}$ yields a modestly improved fit, as indicated by the Akaike Information Criterion (AIC). However, the Bayesian Information Criterion (BIC) penalizes increased model complexity, leading to a continued preference for $Λ$CDM. In contrast, the interaction model that depends on dark matter density does not provide observational support. The preferred interacting scenario indicates that the dark energy equation of state evolves dynamically, transitioning from an effective phantom regime at high redshift to quintessence-like behavior at late times. Further analysis indicates the potential for a transient phase of cosmic acceleration in the future. These findings suggest that interacting dark energy models within the CPL framework enrich the standard cosmological model by introducing more diverse phenomenology while maintaining consistency with current observations.

### [72] [Parametric Resonance in $φ^4$ Preheating: An Exact Numerical Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23224)
*Hrisikesh Thakur,Malay K. Nandy*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper investigates the parametric resonance in the $\phi^4$ chaotic inflationary model during preheating using a fully numerical approach, revealing complex and coupling-dependent resonance patterns that differ from previous approximate analytical treatments.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to provide a more accurate and detailed understanding of the parametric resonance during the preheating phase in the $\phi^4$ chaotic inflationary model. The authors aim to avoid the approximations commonly used in earlier studies by performing a fully numerical analysis of the coupled dynamical equations governing the inflaton field and the mode function of the produced particles.

本文的动机是提供对$\phi^4$混沌暴胀模型在预加热阶段参数共振现象的更准确和详细的理解。作者希望通过完全数值分析来避免以往研究中常用的近似方法，从而更精确地理解标量场和产生粒子模式函数的耦合动力学方程。

Method: The method employed in this paper involves a fully numerical analysis of the coupled dynamical equations governing the inflaton field and the mode function of the produced particles. This approach avoids the approximations typically used in earlier studies and allows for a more precise and detailed examination of the parametric resonance during the preheating phase.

本文采用的方法是对控制inflaton场和产生粒子模式函数的耦合动力学方程进行完全数值分析。这种方法避免了早期研究中通常使用的近似方法，能够更精确和详细地考察预加热阶段的参数共振。

Result: The results reveal that the resonance patterns are significantly different from those obtained with approximate analytical treatments. In the weak coupling regime, short-wavelength modes quickly settle into oscillations with nearly constant amplitude, while long-wavelength modes show gradual amplitude growth. As the coupling strength increases, the dynamics become increasingly nonlinear, leading to stochastic behavior. In the strong coupling regime, short-wavelength modes exhibit a step-like (staircase) evolution in the occupation number, while long-wavelength modes show a more gradual, monotonic growth with small superimposed fluctuations.

结果表明，共振模式与通过近似解析处理得到的结果有显著不同。在弱耦合状态下，短波长模式迅速进入振幅几乎恒定的振荡，而长波长模式则显示出逐渐增长的振幅。随着耦合强度的增加，动力学变得越来越非线性，导致随机行为的出现。在强耦合状态下，短波长模式在占据数上表现出阶梯状（楼梯状）的演化，而长波长模式则显示出更为渐进、单调的增长，并伴有小幅度叠加波动。

Conclusion: The findings highlight the rich, coupling-dependent structure of parametric resonance in the quartic inflationary model and emphasize the importance of exact numerical treatment in accurately capturing preheating dynamics. These results suggest that the use of fully numerical methods is essential for a comprehensive understanding of the preheating process and its implications for cosmology.

这些发现突出了四次方暴胀模型中参数共振的丰富且依赖于耦合强度的结构，并强调了精确数值处理在准确捕捉预加热动力学中的重要性。这些结果表明，使用完全数值方法对于全面理解预加热过程及其对宇宙学的影响至关重要。

Abstract: Preheating after inflation proceeds through parametric resonance, leading to efficient particle production in scalar field models. In this work, we investigate the structure of parametric resonance in the $φ^4$ chaotic inflationary model during the preheating phase by performing a fully numerical analysis of the coupled dynamical equations governing the inflaton field and the mode function of the produced particles, thereby avoiding the approximations commonly employed in earlier studies. Our results reveal resonance patterns that differ significantly from those obtained with approximate analytical treatments. In the weak coupling regime, short-wavelength modes rapidly settle into oscillations with nearly constant amplitude, while the corresponding occupation numbers approach saturation. However, the long-wavelength modes exhibit gradual amplitude growth, with occupation numbers transitioning into a non-linear oscillatory regime. As the coupling strength increases, the dynamics becomes increasingly nonlinear, leading to the emergence of stochastic behavior. In the strong coupling regime, short-wavelength modes display a step-like (staircase) evolution in the occupation number, indicative of intermittent bursts of particle production. However, the long-wavelength modes exhibit a more gradual, monotonic growth with small superimposed fluctuations. These findings highlight the rich, coupling-dependent, structure of parametric resonance in the quartic inflationary model and underscore the importance of exact numerical treatment in accurately capturing preheating dynamics.

### [73] [Testing Scalar Field Dark Matter models in M31 galaxy through the Rotation Curve analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23353)
*Gulnara Suliyeva,Kuantay Boshkayev,Talgar Konysbayev,Yergali Kurmanov,Guldana Rabigulova*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper analyzes the rotation curve of the Andromeda galaxy (M31) using scalar field dark matter models, including fuzzy dark matter, Bose-Einstein condensate, and multistate scalar-field dark matter. It finds that a two-bulge baryonic configuration provides a better statistical description of M31's rotation curve, and smooth cored halos like FDM are more consistent with the observed kinematics.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to investigate the viability of scalar field dark matter halo models by analyzing the rotation curve of the Andromeda galaxy (M31). The study aims to provide a realistic description of the baryonic structure and evaluate different dark matter halo models.

Method: The method involves constructing a mass model for M31, which includes a stellar disk described by the Freeman profile and two alternative bulge configurations: a classical single de Vaucouleurs bulge and a two-component structure consisting of inner and main bulges modeled by exponential sphere profiles. The dark matter halo is modeled using three scalar field motivated models: fuzzy dark matter (FDM), Bose-Einstein condensate, and multistate scalar-field dark matter. The model parameters are determined through the Levenberg-Marquardt nonlinear least-squares fitting, and the relative performance of the models is evaluated using the Bayesian Information Criterion (BIC).

方法涉及构建M31的质量模型，其中包括由Freeman剖面描述的恒星盘和两种替代的核球配置：经典的单de Vaucouleurs核球和由指数球剖面建模的内核球和主核球组成的双组分结构。暗物质晕模型使用三种受标量场启发的模型：模糊暗物质（FDM）、玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚态和多态标量场暗物质。模型参数通过Levenberg-Marquardt非线性最小二乘拟合确定，并使用贝叶斯信息准则（BIC）评估模型的相对性能。

Result: The results show that the two-bulge baryonic configuration provides a better statistical description of the M31 rotation curve, independently of the adopted halo model. Additionally, within the scalar field dark matter scenarios, smooth cored halos, such as FDM, provide the most consistent description of the M31 kinematics.

结果表明，无论采用哪种晕模型，双核球重子配置都能更好地统计描述M31的旋转曲线。此外，在标量场暗物质场景中，如FDM这样的平滑核晕提供了与M31运动学最一致的描述。

Conclusion: The study concludes that a two-bulge baryonic configuration enhances the statistical fit of the M31 rotation curve, and smooth cored halos, particularly FDM, are more consistent with the observed kinematics of M31 within the context of scalar field dark matter models.

研究表明，双核球重子配置提高了M31旋转曲线的统计拟合度，在标量场暗物质模型的背景下，特别是FDM这样的平滑核晕与观测到的M31运动学更为一致。

Abstract: We explore the viability of scalar field dark matter halo models through the rotation curve analysis of the Andromeda galaxy (M31), taking into account a realistic description of its baryonic structure. The mass model includes a stellar disk described by the Freeman profile and two alternative bulge configurations: a classical single de Vaucouleurs bulge and a two-component structure consisting of inner and main bulges modeled by exponential sphere profiles. The dark matter halo is modeled using three scalar field motivated models: fuzzy dark matter (FDM), Bose-Einstein condensate and multistate scalar-field dark matter. The model parameters are determined through the Levenberg-Marquardt nonlinear least-squares fitting, and the relative performance of the models is evaluated using the Bayesian Information Criterion which allows a direct comparison with previous phenomenological halo studies performed for the same galaxy. We find that the two-bulge baryonic configuration ensures a better statistical description of the M31 rotation curve, independently of the adopted halo model. The results also suggest that, within scalar field dark matter scenarios, smooth cored halos, such as FDM, provide the most consistent description of the M31 kinematics.

TL;DR: The paper explores the ability of Scalar-Tensor-Vector Gravity (STVG-MOG) to explain the inverse-square force law at cluster scales, as inferred from kinematic Sunyaev-Zeldovich (kSZ) measurements. Using parameters from the X-COP cluster fit, the authors show that STVG-MOG can account for the observed Newtonian behavior and kSZ data without invoking dark matter, and the results are consistent across cluster and cosmological scales.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to test if STVG-MOG, a modified gravity theory, can explain the observed inverse-square force law in galaxy clusters, as suggested by recent kSZ measurements, without the need for dark matter. The goal is to see if the same set of parameters that describe cluster dynamics can also be extrapolated to explain the kSZ data on larger scales.

Method: The method involves using the X-COP cluster fit parameters, which include a baryonic cluster mass $M\sim 10^{15}M_\odot$, and parameters $\alpha\sim 9.11$ and $\mu\sim 0.196~{\rm Mpc}^{-1}$, to model the gravitational acceleration in STVG-MOG. The authors then extrapolate this model to the separation range relevant for kSZ analysis, where the Yukawa transition length $\mu^{-1}\simeq 5.1~{\rm Mpc}$ is much smaller than the separations. This allows the STVG-MOG acceleration law to reduce to an effective inverse-square form, and the corresponding pairwise velocity curve is derived and compared with the kSZ data.

Result: The result is that the STVG-MOG model, with the parameters from the X-COP cluster fit, can reproduce the trend of the kSZ data after fitting a single overall kSZ amplitude. This indicates that the model can account for the observed Newtonian behavior at cluster scales and is consistent with the kSZ data on cosmological scales, without the need for dark matter.

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the X-COP cluster fit and the kSZ force-law result are mutually consistent within the framework of STVG-MOG. This suggests that STVG-MOG can provide a viable alternative to dark matter in explaining the observed gravitational effects in galaxy clusters and on cosmological scales.

Abstract: We investigate whether Scalar-Tensor-Vector Gravity in its weak-field modified gravity form can account for the cluster-scale inverse-square force law inferred from recent kinematic Sunyaev-Zeldovich measurements of cluster pairwise motions. The starting point is the X-COP cluster fit of STVG-MOG, for which a representative baryonic cluster mass $M\sim 10^{15}M_\odot$ together with parameters $α\sim 9.11$ and $μ\sim 0.196~{\rm Mpc}^{-1}$ provides a successful description of cluster dynamics without particle dark matter. We extrapolate this fit to the separation range $30$ to $230~{\rm Mpc}$, relevant for the pairwise kSZ analysis. Since the Yukawa transition length $μ^{-1}\simeq 5.1~{\rm Mpc}$ is much smaller than these separations, the STVG-MOG acceleration law reduces to an effective inverse-square form. This explains why the theory can satisfy the observed Newtonian behavior while remaining distinct from MOND-like long-distance modifications. We derive the corresponding pairwise velocity curve and show that, after fitting a single overall kSZ amplitude, the extrapolated STVG-MOG prediction reproduces the measured trend of the pairwise kSZ data. The analysis shows that the X-COP cluster fit and the cosmological-scale kSZ force-law result are mutually consistent within STVG-MOG.

### [75] [The open-Universe signal: A model artifact rather than genuine curvature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23492)
*Peng-Ju Wu*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper re-examines the spatial curvature of the Universe using recent observational data, finding a preference for an open Universe in $\Lambda$CDM, but this preference vanishes in extended models. The authors conclude that the open-Universe signal is likely due to model inflexibility rather than a true feature of the late Universe.

该论文使用最近的观测数据重新检查了宇宙的空间曲率，在$\Lambda$冷暗物质模型中发现了一个开放宇宙的偏好，但在扩展模型中这种偏好消失了。作者认为，开放宇宙的信号很可能是由于模型灵活性不足，而不是晚期宇宙的真实特征。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: Within the $\Lambda$CDM paradigm, the combined data prefer an open Universe with $\Omega_K = 0.049 \pm 0.037$. However, in extensions to $\Lambda$CDM, the data favor a flat Universe. 在$\Lambda$CDM范式中，综合数据倾向于一个具有$\Omega_K = 0.049 \pm 0.037$的开放宇宙。然而，在$\Lambda$CDM的扩展模型中，数据更倾向于平坦宇宙。模型比较表明，在$\Lambda$CDM中引入新物理比允许空间曲率更受青睐，而且平坦的$\Lambda$CDM扩展模型比其弯曲的对应模型表现更好。

Conclusion: The mild open-Universe signal observed in the $\Lambda$CDM paradigm is likely an artifact of limited model flexibility. Extended models, which allow for new physics, favor a flat Universe and perform better than their curved counterparts. This suggests that the open-Universe signal is not a genuine feature of late-Universe observations.

在$\Lambda$CDM范式中观察到的轻微开放宇宙信号很可能是由于模型灵活性不足而产生的伪影。允许新物理的扩展模型更倾向于平坦宇宙，并且比其弯曲的对应模型表现更好。这表明开放宇宙的信号并不是晚期宇宙观测的真实特征。

Abstract: Recent late-Universe observations suggest an open Universe. If confirmed, such a departure from spatial flatness would carry profound implications for our understanding of cosmic inflation and the ultimate fate of the Universe. Motivated by this intriguing result and the release of new data, we revisit the question using baryon acoustic oscillation measurements from DESI DR2, multiple Type Ia supernova samples, refined strong gravitational lensing time-delay analyses, and the most up-to-date cosmic chronometer data. We find that within the $Λ$ cold dark matter ($Λ$CDM) paradigm, the combined data still prefer an open Universe with $Ω_K=0.049\pm0.037$. However, this preference vanishes in extensions to $Λ$CDM, where the data instead favor a flat Universe. The model comparison shows that for $Λ$CDM, introducing new physics is preferred over merely allowing spatial curvature, and flat $Λ$CDM extensions perform better than their curved counterparts. We therefore argue that the mild open-Universe signal is an artifact of limited model flexibility, rather than a genuine feature of late-Universe observations.

### [76] [CLASH-VLT: The Fifth Force in Chameleon Gravity from Joint Lensing and Kinematics Cluster Mass Profiles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23631)
*Lorenzo Pizzuti,Federico Rivano,Keiichi Umetsu,Andrea Biviano*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper presents a high-precision analysis of nine massive galaxy clusters to test chameleon screening gravity and its $f(R)$ subclass, using three mass profile models. The results, when assuming NFW or Hernquist profiles, are consistent with General Relativity (GR) and provide tight constraints on modified gravity parameters. A Burkert profile leads to a mild departure from GR. For the $f(R)$ case, the bounds on the scalaron field are in agreement with current cosmological constraints.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to test chameleon screening gravity and its $f(R)$ subclass at Mpc scales using joint gravitational-lensing and kinematic analysis of galaxy clusters. This is important for understanding the nature of gravity and dark energy, and for placing constraints on modified gravity theories beyond General Relativity (GR).

Method: The authors use a high-precision joint gravitational-lensing and kinematic analysis of nine massive galaxy clusters from the CLASH and CLASH-VLT surveys. They adopt three different total cluster mass profile models: Navarro--Frenk--White (NFW), Burkert, and Hernquist. The analysis involves constraining the coupling constant $\mathcal{Q}$ and the background chameleon field $\varphi_\infty$ in the general chameleon framework, and the scalaron field $f_R$ in the $f(R)$ sub-case. The impact of systematics in the kinematical analysis is also investigated.

Result: When assuming NFW or Hernquist profiles, the combined constraints from the nine clusters are fully consistent with General Relativity (GR), providing one of the tightest bounds on general chameleon models with clusters to date. For the $f(R)$ sub-case, the bound on the background scalaron field is $|f_R| \lesssim 2-5 \times 10^{-5}$ (95\% C.L.) for NFW and Hernquist models, in agreement with current constraints at cosmological scales. Adopting a Burkert profile leads to a mild ($\sim 2\sigma$) departure from the GR expectation in joint analysis, with an apparent deviation from standard gravity of $\log_{10}|f_R| = -4.7 \pm 1.2$.

Conclusion: The study provides strong constraints on chameleon screening gravity and its $f(R)$ subclass using galaxy clusters, supporting the consistency of General Relativity (GR) with observations. The results highlight the importance of the choice of mass profile model in such analyses. Future wide-field lensing surveys and spectroscopic follow-up programs will enable similar analyses on larger samples, potentially leading to even tighter constraints on gravity and the dark sector.

Abstract: We present a high-precision joint gravitational-lensing and kinematic analysis of nine massive galaxy clusters from the CLASH and CLASH-VLT surveys to test chameleon screening gravity and its $f(R)$ sub-class at Mpc scales. We investigate the dependence on the assumed parametrization of the total cluster mass profile by adopting three models, namely Navarro--Frenk--White (NFW), Burkert, and Hernquist. When cuspy models (NFW or Hernquist) are assumed in the general chameleon framework, the combined constraints from the nine clusters are fully consistent with General Relativity (GR), excluding large regions of the modified-gravity parameter space (the coupling constant $\mathcal{Q}$ and the background chameleon field $ φ_\infty$), providing one of the tightest bounds on general chameleon models with clusters to date. In contrast, adopting a Burkert profile -- disfavored by lensing data -- leads to a mild ($\sim 2σ$) departure from the GR expectation in joint analysis. When considering the $f(R)$ sub-case, we obtain a bound on the background scalaron field of $|f_R| \lesssim \mathrm{2-5}\times 10^{-5}$ (95\% C.L.) for NFW and Hernquist models, in agreement with current constraints at cosmological scales, and an apparent deviation from standard gravity of $\log_{10}|f_R| = -4.7 \pm 1.2$ for the Burkert case. We investigate the impact of systematics in the kinematical analysis, showing that the tension is mitigated when clusters exhibiting clear dynamical disturbance are excluded from the sample. [...[ The upcoming generation of wide-field lensing surveys and spectroscopic follow-up programs will enable similar analyses on substantially larger samples, offering the prospect of tightening cluster-based constraints on gravity and the dark sector.

### [77] [Reconstructing the cosmic expansion with a generalized q(z) parameterization: A decelerating Universe from late-time constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23992)
*Tomás Verdugo,Alberto Hernández-Almada,Miguel A. García-Aspeitia,Juan Magaña,Verónica Motta*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper introduces a generalized parameterization of the deceleration parameter $q(z)$, incorporating an effective radiative component (ERC) and a localized late-time contribution. The model is constrained using observational data from various sources, resulting in a currently accelerating Universe with a transition redshift earlier than in the $\Lambda$CDM model. The ERC ensures smooth evolution of $q(z)$, $j(z)$, and $w_{\rm eff}(z)$, and the model suggests a possible reduction of the late-time acceleration.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to extend the existing two-parameter reconstructions of the deceleration parameter $q(z)$ by incorporating an effective radiative component (ERC). This new framework aims to regulate the high-redshift behavior while preserving the late-time transition dynamics. The goal is to explore the possibility of a reduced late-time acceleration and to provide a more controlled extension toward early epochs.

本文的动机是通过引入一个有效辐射成分（ERC）来扩展现有的两参数减速参数$q(z)$重构。这个新框架旨在调节高红移行为，同时保持晚期过渡动力学。目标是探索晚期加速减少的可能性，并为早期宇宙提供更受控的扩展。

Method: The authors propose a generalized phenomenological parameterization of the deceleration parameter $q(z)$ that includes an effective radiative component (ERC) and a localized late-time contribution. The free parameters $(h, q_0, z_c, z_e)$ are constrained using observational data from cosmic chronometers (CC), Pantheon+ Type Ia supernovae (SNIa), H\,\textsc{ii} galaxies (HIIG), and intermediate-luminosity quasars (QSO). The method involves fitting the model to these data sets to obtain the best-fit values for the parameters.

作者提出了一种广义现象学参数化方法，用于描述减速参数$q(z)$，该方法包括有效辐射成分（ERC）和局部晚期贡献。自由参数$(h, q_0, z_c, z_e)$使用来自宇宙时钟（CC）、Pantheon+ Ia型超新星（SNIa）、H\,\textsc{ii}星系（HIIG）和中等亮度类星体（QSO）的观测数据进行约束。该方法涉及将模型拟合到这些数据集以获得参数的最佳拟合值。

Result: The analysis of the full data combination (CC+SNIa+HIIG+QSO) yields $q_0 = -0.25^{+0.04}_{-0.04}$ and a transition redshift $z_T \simeq 0.80$, indicating a currently accelerating Universe with a transition occurring earlier than in the $\Lambda$CDM model. The Hubble parameter is found to be $h = 0.729 \pm 0.006$. The ERC remains weakly constrained but ensures a smooth and monotonic evolution of $q(z)$, $j(z)$, and $w_{\rm eff}(z)$ across a wide redshift range. The results suggest a possible reduction of the late-time acceleration compared to the $\Lambda$CDM model.

对全部数据组合（CC+SNIa+HIIG+QSO）的分析得到$q_0 = -0.25^{+0.04}_{-0.04}$和过渡红移$z_T \simeq 0.80$，表明当前宇宙正在加速膨胀，且过渡发生的时间比$\Lambda$CDM模型早。哈勃参数为$h = 0.729 \pm 0.006$。尽管ERC受到的约束较弱，但它确保了$q(z)$、$j(z)$和$w_{\rm eff}(z)$在广泛的红移范围内平滑且单调的演化。结果表明，与$\Lambda$CDM模型相比，晚期加速可能有所减少。

Conclusion: The proposed parameterization of the deceleration parameter $q(z)$, which includes an effective radiative component (ERC), provides a more controlled extension toward early epochs and suggests a possible reduction of the late-time acceleration. The model is consistent with current low- and intermediate-redshift observational data, indicating a currently accelerating Universe with a transition redshift earlier than in the $\Lambda$CDM model. The ERC ensures a smooth and monotonic evolution of the relevant cosmological parameters.

提出的包含有效辐射成分（ERC）的减速参数$q(z)$参数化方法，为早期宇宙提供了更受控的扩展，并表明晚期加速可能有所减少。该模型与当前低红移和中红移观测数据一致，表明当前宇宙正在加速膨胀，且过渡发生的时间比$\Lambda$CDM模型早。ERC确保了相关宇宙学参数的平滑且单调的演化。

Abstract: We present a generalized phenomenological parameterization of the deceleration parameter $q(z)$ that incorporates an effective radiative component (ERC) in addition to a localized late-time contribution. The proposed framework extends previous two-parameter $q(z)$ reconstructions by explicitly regulating the high-redshift behavior while preserving the late-time transition dynamics. We constrain the free parameters $(h, q_0, z_c, z_e)$ using late-time observational data from cosmic chronometers (CC), Pantheon+ Type Ia supernovae (SNIa), H\,\textsc{ii} galaxies (HIIG), and intermediate-luminosity quasars (QSO). For the full data combination (CC+SNIa+HIIG+QSO), we obtain $q_0 = -0.25^{+0.04}_{-0.04}$ and a transition redshift $z_T \simeq 0.80$, indicating a currently accelerating Universe with a transition occurring earlier than in the $Λ$CDM model. Within the redshift range probed by the data, the reconstructed $q(z)$ deviates from the $Λ$CDM trend, suggesting a possible reduction of the late-time acceleration. Furthermore, the reconstruction favors a relatively high value of the Hubble parameter, $h = 0.729 \pm 0.006$. The ERC remains weakly constrained by late-time data but ensures a smooth and monotonic evolution of $q(z)$, $j(z)$, and $w_{\rm eff}(z)$ across a wide redshift range. Within the observed interval, the model effectively reproduces the late-time behavior of the previous parametrization, while providing a controlled extension toward early epochs. Our results show that current low- and intermediate-redshift data are compatible with a reduced late-time acceleration.

### [78] [A sound-horizon-free measurement of the Hubble constant from DESI DR2 baryon acoustic oscillations using artificial neural networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24050)
*Gaurav N. Gadbail,Kazuharu Bamba*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: A model-independent and sound-horizon-free measurement of the Hubble constant $H_0$ is achieved using baryon acoustic oscillation tracers from DESI DR2, combined with Type Ia supernovae and cosmic chronometers. The method uses an artificial neural network for data-driven function reconstructions, avoiding $\Lambda$CDM prior dependence. The result, $H_0 = 71.5\pm2.2$ km s$^{-1}$ Mpc$^{-1}$, is consistent with other measurements and supports the Hubble tension.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to provide a robust and independent measurement of the Hubble constant $H_0$ that is free from the assumptions and priors typically used in cosmological models, such as the sound horizon scale or the absolute luminosity of Type Ia supernovae. This is important to address the Hubble tension, which is the discrepancy between local and CMB-inferred values of $H_0$.

动机是提供一个鲁棒且独立的哈勃常数 $H_0$ 测量，该测量不依赖于通常在宇宙学模型中使用的假设和先验，如声视界尺度或Ia型超新星的绝对光度。这对于解决哈勃张力（即局部测量值与CMB推断值之间的差异）非常重要。

Method: The method involves using baryon acoustic oscillation (BAO) tracers from the Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument (DESI) Data Release 2, combined with Type Ia supernovae and cosmic chronometer data. The function reconstructions are performed using an artificial neural network (ANN), which is a completely data-driven approach. This method avoids the mild $\Lambda$CDM prior dependence and does not require knowledge of the sound horizon scale $r_d$ or any assumption about the absolute luminosity of SNe Ia.

方法涉及使用来自暗能量光谱仪（DESI）数据发布2的重子声波振荡（BAO）示踪器，结合Ia型超新星和宇宙时钟数据。函数重构使用人工神经网络（ANN）进行，这是一种完全数据驱动的方法。这种方法避免了对$\Lambda$CDM先验的轻微依赖，也不需要了解声视界尺度 $r_d$ 或对Ia型超新星绝对光度的任何假设。

Result: The joint constraint on the Hubble constant $H_0$ obtained from the combination of BAO, Type Ia supernovae, and cosmic chronometers is $H_0 = 71.5 \pm 2.2$ km s$^{-1}$ Mpc$^{-1}$ at 68% confidence level. This result is consistent with the TRGB and SH0ES measurements within $0.6\sigma$, and with the Planck 2020 result within $2\sigma$. The higher value of $H_0$ compared to the Planck CMB inference adds independent support for the reality of the Hubble tension.

从BAO、Ia型超新星和宇宙时钟的组合中获得的哈勃常数 $H_0$ 的联合约束为 $H_0 = 71.5 \pm 2.2$ km s$^{-1}$ Mpc$^{-1}$，置信水平为68%。这一结果在$0.6\sigma$内与TRGB和SH0ES测量一致，在$2\sigma$内与Planck 2020结果一致。与Planck CMB推断相比，$H_0$的较高值为哈勃张力的真实性提供了独立的支持。

Conclusion: The study provides a model-independent and sound-horizon-free measurement of the Hubble constant $H_0$ using a data-driven approach based on an artificial neural network. The result, $H_0 = 71.5 \pm 2.2$ km s$^{-1}$ Mpc$^{-1}$, is consistent with other recent measurements and supports the existence of the Hubble tension, adding to the growing body of evidence for new physics beyond the standard $\Lambda$CDM model.

研究使用基于人工神经网络的数据驱动方法，提供了独立于模型且无声视界的哈勃常数 $H_0$ 测量。结果 $H_0 = 71.5 \pm 2.2$ km s$^{-1}$ Mpc$^{-1}$ 与其他最近的测量结果一致，并支持哈勃张力的存在，为超出标准$\Lambda$CDM模型的新物理提供了越来越多的证据。

Abstract: We present a model-independent, sound-horizon-free measurement of the Hubble constant $H_0$ using baryon acoustic oscillation tracers from the Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument Data Release 2. The function reconstructions are performed using the artificial neural network method, which is a completely data-driven approach that avoids the mild $Λ$CDM prior dependence. Our approach is based on the distance duality relation and combines three complementary observational probes, such as Type Ia supernovae, cosmic chronometer, and DESI DR2 BAO -- without requiring any knowledge of the sound horizon scale $r_d$ or any assumption about the absolute luminosity of SNe Ia. We obtain a joint constraint of $H_0 = 71.5\pm2.2$ km s$^{-1}$ Mpc$^{-1}$ at 68\% confidence for 1000 bootstrap realisations and 4096 neurons, which is consistent with the TRGB result and the SH0ES measurement within $0.6σ$, consistent with the Planck 2020 result within $2σ$. Our results favor a higher value of $H_0$ compared to the Planck CMB inference, adding independent support for the reality of the Hubble tension.

### [79] [The Tracking Tapered Gridded Estimator for the 21-cm power spectrum from the Murchison Widefield Array (MWA) drift scan observations -- III. Improved upper limits at $z = 8.2$ from multiple pointings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24144)
*Shouvik Sarkar,Khandakar Md Asif Elahi,Samir Choudhuri,Somnath Bharadwaj,Suman Chatterjee,Baijayanta Bhattacharyya,Shiv Sethi,Akash Kumar Patwa*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper analyzes MWA drift scan observations, focusing on angular brightness temperature fluctuations and their implications for Epoch of Reionization (EoR) studies. The best 2σ upper limit on the 21-cm brightness temperature fluctuations is given, and a tighter upper limit is obtained by incoherently combining multiple pointing centers.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to study the mean-squared angular brightness temperature fluctuations, $D_{\\ell}$, from Murchison Widefield Array (MWA) zenith-pointing drift scan observations. The authors aim to identify the contributions from bright extended sources like Fornax A and point sources, and to determine the best regions for Epoch of Reionization (EoR) science, which are relatively free from foreground contamination. They also seek to place the tightest upper limits on the 21-cm brightness temperature fluctuations, $Δ^2(k)$, using the MWA data.\n\n本文的动机是研究来自默奇森宽视场阵列（Murchison Widefield Array, MWA）天顶指向漂移扫描观测的平均平方角亮度温度波动$D_{\\ell}$。作者旨在识别来自Fornax A等明亮扩展源和点源的贡献，并确定相对不受前景污染影响的最佳宇宙再电离时期（Epoch of Reionization, EoR）科学研究区域。他们还试图使用MWA数据对21厘米亮度温度波动$Δ^2(k)$设置最严格的上限。

Method: The method involves analyzing MWA drift scan observations at a central frequency of $ν_c=154.2 \, {\\rm MHz}$, covering right ascension $349.0^{\\circ} \\le α \\le 70.0^{\\circ}$ with 163 pointing centers (PCs) spaced by $0.5^{\\circ}$. The authors measure the mean-squared angular brightness temperature fluctuations, $D_{\\ell}$, as a function of right ascension, $α$, and interpret the results in terms of contributions from bright sources and Poisson fluctuations from point sources. They also present the mean-squared 21-cm brightness temperature fluctuations, $Δ^2(k)$, as a function of $α$, and identify regions that are relatively free from foreground contamination. Finally, they incoherently combine multiple PCs to obtain tighter upper limits on $Δ^2(k)$.\n\n该方法涉及分析中心频率为$ν_c=154.2 \, {\\rm MHz}$的MWA漂移扫描观测，覆盖赤经$349.0^{\\circ} \\le α \\le 70.0^{\\circ}$，并使用间隔$0.5^{\\circ}$的163个指向中心（pointing centers, PCs）。作者测量了作为赤经$α$函数的平均平方角亮度温度波动$D_{\\ell}$，并根据明亮源和点源的泊松波动解释结果。他们还展示了作为$α$函数的21厘米亮度温度波动$Δ^2(k)$，并确定了相对不受前景污染影响的区域。最后，他们不相干地组合多个PC以获得更严格的$Δ^2(k)$上限。

Result: The results show a broad peak in $D_{\\ell}$ at $α \\approx 50.0^{\\circ}$, corresponding to the bright extended source Fornax A in the main lobe of the primary beam. A smaller peak at $α \\approx 5.0^{\\circ}$ is possibly due to Fornax A in the first sidelobe. For $α \\leq 22.0^{\\circ}$ and $\\ell \\ge 200$, $D_{\\ell} \\propto \\ell^2$, indicating Poisson fluctuations from point sources. The region $358.5^{\\circ} \\leq α \\leq 11.5^{\\circ}$ is found to be relatively foreground-free and best suited for EoR science. The PC at $α = 11.0^{\\circ}$ yields the best $2σ$ upper limit $Δ^2_{\\rm UL}(k) = (173.13)^2\\, {\\rm mK}^2$ at $k = 0.161\\, {\\rm Mpc}^{-1}$. Incoherent combination of 23 PCs gives $Δ^2_{\\rm UL}(k) = (98.67)^2\\, {\\rm mK}^2$ at $k = 0.156\\, {\\rm Mpc}^{-1}$, which is the tightest upper limit from the MWA, but still higher than LOFAR and HERA limits.\n\n结果显示，在$α \\approx 50.0^{\\circ}$处$D_{\\ell}$有一个宽峰，对应于主瓣中的明亮扩展源Fornax A。在$α \\approx 5.0^{\\circ}$处有一个较小的峰值，可能是由于第一旁瓣中的Fornax A造成的。对于$α \\leq 22.0^{\\circ}$和$\\ell \\ge 200$的情况，$D_{\\ell} \\propto \\ell^2$，表明点源的泊松波动。发现区域$358.5^{\\circ} \\leq α \\leq 11.5^{\\circ}$相对不受前景污染影响，最适合进行EoR科学研究。$α = 11.0^{\\circ}$的指向中心给出了最佳的$2σ$上限$Δ^2_{\\rm UL}(k) = (173.13)^2\\, {\\rm mK}^2$，对应$k = 0.161\\, {\\rm Mpc}^{-1}$。不相干地组合23个指向中心得到$k = 0.156\\, {\\rm Mpc}^{-1}$时的$Δ^2_{\\rm UL}(k) = (98.67)^2\\, {\\rm mK}^2$，这是MWA给出的最严格上限，但仍高于LOFAR和HERA的限制。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the MWA drift scan observations provide valuable insights into the angular brightness temperature fluctuations and their implications for EoR studies. The identified foreground-free regions and the tighter upper limits on $Δ^2(k)$, especially when incoherently combining multiple PCs, are significant steps towards detecting the 21-cm signal from the EoR. However, the current upper limits are still several orders of magnitude above theoretical predictions, indicating the need for further improvements in sensitivity and foreground subtraction techniques.\n\n结论是MWA漂移扫描观测提供了关于角亮度温度波动及其对EoR研究意义的宝贵见解。所确定的无前景污染区域以及$Δ^2(k)$的更严格上限，尤其是在不相干地组合多个指向中心时，是朝着探测EoR的21厘米信号迈出的重要一步。然而，当前的上限仍比理论预测高出几个数量级，这表明需要进一步提高灵敏度和前景扣除技术。

Abstract: We analyze zenith-pointing $(δ=-26.7^{\circ})$ Murchison Widefield Array (MWA) $ν_c=154.2 \,{\rm MHz}$ drift scan observations covering $349.0^{\circ} \le α\le 70.0^{\circ}$ with 163 pointing centers (PCs) spaced by $0.5^{\circ}$. We measure $D_{\ell}$, the mean-squared angular brightness temperature fluctuations, as a function of $α$. A broad peak at $α\approx 50.0^{\circ}$ corresponds to the bright extended source Fornax~A in the main lobe of the primary beam. A smaller peak at $α\approx 5.0^{\circ}$ possibly corresponds to Fornax~A in the first sidelobe. For $α\leq 22.0^{\circ}$ and $\ell \ge 200$, we find $D_{\ell} \propto \ell^2$, which we interpret as Poisson fluctuations from point sources. We present $Δ^2(k)$, the mean-squared 21-cm brightness temperature fluctuations from the Epoch of Reionization, as a function of $α$. Fornax~A causes strong contamination near $α\approx 50.5^{\circ}$, elsewhere several PCs are consistent with noise. The range $358.5^{\circ} \leq α\leq 11.5^{\circ}$ is relatively foreground-free and best suited for EoR science. The PC at $α= 11.0^{\circ}$ yields the best $2σ$ upper limit $Δ^{2}_{\rm UL}(k) = (173.13)^{2}\,{\rm mK^{2}}$ at $k = 0.161\,{\rm Mpc^{-1}}$. We incoherently combine $23$ PCs to obtain $Δ_{\rm UL}^2(k)=(98.67)^{2}\,{\rm mK}^{2}$ at $k=0.156\,{\rm Mpc}^{-1}$. This is the tightest upper limit from the MWA, being $\approx3$ times lower than earlier MWA limits, but $\approx2$ and $\approx21$ times higher than the LOFAR and HERA limits, respectively, and $\approx3$ orders of magnitude above theoretical predictions.

### [80] [The Three Hundred project: cosmic web identification from 2D gas and Compton-$y$ maps of galaxy clusters outskirts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24200)
*Sara Santoni,Marco De Petris,Gustavo Yepes,Weiguang Cui,Daniel de Andrés,Antonio Ferragamo,Raphaël Wicker*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper evaluates the reliability of reconstructing the cosmic web from 2D observational data, particularly using the Sunyaev-Zel'dovich (SZ) effect, and compares it with the underlying 3D network. The study finds that 2D maps provide a good representation of the 3D networks, with minor underestimation in connectivity, and that gas outside galaxy clusters is predominantly found in filamentary structures, contributing significantly to the Compton-$y$ parameter.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to assess the accuracy and limitations of reconstructing the cosmic web from 2D observational data, specifically focusing on the effects of 2D projection and the use of the SZ effect as a tracer. This is important for understanding the environment of galaxy clusters and their connection to the larger cosmic web.

本文的动机是评估从二维观测数据重建宇宙网的准确性和局限性，特别关注二维投影的影响以及使用SZ效应作为示踪剂的效果。这对于理解星系团的环境及其与更大的宇宙网的连接非常重要。

Method: The method involves using the DisPerSE filament finder to reconstruct the filamentary networks in the outskirts of The Three Hundred simulated clusters. The authors first extract the networks from 2D gas distributions and compare them with the 3D networks projected along the line of sight. They also identify filaments from simulated Compton-$y$ maps and compare these with the 2D gas networks. Distances between corresponding skeletons are computed, and the contribution of filamentary structures to the integrated Compton-$y$ parameter is evaluated.

该方法涉及使用DisPerSE细丝查找器来重建The Three Hundred模拟星系团外围的细丝网络。作者首先从二维气体分布中提取网络，并将其与沿视线投影的三维网络进行比较。他们还从模拟的Compton-$y$图中识别出细丝，并将其与二维气体网络进行比较。计算了相应骨架之间的距离，并评估了细丝结构对集成Compton-$y$参数的贡献。

Result: The results show that the 2D maps provide a good representation of the 3D networks, with a median distance of approximately $0.22 \, h^{-1}$ Mpc between the spines of the 2D and projected 3D networks. The connectivity derived from the 2D networks is slightly underestimated. There is a good spatial agreement between the gas and SZ networks, with a median distance of $\approx 0.24 \, h^{-1}$ Mpc. Gas outside galaxy clusters is preferentially located in filamentary structures, which contribute $\sim 80\%$ of the integrated Compton-$Y$ parameter of clusters' outskirts.

结果表明，二维地图很好地代表了三维网络，二维和投影三维网络主干之间的中位距离约为$0.22 \, h^{-1}$ Mpc。从二维网络得出的连通性略有低估。气体网络和SZ网络之间有很好的空间一致性，中位距离为$\approx 0.24 \, h^{-1}$ Mpc。星系团外的气体主要位于细丝结构中，这些结构对星系团外围集成Compton-$Y$参数的贡献约为$\sim 80\%$。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that 2D observational data, particularly the SZ effect, can be used to reliably reconstruct the cosmic web, although there is a slight underestimation in the connectivity. Filamentary structures play a significant role in the distribution of gas outside galaxy clusters, and they contribute substantially to the Compton-$y$ parameter.

结论是，二维观测数据，特别是SZ效应，可以可靠地用于重建宇宙网，尽管在连通性方面略有低估。细丝结构在星系团外气体分布中起着重要作用，并对Compton-$y$参数有显著贡献。

Abstract: Galaxy clusters are located at the nodes of the filamentary network known as the cosmic web. A more comprehensive understanding of galaxy clusters can be achieved by considering their environment, in particular, the filamentary structures to which they are connected. In this work, we aim to assess the reliability of the cosmic web reconstruction from mock observational data. In particular, we aim to quantify the effects of the 2D projection relative to the underlying 3D network and the impact of using the Sunyaev-Zel'dovich (SZ) effect as a tracer of the cosmic web. We reconstruct the filamentary networks in the outskirts of The Three Hundred simulated clusters with the filament finder DisPerSE. First, we extract the networks from the 2D gas distribution and evaluate their purity and completeness with respect to the 3D networks projected along the line of sight. We also compute the distances between the corresponding skeletons. Moreover, we identify filaments from simulated Compton-$y$ maps of the clusters at redshift $z=0$, and we compare them with the 2D gas network. The skeletons extracted from 2D maps provide good representations of the underlying 3D ones, both in terms of critical points and filaments. We find a median distance between the spines of the 2D and projected 3D networks of approximately $0.22 \, h^{-1}$ Mpc, although the connectivity derived from the 2D networks is slightly underestimated. We observe a good spatial agreement between the gas and SZ networks, with a median distance of $\approx 0.24 \, h^{-1}$ Mpc. Finally, we show that gas outside galaxy clusters is preferentially located in filamentary structures, which contribute $\sim 80\%$ of the integrated Compton-$Y$ parameter of clusters' outskirts.

### [81] [The FLAMINGO simulations data release](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24324)
*John C. Helly,Robert J. McGibbon,Joop Schaye,Matthieu Schaller,William McDonald,Joey Braspenning,Jeger C. Broxterman,Emily E. Costello,Willem Elbers,Carlos S. Frenk,Adrian Jenkins,Roi Kugel,Ian G. McCarthy,Jaime Salcido,Marcel P. van Daalen,Bert Vandenbroucke,Tianyi Yang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The FLAMINGO project has publicly released over 2.3 petabytes of data from a suite of 22 hydrodynamical and 16 gravity-only cosmological simulations, including detailed data products and a web service for selective data access.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation behind the FLAMINGO project is to provide a comprehensive and high-fidelity dataset from a series of cosmological simulations that include a wide range of astrophysical processes such as radiative cooling, star formation, stellar mass loss, chemical enrichment, supernova feedback, and AGN feedback. The simulations also explicitly simulate neutrinos using particles. The data release aims to support a broad range of scientific investigations by providing a variety of data products and making them accessible through a web service.

FLAMINGO 项目的动机是提供一系列宇宙学模拟的全面和高保真数据集，这些模拟包括辐射冷却、恒星形成、恒星质量损失、化学富集、超新星反馈和AGN反馈等一系列天体物理过程。模拟还使用粒子显式地模拟中微子。此次数据发布旨在通过提供多种数据产品并通过网络服务使其可访问，以支持广泛的科学研究。

Method: The FLAMINGO project employs a suite of 22 hydrodynamical simulations and 16 gravity-only simulations. The hydrodynamical simulations include a range of physical processes such as radiative cooling, star formation, stellar mass loss, chemical enrichment, supernova feedback, and two implementations of AGN feedback. Neutrinos are simulated explicitly using particles. The simulations are calibrated to reproduce the present-day galaxy stellar mass function and gas fractions in low-redshift clusters. Additionally, the project includes simulations with varied galaxy stellar mass functions, cluster gas fractions, cosmologies, and dark matter properties. A web service is implemented to enable users to selectively download datasets or parts of datasets.

FLAMINGO 项目采用22个流体动力学模拟和16个纯引力模拟。流体动力学模拟包括辐射冷却、恒星形成、恒星质量损失、化学富集、超新星反馈以及两种AGN反馈实现等物理过程。中微子通过粒子显式模拟。这些模拟经过校准，以再现当今星系的恒星质量函数和低红移星团中的气体分数。此外，该项目还包括具有不同星系恒星质量函数、星团气体分数、宇宙学参数和暗物质性质的模拟。实施了一个网络服务，使用户能够有选择地下载数据集或部分数据集。

Result: The public release of the FLAMINGO project includes over 2.3 petabytes of data from 22 hydrodynamical and 16 gravity-only simulations. Data products consist of snapshots, halo and galaxy catalogues, HEALPix all-sky lightcone maps, particle data for lightcone maps, and power spectra. The fiducial hydrodynamical simulations span three numerical resolutions, each calibrated to match the present-day galaxy stellar mass function and gas fractions in low-redshift clusters. Other simulations vary parameters such as the galaxy stellar mass function, cluster gas fractions, cosmology, and dark matter properties. The release also includes previously unpublished simulations with extra dark matter particles. A web service is provided to facilitate selective data access.

FLAMINGO 项目的公开发布包括来自22个流体动力学和16个纯引力模拟的超过2.3 PB的数据。数据产品包括快照、晕轮和星系目录、HEALPix全天光锥图、光锥图的粒子数据和功率谱。基准流体动力学模拟跨越三种数值分辨率，每种都经过校准以匹配当今星系的恒星质量函数和低红移星团中的气体分数。其他模拟则变化了星系恒星质量函数、星团气体分数、宇宙学参数和暗物质性质等参数。此次发布还包括之前未发布的包含额外暗物质粒子的模拟。提供了一个网络服务以方便选择性数据访问。

Conclusion: The FLAMINGO project represents a significant advancement in the field of cosmological simulations, offering a vast and detailed dataset that encompasses a wide array of astrophysical processes. The inclusion of multiple simulation types, varying parameters, and the provision of a web service for data access make this a valuable resource for researchers in cosmology and astrophysics.

FLAMINGO 项目代表了宇宙学模拟领域的一个重大进展，提供了涵盖广泛天体物理过程的庞大而详细的数据集。包括多种模拟类型、变化参数以及提供的数据访问网络服务，使其成为宇宙学和天体物理学研究者的宝贵资源。

Abstract: We describe the public release of $>2.3$ petabytes of data from the FLAMINGO cosmological simulations. The suite consists of hydrodynamical simulations that include radiative cooling, star formation, stellar mass loss and the resulting chemical enrichment, supernova feedback, and two implementations of AGN feedback. Neutrinos are simulated explicitly using particles. Data products include snapshots, halo and galaxy catalogues, HEALPix all-sky lightcone maps, particle data for lightcone maps, and power spectra. The FLAMINGO set includes 22 hydrodynamical simulations. In addition, there are 16 gravity-only simulations, including the $10080^3$ particles FLAMINGO-10k run, with initial conditions that match those of the corresponding hydrodynamical runs. The fiducial hydrodynamical simulations span three numerical resolutions that have each been calibrated to reproduce the present-day galaxy stellar mass function and gas fractions in low-redshift clusters. Other simulations systematically vary the galaxy stellar mass function, cluster gas fractions, cosmology (including neutrino masses), and/or the nature of dark matter, in volumes of 1Gpc$^3$. The release includes hitherto unpublished simulations that use extra dark matter particles. While we provide a facility for downloading complete simulation outputs, we recognise that for many users this will not be possible due to limited local storage or network bandwidth. We implement a web service that enables users to explore available outputs and selectively download datasets or parts of datasets.

### [82] [Propagating data-driven galaxy redshift distribution uncertainties in 3$\times$2-pt analyses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24425)
*Jaime Ruiz-Zapatero,Qianjun Hang,Yun-Hao Zhang,Benjamin Joachimi,Joe Zuntz,Ian Harrison,Carlos García-García,Alex Malz,Benjamin Stölzner,the LSST Dark Energy Science Collaboration*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper investigates the impact of different models for uncertainties in the radial distribution of galaxies, $\boldsymbol{n}(\boldsymbol{z})$, on Stage-IV 3$\times$2-pt analyses. It finds that PCA models are preferable to simple shift & stretch models, as they provide more accurate constraints on cosmological parameters with a minor increase in computational cost.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Uncertainties in the radial distribution of galaxies, $\boldsymbol{n}(\boldsymbol{z})$, significantly affect the error budget in early Stage-IV galaxy survey analyses. The study aims to evaluate the impact of four different $\boldsymbol{n}(\boldsymbol{z})$ uncertainty models: shifts, shifts & stretches, Gaussian processes (GP), and principal component analysis (PCA). The goal is to determine which model provides the best balance between accuracy and computational efficiency.

星系的径向分布不确定性，$\boldsymbol{n}(\boldsymbol{z})$，显著影响早期Stage-IV星系巡天分析中的误差预算。本研究旨在评估四种不同的$\boldsymbol{n}(\boldsymbol{z})$不确定性模型的影响：平移、平移和拉伸、高斯过程（GP）以及主成分分析（PCA）。目标是确定哪种模型在准确性和计算效率之间提供了最佳平衡。

Method: The study uses ensembles of simulated $\boldsymbol{n}(\boldsymbol{z})$ including stochastic and systematic variations to assess the impact of different uncertainty models. For high-dimensional models like GP and PCA, state-of-the-art gradient-based inference methods and approximate analytical marginalisation schemes are employed. The performance of each model is evaluated in terms of their effect on the constraint of the $S_{\rm 8}$ parameter and the bias in its constituents, $Ω_{\rm m}$ and $σ_{\rm 8}$.

该研究使用包括随机和系统变化的模拟$\boldsymbol{n}(\boldsymbol{z})$集合来评估不同不确定性模型的影响。对于像GP和PCA这样的高维模型，采用最先进的基于梯度的推理方法和近似的解析边缘化方案。每个模型的性能通过它们对$S_{\rm 8}$参数约束的影响以及其组成部分$Ω_{\rm m}$和$σ_{\rm 8}$的偏差来评估。

Result: The results show that for Stage-IV 3$\times$2-pt analyses, PCA models are more effective than simple shift & stretch models. A five-parameter PCA model only degrades the constraint on the $S_{\rm 8}$ parameter by 5 per cent compared to a model with just a shift and a stretch parameter, while reducing the bias in $Ω_{\rm m}$ and $σ_{\rm 8}$ by half. All models can be safely marginalised analytically, with speed-ups of up to a factor of 25 depending on the dimensionality of the model.

结果表明，对于Stage-IV 3$\times$2-pt分析，PCA模型比简单的平移和拉伸模型更有效。一个五参数PCA模型仅使$S_{\rm 8}$参数的约束降低5%，而与只有平移和拉伸参数的模型相比，将$Ω_{\rm m}$和$σ_{\rm 8}$的偏差减少了一半。所有模型都可以安全地进行解析边缘化，根据模型的维度，速度可以提高到25倍。

Conclusion: The study concludes that for Stage-IV 3$\times$2-pt analyses, it is necessary to go beyond simple shift & stretch models for $\boldsymbol{n}(\boldsymbol{z})$ uncertainties. PCA models, even in early surveys, are recommended due to their ability to provide more accurate constraints on cosmological parameters with a manageable increase in computational cost. Analytical marginalisation schemes allow for the efficient inclusion of higher-dimensional $\boldsymbol{n}(\boldsymbol{z})$ uncertainty models in the analysis.

研究得出结论，对于Stage-IV 3$\times$2-pt分析，有必要超越简单的平移和拉伸模型来处理$\boldsymbol{n}(\boldsymbol{z})$不确定性。即使在早期调查中，也建议使用PCA模型，因为它们能够在计算成本可控的情况下提供更精确的宇宙学参数约束。解析边缘化方案允许在分析中高效地包含更高维度的$\boldsymbol{n}(\boldsymbol{z})$不确定性模型。

Abstract: Uncertainties in the radial distribution of galaxies, $\boldsymbol{n}(\boldsymbol{z})$, are one of the major contributions to the error budget of early Stage-IV galaxy survey analyses of weak gravitational lensing, galaxy clustering and galaxy-galaxy lensing (3$\times$2-pt). Based on ensembles of simulated $\boldsymbol{n}(\boldsymbol{z})$ including stochastic and systematic variations, we study the impact of four different $\boldsymbol{n}(\boldsymbol{z})$ uncertainty models: shifts, shifts & stretches, Gaussian processes (GP) and principal component analysis (PCA). Due to the high dimensionality of the latter models, we make use of state-of-the-art gradient-based inference methods as well as approximate analytical marginalisation schemes. Our results show that Stage-IV 3$\times$2-pt analyses must go beyond simple shift & stretch models. In particular, we advocate for the adoption of PCA models even in early Stage-IV surveys. Our results show that considering a five-parameters PCA model only degrades the constraint on the $S_{\rm 8}$ parameter by $5$ per cent with respect to the case when only a shift and a stretch parameter are included, while incurring half the bias in its constituents parameters, $Ω_{\rm m}$ and $σ_{\rm 8}$. We demonstrate that all models considered can be safely marginalised analytically, with speed-ups of up to a factor of 25 depending on the dimensionality of the model. This will allow Stage-IV analyses to safely include higher-dimensional $\boldsymbol{n}(\boldsymbol{z})$ uncertainty models in their analysis at negligible additional computational cost.

### [83] [Nonparametric Variational Inference Reconstruction of the Cosmic Expansion History from SNe Ia -- the \texttt{charm2} code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24630)
*Iason Saganas,Matteo Guardiani,Natalia Porqueres,Torsten Enßlin*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper uses Information Field Theory (IFT) to develop a nonparametric reconstruction algorithm, charm2, for analyzing the redshift evolution of the cosmic energy density from Type Ia supernova data. It finds that while some data sets (Union2.1 and Pantheon+) agree with the flat LCDM model, others (DESY5 and DESY5-Dovekie) suggest an evolving dark energy. However, the evidence lower bound (ELBO) does not conclusively favor either model, and at current noise levels, it prefers the flat LCDM model despite the nonparametric model's better performance with synthetic EDE data.

本文使用信息场理论（IFT）开发了一种非参数重构算法charm2，用于分析Ia型超新星数据中的宇宙能量密度红移演化。发现虽然一些数据集（Union2.1和Pantheon+）与平坦LCDM模型一致，其他数据集（DESY5和DESY5-Dovekie）则暗示了演化暗能量。然而，证据下界（ELBO）并没有明确偏向任一模型，在当前噪声水平下，尽管非参数模型在合成EDE数据中表现更好，但它仍偏好平坦LCDM模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation behind this work is to investigate whether nonparametric reconstructions of the expansion history, which do not assume a specific functional form for the evolution of dark energy, can reveal signal features potentially missed by parametric LCDM models. This is important because recent cosmological analyses using type Ia SNe data have shown a weak preference for evolving dark energy (EDE) models without strongly disfavoring the standard LCDM paradigm.

这项工作的动机是研究不假设暗能量演化特定函数形式的膨胀历史的非参数重构是否可以揭示参数LCDM模型可能遗漏的信号特征。这一点很重要，因为最近使用Ia型超新星数据的宇宙学分析显示，虽然没有强烈反对标准LCDM范式，但对演化暗能量（EDE）模型有轻微偏好。

Method: The authors employ Information Field Theory (IFT), a Bayesian framework, to develop charm2, an advanced version of their previous code, charm1, which is used for nonparametric reconstruction of the cosmic energy density's redshift evolution from Type Ia supernovae (SNe Ia) data. Geometric variational inference is applied to enable accurate Gaussian approximation by finding a coordinate transformation that 'flattens' the posterior. The redshift evolution of the energy density is then analyzed on a double-logarithmic scale, after de-trending, as a stationary Gaussian process.

作者采用信息场理论（IFT），这是一种贝叶斯框架，开发了charm2，这是他们先前代码charm1的高级版本，用于从Ia型超新星（SNe Ia）数据中进行宇宙能量密度红移演化的非参数重构。通过应用几何变分推断找到一个坐标变换来“展平”后验分布，从而实现准确的高斯近似。然后，在去趋势后，将能量密度的红移演化作为平稳高斯过程在双对数尺度上进行分析。

Result: The results show that while the nonparametric reconstructions using Union2.1 and Pantheon+ data sets align with the flat LCDM model, the reconstructions from DESY5 and DESY5-Dovekie data sets indicate deviations and are more compatible with an evolving dark energy signal. However, the evidence lower bound (ELBO) measure does not conclusively favor either the nonparametric or the flat LCDM model across all data sets. Additionally, at current noise levels, the ELBO tends to prefer the flat LCDM model, although the nonparametric model shows better performance in recovering the ground truth in synthetic EDE data, with this trend reversing only at significantly lower noise levels.

结果表明，虽然使用Union2.1和Pantheon+数据集的非参数重构与平坦LCDM模型一致，但来自DESY5和DESY5-Dovekie数据集的重构显示出偏差，更符合演化暗能量信号。然而，证据下界（ELBO）度量并没有在所有数据集中明确偏向于非参数模型或平坦LCDM模型。此外，在当前噪声水平下，ELBO倾向于偏好平坦LCDM模型，尽管非参数模型在合成EDE数据中恢复真实情况方面表现更好，只有在噪声水平显著降低时这种趋势才会逆转。

Conclusion: The nonparametric charm2 reconstructions using the Union2.1 and Pantheon+ data sets are consistent with flat LCDM signal fields. The DESY5 and DESY5-Dovekie reconstructions, however, deviate from flat LCDM comparison fields and suggest an evolving dark energy signal. Despite this, the evidence lower bound (ELBO) measure does not provide conclusive support for a preference of non-flat-LCDM features in any of the data sets. At current noise levels, ELBO favors flat LCDM over the nonparametric model, even though the latter better recovers the ground truth in synthetic EDE data; this trend reverses at approximately 7 times lower noise covariance.

使用Union2.1和Pantheon+数据集的非参数charm2重构与平坦LCDM信号场一致。然而，DESY5和DESY5-Dovekie重构偏离了平坦LCDM比较场，并暗示了演化暗能量信号。尽管如此，证据下界（ELBO）度量并未提供任何数据集中对非平坦LCDM特征偏好的决定性支持。在当前噪声水平下，即使非参数模型在合成EDE数据中更好地恢复了真实情况，ELBO仍然倾向于平坦LCDM；这一趋势仅在噪声协方差降低约7倍时才逆转。

Abstract: Cosmological analyses using the latest set of type Ia SNe data weakly favor an evolving dark energy (EDE) model without strongly disfavoring the standard LCDM paradigm. Nonparametric reconstructions of the expansion history may reveal signal features potentially missed by a parametric LCDM model without laying out a specific functional form for the evolution of dark energy. Information field theory (IFT) is a Bayesian framework for optimal, nonparametric reconstruction algorithms. In this work, we present charm2, the successor to charm1, a previous IFT-based code to reconstruct the cosmic energy density's redshift evolution from SNe Ia. We apply our reconstruction algorithm to the Union2.1, Pantheon+, DESY5 and DESY5-Dovekie data sets to investigate the agreement between the nonparametric reconstruction and the signal suggested by a parametric, flat LCDM model. To enable an accurate Gaussian approximation, we employ geometric variational inference, which finds a coordinate transformation through which a curved posterior gets "flattened". The redshift evolution of the energy density can then be traced on a double-logarithmic scale, which, after de-trending, is well described by a stationary Gaussian process. The nonparametric charm2 reconstructions using the Union2.1 and Pantheon+ data sets are consistent with flat LCDM signal fields. The DESY5 and DESY5-Dovekie reconstructions deviate from flat LCDM comparison fields and are compatible with an evolving dark energy signal. However, using the evidence lower bound (ELBO) measure for model selection, we find no conclusive evidence supporting a preference for non-flat-LCDM features in any of the data sets. We note that at current DESY5 noise levels, the ELBO tends to favor flat LCDM over our nonparametric model although the latter better recovers the ground truth in synthetic EDE data; a trend reversing only at ~7x lower noise covariance.
