### [84] [Measurement of the Weyl Potential Evolution and $E_G$ Statistic from KiDS-1000, BOSS and 2dFLenS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24631)
*Xuwei Zhang,Ming Zhang,Yunliang Ren,Xiaofeng Yang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The study applies a model-independent approach to measure the Weyl potential and $E_G$ using KiDS-1000 weak lensing and BOSS/2dFLenS galaxy clustering data. Without CMB priors, results are consistent with late-time constraints. With Planck18 priors, the high redshift bin shows a weaker Weyl potential and lower $E_G$, indicating a mild deviation from $\Lambda$CDM. The deviation is linked to the high redshift CMASS sample, suggesting a connection to the 'Lensing is low' problem.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to test the consistency of the $\Lambda$CDM model by measuring the Weyl potential and $E_G$ using a model-independent approach. Previous studies have shown some tensions with $\Lambda$CDM in DES Y3 data, and this work aims to extend the analysis to KiDS-1000 and BOSS/2dFLenS data, providing further insights into possible deviations from General Relativity and the $\Lambda$CDM cosmology.

动机是通过使用模型无关的方法测量Weyl势和$E_G$来测试$\Lambda$CDM模型的一致性。之前的研究在DES Y3数据中显示了与$\Lambda$CDM的一些张力，而这项工作旨在将分析扩展到KiDS-1000和BOSS/2dFLenS数据，为进一步了解可能偏离广义相对论和$\Lambda$CDM宇宙学提供见解。

Method: The method involves applying a recently developed model-independent framework to measure the Weyl potential and $E_G$ using KiDS-1000 weak lensing and BOSS/2dFLenS galaxy clustering data. The analysis is performed in two redshift bins without external CMB priors and then with Planck18 priors. The KiDS Cosmology Analysis Pipeline (KCAP) is used for the analysis.

该方法涉及应用最近开发的模型无关框架，利用KiDS-1000弱引力透镜和BOSS/2dFLenS星系团聚数据来测量Weyl势和$E_G$。分析在两个红移区间内进行，首先不使用外部CMB先验，然后使用Planck18先验。分析过程中使用了KiDS宇宙学分析管道（KCAP）。

Result: Without external CMB priors, the Weyl potential and $E_G$ measurements are consistent with late-time constraints. When Planck18 priors are imposed, the low redshift bin remains compatible with General Relativity, while the high redshift bin shows a weaker Weyl potential and lower $E_G$, corresponding to a mild $1.52\sigma$ deviation from the $\Lambda$CDM cosmology. Phenomenological modified gravity models show a mild preference for a suppressed high redshift Weyl potential, but late time data alone remain consistent with $\Lambda$CDM. The deviation is primarily driven by the specific high redshift CMASS sample, reflecting the well-known 'Lensing is low' problem.

在没有外部CMB先验的情况下，Weyl势和$E_G$的测量结果与晚期约束一致。当施加Planck18先验时，低红移区间仍与广义相对论一致，而高红移区间显示出较弱的Weyl势和较低的$E_G$，对应于与$\Lambda$CDM宇宙学的轻微$1.52\sigma$偏差。现象学修正引力模型对高红移Weyl势的抑制表现出轻微偏好，但仅晚期数据仍与$\Lambda$CDM一致。这种偏差主要是由特定的高红移CMASS样本驱动的，反映了众所周知的“引力透镜偏低”问题。

Conclusion: The study finds that the Weyl potential and $E_G$ measurements are generally consistent with the $\Lambda$CDM model, especially in the low redshift bin. However, a mild deviation is observed in the high redshift bin, which is mainly attributed to the high redshift CMASS sample. This deviation is consistent with the 'Lensing is low' problem, suggesting that further investigation is needed to understand the underlying physics.

研究发现，Weyl势和$E_G$的测量结果总体上与$\Lambda$CDM模型一致，特别是在低红移区间。然而，在高红移区间观察到了轻微的偏差，这主要归因于高红移CMASS样本。这种偏差与“引力透镜偏低”问题一致，表明需要进一步研究以理解其背后的物理机制。

Abstract: A recently developed model-independent approach to measuring the Weyl potential has shown some tensions with $Λ$CDM (Lambda Cold Dark Matter) in DES (Dark Energy Survey) Y3 data. We apply this framework to Kilo-Degree Survey (KiDS-1000) weak lensing and BOSS/2dFLenS galaxy clustering using the KiDS Cosmology Analysis Pipeline (KCAP) in two redshift bins. Without external CMB priors, both the Weyl potential and $E_G$ measurements are consistent with late time constraints. After imposing Planck18 priors, the low redshift bin remains compatible with General Relativity, whereas the high redshift bin shows a weaker Weyl potential and lower $E_G$, corresponding to a mild $1.52σ$ deviation from the $Λ$CDM cosmology. Furthermore, phenomenological modified gravity models show a mild preference for a suppressed high redshift Weyl potential, but late time data alone remain consistent with $Λ$CDM. Our results also suggest that this deviation is primarily driven by the specific high redshift CMASS sample, reflecting the well-known ``Lensing is low'' problem.

### [85] [\texttt{SWIM}: Stochastic Warm Inflation Module to generate and analyse Warm Inflationary power spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24654)
*Umang Kumar,Suratna Das*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper introduces SWIM, a tool for generating and analyzing the scalar power spectrum in Warm Inflation models. It integrates with Cobaya for parameter estimation and uses machine learning to speed up MCMC analysis, providing a complete numerical platform for model testing against current CMB data.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to provide a comprehensive numerical tool (SWIM) that can generate the scalar power spectrum for Warm Inflation models, either semi-analytically or fully numerically, and integrate with existing MCMC codes like Cobaya to constrain model parameters using current CMB data. The necessity arises from the fact that traditional semi-analytical methods may not always be sufficient for accurate parameter estimation.

动机是提供一个全面的数值工具（SWIM），该工具可以为温热暴涨模型生成标量功率谱，无论是半解析地还是完全数值地，并与现有的MCMC代码（如Cobaya）集成，以使用当前的CMB数据来约束模型参数。传统半解析方法可能并不总是足以进行准确的参数估计。

Method: The method involves developing a software module, SWIM, written in C++ and Python. This module numerically solves the standard stochastic perturbation equations of Warm Inflation without approximations, generates the scalar power spectrum, and integrates with Cobaya for MCMC analysis. Machine learning techniques are employed to speed up the MCMC process, especially when dealing with fully numerical power spectra, which significantly reduces computational costs.

该方法涉及开发一个用C++和Python编写的软件模块SWIM。该模块在不进行任何近似的情况下数值求解温热暴涨的标准随机扰动方程，生成标量功率谱，并与Cobaya集成进行MCMC分析。机器学习技术被用来加速MCMC过程，特别是在处理完全数值的功率谱时，这大大降低了计算成本。

Result: The results show that SWIM outperforms other numerical codes designed for semi-analytical power spectrum generation in terms of runtime. Additionally, SWIM is capable of handling situations where semi-analytical methods fall short, making it the only available code for full numerical power spectrum analysis and parameter estimation with observational data.

结果显示，在运行时间方面，SWIM优于其他设计用于半解析功率谱生成的数值代码。此外，SWIM能够处理半解析方法不足的情况，使其成为唯一可用于完全数值功率谱分析和利用观测数据进行参数估计的代码。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that SWIM offers a complete and efficient numerical platform for the thorough analysis of Warm Inflation models against current cosmological data. It is the only publicly available code that can handle both semi-analytical and fully numerical power spectra, and it is integrated with MCMC tools for robust parameter estimation.

结论是SWIM提供了一个完整且高效的数值平台，可以针对当前的宇宙学数据对温热暴涨模型进行全面分析。它是唯一公开可用的代码，可以处理半解析和完全数值的功率谱，并与MCMC工具集成以进行稳健的参数估计。

Abstract: Numerical analysis to determine the form of the scalar power spectrum in Warm Inflationary paradigm is inevitable. One further needs numerical techniques to analyse any Warm Inflation model with the current observational data through the MCMC codes that are available publicly, like COSMOMC or Cobaya. We present \texttt{SWIM} (Stochastic Warm Inflation Module) written in C++ and Python, that not only helps generate the Warm Inflationary scalar power spectrum, either semi-analytically or fully numerically, but also is integrated with Cobaya enabling the user to constrain the model parameters with current CMB data and thus to put any Warm Inflation model to test. \texttt{SWIM} numerically solves the standard stochastic perturbation equations of Warm Inflation without any approximations, uses machine learning techniques to speed up the MCMC analysis while analysing the fully numerical power spectrum that significantly reduces the computational cost, and is able to accommodate any Warm Inflation model with any form of inflationary potential and dissipative coefficient for numerical analysis. We show that \texttt{SWIM}, in most of the cases, outperforms other numerical codes on Warm Inflation that are designed to yield only the semi-analytical power spectrum as far as the runtimes are concerned. We further point out that there can be situations where the semi-analytical way of determining the scalar power spectrum in Warm Inflation can fall short, and one needs the full numerical power spectrum for parameter estimation given the observational data. In such cases, \texttt{SWIM} is the only code available so far that is designed to perform the task. Hence, \texttt{SWIM} offers a complete numerical platform for thorough analysis of Warm Inflation models against the current cosmological data. \texttt{SWIM} has been made publicly available at https://github.com/umg-kmr/SWIM.

</details>


### [86] [Cosmological Impact of Redshift-Dependent Type Ia Supernovae Calibration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24761)
*Seyed Hamidreza Mirpoorian,Meng-Xiang Lin,Levon Pogosian*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper investigates the impact of a redshift-dependent correction to SNIa magnitudes on cosmological parameters. No evidence for such an effect is found in $\Lambda$CDM, but it can help reduce the Hubble tension when combined with dynamical dark energy models.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore the possibility of unaccounted redshift-dependent calibration systematics or new physics that could affect SNIa magnitude measurements and their implications on cosmological tensions, particularly the Hubble tension.

动机是探索未被考虑的红移依赖的校准系统误差或新物理，这些因素可能影响Ia型超新星的亮度测量及其对宇宙学张力（特别是哈勃张力）的影响。

Method: The authors parameterize a phenomenological correction to SNIa magnitudes that scales with cosmic look-back time. They use a combination of CMB, BAO, and SNIa data to constrain this free amplitude, considering both $\Lambda$CDM and dynamical dark energy models.

作者参数化了一个与宇宙回溯时间成比例的Ia型超新星亮度的现象学修正。他们使用CMB、BAO和Ia型超新星的数据来约束这个自由振幅，并考虑了$\Lambda$CDM模型和动态暗能量模型。

Result: No significant evidence for a redshift-dependent calibration effect is found in $\Lambda$CDM, and its inclusion has a negligible impact on cosmological parameters. However, when combined with a prior on the SNIa absolute magnitude from SH0ES, a nonzero calibration parameter is weakly preferred. In dynamical dark energy models, the preference for a nonzero calibration parameter increases, reducing the Hubble tension to 1.5$\sigma$.

在$\Lambda$CDM模型中，没有发现显著的红移依赖的校准效应，其包含对宇宙学参数的影响可以忽略不计。然而，当结合SH0ES给出的Ia型超新星绝对星等的先验时，非零校准参数被弱偏好。在动态暗能量模型中，对非零校准参数的偏好增加，将哈勃张力降低到1.5$\sigma$。

Conclusion: Redshift-dependent SNIa calibration effects, as parameterized in this study, are not supported by current data within $\Lambda$CDM. However, they can play a role in reconciling cosmological datasets when combined with extensions to the late-time expansion history, such as dynamical dark energy models.

在$\Lambda$CDM模型中，当前数据并不支持本文参数化的红移依赖的Ia型超新星校准效应。然而，当与晚期宇宙膨胀历史的扩展（如动态暗能量模型）结合时，它们可以在协调宇宙学数据集方面发挥作用。

Abstract: Type Ia supernovae (SNIa) play a central role in constraining the late-time expansion history of the Universe and are directly implicated in current cosmological tensions. Motivated by the possibility of unaccounted redshift-dependent calibration systematics or new physics, we investigate the impact of a phenomenological correction to SNIa magnitudes that scales with cosmic look-back time. We parameterize this effect with a free amplitude and constrain it using a combination of cosmic microwave background, baryon acoustic oscillation, and SNIa data, considering both $Λ$CDM and dynamical dark energy models. Importantly, our parameterization is not intended to serve as a proxy for SNIa progenitor age, as current observations show no significant difference in standardized SNIa brightness between young and old progenitor populations at low redshift. We find no evidence for a redshift-dependent calibration effect when fitting uncalibrated SNIa data, and its inclusion has a negligible impact on cosmological parameters within $Λ$CDM, nor does it qualitatively change the inferred dynamics of evolving dark energy. When incorporating a prior on the SNIa absolute magnitude from SH0ES, a nonzero calibration parameter is weakly preferred within $Λ$CDM. Interestingly, with dynamical dark energy, the preference of a nonzero calibration parameter increases to $4.3σ$, and it can accommodate both the distance ladder and early-Universe constraints, reducing the Hubble tension to $1.5σ$, with the best-fit model effectively corresponding to a constant equation of state with $w < -1$. Overall, our results indicate that redshift-dependent SNIa calibration effects, as parameterized here, are not supported by current data within $Λ$CDM, but can play a role in reconciling cosmological datasets when combined with extensions to the late-time expansion history.

</details>
